### [1] [IdiomX A Multilingual Benchmark for Idiom Understanding, Retrieval, and Interpretation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02584)
*Ayman Ali Sharara*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了 IdiomX，这是一个包含 12000 多个习语、覆盖英阿法三种语言的的大规模多语言习语基准数据集，旨在通过四个核心任务推进习语检测、检索与语义解释的研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的习语资源规模有限、缺乏语境多样性及多语言覆盖，难以满足现代语言模型的需求，且习语的非组合性、上下文依赖性和跨语言对齐难度大，持续挑战自然语言处理技术。

Method: 提出了一种多阶段构建流水线，结合词汇资源提取、大规模标准化、大语言模型（LLM）增强以及结构化验证；构建了包含超过 19 万个上下文语境示例的资源，并定义了涵盖习语检测、检索及解释的四项任务基准。

Result: 实验表明，上下文 Transformer 模型显著提升了习语检测能力，混合检索与重排序架构加强了单语言及跨语言检索效果，且习语解释任务可有效建模为语义检索问题。

Conclusion: IdiomX 为研究习语提供了从检测到检索及语义解释的标准化基准，该框架具有高度的可扩展性，为未来跨语言隐喻推理研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Idiomatic expressions remain a persistent challenge for natural language processing because their meanings are often non-compositional, context-dependent, and difficult to align across languages. Existing idiom resources are often limited in scale, contextual diversity, or multilingual coverage, restricting their utility for modern language models. We introduce IdiomX, a large-scale multilingual benchmark for idiom understanding, retrieval, and interpretation, constructed through a reproducible multi-stage pipeline combining lexical resource extraction, large-scale normalization, controlled large language model enrichment, and structured validation. The resulting dataset contains over 190K contextualized examples spanning 12K+ idioms, with aligned English, Arabic, and French semantic representations, idiomatic and literal usage labels, and rich linguistic metadata. Building on this resource, we define a unified four-task benchmark covering idiom detection, context-to-idiom retrieval, Arabic-to-English idiom retrieval, and idiom interpretation, extending evaluation from figurative recognition to semantic grounding and explainable meaning retrieval. Experiments show that contextual transformer models substantially improve idiom detection, while hybrid retrieval and reranking architectures significantly strengthen both monolingual and cross-lingual idiom retrieval. Results further demonstrate that idiom interpretation can be effectively modeled as a semantic retrieval task, introducing interpretability as a complementary benchmark dimension. Overall, IdiomX provides a scalable benchmark for studying idiomatic language as a progression from detection to retrieval and semantic interpretation, and offers a modular framework extensible to additional languages and figurative reasoning tasks

</details>


### [2] [Greener Than Humans? Environmental Attitudes in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02741)
*Stefanie Kunkel,Tilman Hartwig,Marcus Voss,Emma K. Schütt,Angelika Gellrich*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究评估了31种大模型在环境议题上的态度倾向，发现模型普遍表现出比人类更“环保”的倾向，但其立场极易受用户引导影响，缺乏规范性稳定性，呼吁加强AI在可持续决策应用中的伦理治理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型语言模型（LLM）正越来越多地应用于可持续发展决策与传播，但目前尚缺乏对其输出中隐含的环境态度进行系统性评估的证据。因此，研究旨在量化并理解LLM在环境议题上的价值取向及其可靠性。

Method: 研究者构建了一套基准测试框架，通过环境认知、情感和行为建议三个维度评估了31种主流模型。研究方法包括对比模型间的响应差异、将模型输出与德国人类环境意识调查数据进行基准比对，以及通过人格设定和特定偏好提示词（Sycophancy）测试模型的鲁棒性与受操纵程度。

Result: 大多数LLM在环境认知、情感和行为建议上比平均人类受访者更偏向“进步”；模型在可持续相关回应的表现与模型规模、开发来源或发布背景之间无显著关联；但模型对提示词极度敏感，表现出明显的顺从性（sycophancy），即会根据用户设定的意识形态立场改变回应倾向。

Conclusion: LLM在可持续发展议题上展现出较强的“亲环境”偏向，但其表现容易受提示词（尤其是人格设定）的影响而发生动摇。研究强调，鉴于AI在可持续决策中的应用日益广泛，必须加强对其价值对齐、治理透明度和规范性可靠性的监管与审查。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used in sustainability-related decision support, reporting, and public communication, yet little systematic evidence exists on the environmental attitudes embedded in their outputs. This paper develops a benchmark for evaluating environmental cognition, affect, and behavioural recommendations in LLMs and applies it to 31 widely used proprietary and open-weight models. Drawing on questions from established environmental awareness surveys and additional sustainability-related behavioural measures, we compare LLM responses 1) among models and 2) between models and human survey benchmarks from Germany. We assess their robustness across prompting conditions. We find that many LLMs align more closely with environmentally progressive attitudes than the average survey respondent, exhibiting higher levels of environmental affect and cognition and recommending behaviours associated with substantial potential CO2 reductions. At the same time, we observe no systematic relationship between sustainability-oriented responses and model origin, size, or release context. However, models exhibit contextual sensitivity, controlled by persona-based prompting and show sycophantic shifts mirroring user-specified ideological positions, which raises concerns about steerability and normative reliability in real-world deployments. Our findings provide a reusable evaluation framework for assessing sustainability-related value alignment in LLMs and highlight the importance of governance, transparency, and critical oversight as AI systems become increasingly embedded in sustainability transformations and public decision-making.

</details>


### [3] [On the Persistent Effects of Lexicality in Large Language Mod](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02750)
*Hammad Rizwan,Muhammad Umair Haider,Nishant Subramani,Mona T. Diab,A. B. Siddique,Hassan Sajjad*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文量化了大型语言模型表征中词汇重叠对语义理解的干扰，发现词汇偏见在各层级和架构中广泛存在，并在中间层表现出性能谷值，直接影响模型在下游任务中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对大型语言模型（LLM）中词汇重叠与语义内容之间的相互影响及其对下游任务的制约关系缺乏深入理解，作者旨在量化并探究这种词汇偏见的影响机制。

Method: 研究者通过设计一系列对抗性语义压力测试（adversarial semantic stress tests），并结合信息论视角，量化了词汇重叠与语义内容对表征的影响，并对不同模型架构、训练机制及目标函数的表现进行了对比分析。

Result: 研究发现：1. 词汇影响贯穿模型全深度，且在不同架构和训练目标下表现一致；2. 模型存在一个“中间深度区域”，在此区域内词汇和语义信号同时衰减，表现出严重的性能退化；3. 词汇偏见会显著负面影响总结任务和模型编辑等下游应用。

Conclusion: 大型语言模型的表征深受词汇重叠影响，而非仅仅关注语义内容。这种词汇偏见在模型深层结构中持续存在，并会直接干扰摘要生成和模型编辑等下游任务的性能，揭示了当前LLM在理解语义时的局限性。

Abstract: Representations extracted from large language models (LLMs) play an important role in many downstream applications. However, the structure of these representations is often influenced by lexical overlap rather than semantic content. Our understanding of the relationship between this lexical influence and semantic content, and its implications for downstream tasks, remains limited. In this work, we investigate representations to quantify the effect of lexical overlap relative to semantic content. We consider several adversarial semantic stress tests and further connect our findings to the information theory perspective. We find that lexical influence extends across the depth of models, consistently across architectures, training regimes, and objective functions, including the models trained for semantic similarity. Moreover, we observe a mid-depth region in which both lexical and semantic signals degrade simultaneously, indicating a transitional regime where representations are poor for both surface form and meaning. We further demonstrate the effect of lexical influence on downstream uses of LLMs using summarization and model editing as a case study.

</details>


### [4] [Topics as Proxies for Sociodemographics: How Conversational Context Affects LLM Answers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02776)
*Vera Neplenbroek,Gabriele Sarti,Arianna Bisazza,Raquel Fernández*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出，在大语言模型的高风险建议应用中，用户人口统计学特征并非导致输出差异的主要原因，对话话题才是影响模型表现的核心因素。这一发现挑战了既有关于社会人口统计学偏见的认知，强调了理解对话上下文对确保模型安全应用的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究普遍认为大语言模型在医疗、法律等高风险领域存在针对不同社会人口统计学群体的输出偏见。本研究旨在深入探讨这些偏见的真实驱动因素，验证模型是否确实能根据对话历史推断出人口统计学信息，并识别导致结果差异的核心变量。

Method: 研究者通过定量分析，对比了用户人口统计学特征与多种（心理）语言学特征（如对话话题、情绪、可读性）对大语言模型输出的影响。研究采用了预测性分析方法，评估了不同特征对模型建议的预测能力，以确定差异的主要驱动力。

Result: 研究发现：1. 大语言模型在仅通过单次对话历史推断用户人口统计学特征方面表现欠佳；2. 不同群体间的结果差异在量级上非常小；3. 对话话题（而非人口统计学特征）是预测模型输出差异的最强因素，且这些话题往往会以不可预测的方式影响建议质量。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在处理高风险建议时，其输出差异的主要驱动因素并非用户的人口统计学特征，而是对话内容（特别是话题）。这揭示了对话上下文对模型行为的深远影响，研究者强调未来需要深入研究并缓解这种上下文偏差，以确保模型输出的公平性与稳定性。

Abstract: When large language models (LLMs) are used in high-stakes scenarios, such as legal, medical and financial advice, even a single conversation history is enough to drive differences in outcomes between users. Prior work has demonstrated that this results in outcome disparities between sociodemographic groups, with some groups receiving more advantageous outcomes than others. In this work, we demonstrate that LLMs actually struggle to infer user sociodemographics from a single conversation history and that although there are disparities between sociodemographic groups, they are minimal in magnitude. To investigate what the main driver of these disparities is, we compare user sociodemographics to a range of (psycho)linguistic features of conversations, including conversation topic, emotions, and readability. We find that conversation topics are most predictive of LLM-generated advice within a conversational context, which, to some extent, function as proxies for sociodemographic groups and often affect advice in unpredictable ways. This is cause for concern and highlights the need for future research to better understand and, if needed, mitigate the effect of conversational context on LLM outputs in high-stakes scenarios.

</details>


### [5] [Do Value Vectors in Deep Layers Need Context from the Residual Stream?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02780)
*Muyu He,Yuchen Liu,Qingya Huang,Li Zhang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种名为Bank of Values (BoV)的创新机制，通过用存储的查表式“上下文无关价值向量”替换Transformer深层中的传统注意力计算，在降低计算资源消耗的同时提升了大型语言模型的综合性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究者发现Transformer深层网络在处理价值向量时，对残差流的依赖存在冗余。模型无需始终通过复杂上下文计算价值向量，直接使用上下文无关的预存值即可保留有效的令牌信息，以此降低计算复杂度。

Method: 作者提出了“Bank of Values (BoV)”方法，通过在模型后三分之一层使用可学习的查表（Lookup Table）来存储上下文无关的令牌特定价值向量，从而替代了传统的、依赖残差流计算的价值向量生成方式。

Result: 在135M和780M参数规模的模型实验中，BoV方法降低了验证集损失，并在21个基准测试任务的平均得分上达到了最优性能，同时显著减少了计算和缓存资源的占用。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了在LLM深层网络中使用“上下文无关”的价值向量（Value Vectors）是有效的。通过引入Bank of Values (BoV)方法，模型能够减少计算与内存开销，同时维持甚至提升模型性能，揭示了深度模型层级在信息处理上的冗余性。

Abstract: The success of the transformer architecture as the backbone of modern LLMs is in large part due to its use of attention layers. An attention layer follows the standard neural network paradigm: it takes the residual stream as input and thereby produces context-dependent query, key, and value vectors. However, we find that model performance meaningfully improves when deeper layers learn only a context-free value vector to preserve the original token information, without drawing on any context from the residual stream. When the model has access to this context-free value vector, adding back the context-dependent component provides little additional benefit for aggregate benchmark performance. Such context-free value vectors can be stored as sparse model parameters, eliminating the need to recompute or persistently cache these values. Through systematic ablations on the key design choices for such context-free value vectors, we propose Bank of Values (BoV), a new way of computing value vectors in attention by learning a lookup table of token-specific value vectors for each of the last third of layers. Across 135M and 780M models, BoV improves validation loss over standard attention and, at 780M, the average score across 21 benchmarks, matching the previous best method that adds token information to the value vector with less compute and memory.

</details>


### [6] [Translating Classical Poetry into Modern Prose](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02806)
*Chalamalasetti Kranti,Sowmya Vajjala*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文推出了Padyam2Gadyam数据集，涵盖600首泰卢固语古典诗歌的散文翻译，并评估了主流大语言模型在古典诗歌转散文任务上的表现，结果发现模型性能尚有不足，且现有评估指标难以衡量文学翻译的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决古典诗歌（泰卢固语）向现代散文翻译语料缺失的问题，并评估现有大语言模型处理此类高度复杂、具文化特性的文学翻译任务的能力。

Method: 研究构建了包含600首13至17世纪泰卢固语古典诗歌及其人工校对后的现代泰卢固语和英语散文翻译数据集（Padyam2Gadyam），并基于此评估了5种主流大语言模型在诗歌转散文任务中的表现，同时结合定性分析探讨了当前翻译评估方法的局限。

Result: 实验显示，不同的大语言模型在泰卢固语和英语的翻译性能上存在显著差异，但整体表现均未达到理想水平，翻译质量仍有巨大提升空间；同时指出通用机器翻译评估指标在处理古典文学翻译时存在明显短板。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，虽然大语言模型在古典诗歌转散文任务中展现了一定能力，但仍存在显著局限，且现有的机器翻译评估指标难以充分捕捉古典文学翻译的复杂性和艺术性。未来需要更针对性的评估标准和模型优化方法来提升翻译质量。

Abstract: We introduce Padyam2Gadyam, a dataset for the task of poem-to-prose translation from 13th-17th Century Telugu Classical Poetry to contemporary Telugu and English prose. The dataset consists of 600 poems and their human-verified Telugu and English prose translations. We evaluated 5 contemporary Large Language Models (LLMs) on their ability to do poem-to-prose translation into Telugu and English. Our results indicate that while there are differences across LLMs, their overall performance leave a large room for improvement in both languages. Through qualitative analysis, we discuss the the capabilities and limitations of contemporary MT evaluation approaches for this task.

</details>


### [7] [Fixing FOLIO and MALLS: Verified Annotations and an LLM-assisted Framework to Focus Human Relabeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02837)
*Andrea Brunello,Cristian Curaba,Luca Geatti,Michele Mignani,Angelo Montanari,Nicola Saccomanno*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了主流NL-to-FOL数据集存在约三分之一的标注错误，导致现有LLM性能评估出现显著偏差；作者通过修正数据并提出一种高效的AI辅助审核框架，显著提升了基准测试的准确性和人工校验效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前神经符号AI和自然语言推理（NLI）领域高度依赖NL-to-FOL数据集，但这些数据集从未经过严格质量审查，潜在的标注错误可能严重影响模型的评估效果与研究结论。

Method: 1. 针对FOLIO和MALLS数据集进行系统性的人工审计与错误识别；2. 构建并发布修正后的基准数据；3. 提出一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的辅助人工审核框架，通过识别高错误风险实例，优化人工校验流程。

Result: 1. 发现FOLIO和MALLS数据集分别存在约39%和36%的逻辑形式化错误；2. 使用修正后的数据集进行评估，SOTA大模型的准确率提升了9至22个百分点；3. 新提出的辅助框架实现了在审核少于24%实例的情况下达到90%的整体数据集准确率。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，现有的自然语言到一阶逻辑（NL-to-FOL）基准数据集存在严重的标注质量问题，这误导了当前大语言模型的性能评估。通过修正后的数据集及辅助审核框架，研究不仅提升了评估的准确性，还极大地提高了人工校验的效率。

Abstract: Accurate translation from Natural Language to First-Order Logic (NL-to-FOL) underpins neurosymbolic AI systems and Natural Language Inference (NLI), making the quality of NL-to-FOL benchmarks essential -- yet these datasets have never been rigorously audited. Our first contribution is to present a systematic human inspection of the validation split of \textsf{FOLIO} and a subset of \textsf{MALLS} test instances, finding that approximately 39% and 36% of entries, respectively, contain incorrect FOL formalizations (i.e., ground truth labels), with additional rates of ambiguous NL sentences (16.4% and 48%) and incorrect NLI labels in \textsf{FOLIO} (8.4%). Our second contribution is to develop and release corrected ground truths for such datasets, showing that annotation errors distort model evaluation on a reference benchmark task: testing three state-of-the-art LLMs (Gemma~4 31B-it, Qwen3-30B-A3B, and GPT-4o-mini) with the corrected ground truths yields accuracy gains from +9 to +22 percentage points. Motivated by these findings, we propose an LLM-based framework to support humans in manual reviewing NL-to-FOL datasets. By directing reviewers toward the most error-prone instances, we empirically show that it is possible to achieve 90% dataset accuracy after reviewing fewer than 24% of instances, compared to over 70% required by unguided review. We release all human-verified annotations and the code for our framework.

</details>


### [8] [Economy of Minds: Emerging Multi-Agent Intelligence with Economic Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02859)
*Zhenting Qi,Huangyuan Su,Ao Qu,Chenyu Wang,Yu Yao,Han Zheng,Kushal Chattopadhyay,Guowei Xu,Zihan Wang,Weirui Ye,Vijay Janapa Reddi,Ju Li,Paul Pu Liang,Himabindu Lakkaraju,Sham Kakade,Yilun Du*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 受哈耶克经济理论启发，该研究提出了一种通过拍卖、交易和财富积累等经济激励驱动智能体协作的框架。无需中心化调度，该模型通过群体内的“经济选择”（优胜劣汰），让智能体自发涌现出多步推理能力，并在多个复杂任务中展现出卓越的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多智能体协同大多依赖中心化控制或显式通信协议，但在复杂、动态的环境下难以扩展。本研究旨在探索如何在没有全局干预的情况下，通过模仿市场经济的去中心化协作机制，实现智能体群体自发地演化出更强的集体智能。

Method: 研究引入了一种基于哈耶克经济理论的代理人经济框架。核心机制包括：1. 拍卖机制：智能体竞拍行动权；2. 支付与财富积累：通过环境奖励获取财富，以此作为去中心化的信用分配信号；3. 经济选择机制：通过“富者生存”（变异/复制）与“弱者破产”（探索/替换）的动态过程实现群体演化，无需全局协调或显式通信协议。

Result: 在数学推理、金融/科学研究、加速器设计及分布式系统优化等五个复杂智能任务中，该经济模型均表现优异。即便初始智能体较弱，通过经济演化过程，系统仍能涌现出多步推理策略，且整体性能超越了更强的单一模型基线（monolithic baselines）。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了无需中心化控制，仅通过设计去中心化的经济激励结构，即可让智能体群体自组织并涌现出超越单一强模型的高级协同推理能力。这为构建多智能体系统提供了一种全新的范式：从“工程化协调”转向“设计激励结构”。

Abstract: How can a population of agents self-orchestrate and self-adapt into stronger collective intelligence without centralized control? Inspired by Friedrich Hayek's economic theory of decentralized coordination in markets, we study this question through an agent economy in which agents compete via auctions for the right to act, exchange payments, and accumulate wealth from environmental rewards. These simple economic signals induce decentralized credit assignment, driving planning without global orchestration or explicit communication protocols. The population evolves through economic selection: effective agents accumulate wealth and are mutated via exploitation, while ineffective ones go bankrupt and are replaced via exploration. We show that, initialized with weak agents, the economy produces emergent multi-step reasoning strategies and outperforms stronger monolithic baselines across five agentic tasks, including mathematical reasoning, financial research, scientific research, accelerator design, and distributed-system optimization. We further provide theoretical insights into how economic dynamics shape agent behaviors, linking local incentives to long-term global performance. Our results suggest a new path to multi-agent intelligence: rather than engineering coordination, we can design decentralized incentive structures under which it automatically emerges.

</details>


### [9] [Adaptive Latent Agentic Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02871)
*Dongwon Jung,Peng Shi,Yi Zhang,Junshan Zhang,Muhao Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出 ALAR 框架，通过让 LLM 代理在常规步骤执行紧凑的“潜在推理”，仅在关键困难决策时使用“显式思维链”，在显著提升推理效率（大幅减少 Token 消耗）的同时，保持了高质量的任务执行能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LLM 代理在每个决策步骤中均生成冗长的思维链，导致多轮任务轨迹中计算资源的严重浪费和推理效率低下。因此，需要一种能够动态分配推理努力、避免过度冗余的推理机制。

Method: 提出了一种名为“自适应潜在代理推理”（ALAR）的双模式框架。该框架利用代理的动作作为监督锚点来学习潜在推理，并引入选择性机制：在常规步骤中使用简洁的潜在推理，仅在评估认为需要深度审议时切换到显式思维链（CoT）。

Result: 在代理搜索和工具使用基准测试中，ALAR 表现优异：在搜索任务中减少了高达 43.6% 的生成 Token，在工具使用任务中减少了高达 84.6% 的生成 Token，同时保持或提升了任务准确率。

Conclusion: ALAR 证明了通过在常规决策中使用紧凑的潜在推理，并在困难步骤中按需升级为显式思维链（CoT），可以有效打破 LLM 代理在准确性和效率之间的权衡。该方法在大幅降低推理成本的同时，成功保持甚至提升了任务执行的准确性。

Abstract: Large reasoning models improve performance by generating extended chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning, but this behavior becomes inefficient when applied to LLM agents. Current LLM agents often generate verbose textual reasoning at every decision step and allocate reasoning effort nearly uniformly across turns, leading to substantial inefficiency in multi-turn agentic trajectories. We propose Adaptive Latent Agentic Reasoning (ALAR), a dual-mode framework that uses compact latent reasoning for routine turns and selectively escalates to explicit chain-of-thought when deeper deliberation is needed. ALAR learns latent reasoning by using the agent's actions as supervision anchors and is further optimized to use latent reasoning when it is sufficient for task success and reserve explicit CoT for harder decisions. Experiments on agentic search and tool-use benchmarks show that ALAR maintains comparable or better task accuracy while substantially reducing generated tokens by up to 43.6% in search and 84.6% in tool use. These results demonstrate that ALAR improves the accuracy-efficiency trade-off of LLM agents by reducing unnecessary textual reasoning while preserving explicit deliberation for harder decision steps.

### [10] [Linear Probes Detect Task Format, Not Reasoning Mode in Language Model Hidden States](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02907)
*Subramanyam Sahoo,Vinija Jain,Aman Chadha,Divya Chaudhary*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了利用线性探针区分 LLM 推理类型的常见做法存在严重偏差：看似“独特”的推理表征，实际上主要由任务的格式特征驱动，而非真正的推理机制。研究强调在机械可解释性研究中必须进行格式去混淆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 目前主流研究常通过对大语言模型（LLM）隐藏状态进行线性探测（linear probing）来论证模型针对不同推理类型学习到了独特的内部表征。本研究旨在验证这种高准确率的探测结果究竟是真实捕捉到了推理机制，还是仅仅捕捉到了任务格式带来的混淆变量。

Method: 研究人员以 Qwen3-14B 模型为对象，在 LogiQA 2.0（演绎）、ARC-Challenge（归纳）和 αNLI（溯因）三个代表不同推理类型的基准测试中进行线性探测实验。通过分析模型第 32 层隐藏状态的几何特征，并采用残差化处理（剔除任务来源、选项数量和响应长度等格式混淆因素），对比不同任务间的轨迹相似性，并利用因果干预（causal steering）验证推理模式与几何结构之间的函数联系。

Result: 尽管实验初期在探测中达到了 100% 的准确率且几何分布清晰，但在剔除任务来源、选项数量和响应长度等格式混淆项后，探测准确率降至随机水平。轨迹相似性分析显示不同推理任务间存在大量重叠，且因果干预实验表明模型几何结构与推理模式之间不存在显著的函数关联。

Conclusion: 高探针准确率往往反映的是任务格式（如选项数量、长度等）的特征，而非模型内部真实的推理模式。因此，在机械可解释性研究中，进行“格式去混淆”（format deconfounding）是至关重要的，否则会导致对模型推理机制的错误解释。

Abstract: Linear probing of large language model (LLM) hidden states is widely used to claim that models learn distinct representations for different reasoning types. We test this by probing Qwen3-14B on three benchmarks spanning the classical trichotomy: LogiQA 2.0 (deductive), ARC-Challenge (inductive), and $α$NLI (abductive). At layer 32 of 40, linear probes achieve 100\% cross-validated accuracy with well-separated geometry (intrinsic dimensionalities: 20.6, 28.5, 33.6; convex hull contamination $\leq$1.5\%). However, this separation is entirely driven by format confounds. Residualizing source identity, option count, and response length reduces accuracy to chance. Trace-anchor similarity indicates largely shared reasoning across tasks (42.5\% agreement vs.\ 33.3\% chance), and causal steering with random controls ($n=20$) shows no functional link between geometry and reasoning mode ($p=0.286$). Thus, high probe accuracy reflects task format rather than computational structure, motivating routine format deconfounding in mechanistic interpretability.

### [11] [WRIT: Write-Read Intensive Trajectory Synthesis for Multi-Turn User-Facing Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02908)
*Hengrui Gu,Xiaotian Han,Kaixiong Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对现有智能体训练数据缺乏证据处理能力的缺陷，本文提出了WRIT合成框架，通过平衡“写入”复杂度和“读取”证据负载，训练出能在高信息负载下高效、准确决策的智能体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体训练大多侧重于通过组合任务来增加“写操作”的长度，忽视了智能体在做出决策前需要处理海量“读操作”证据的挑战。作者认为，如何从大量证据中提取关键信息并作出决策，是提升智能体能力的关键痛点，现有数据缺乏对此类高信息负载场景的覆盖。

Method: 提出了WRIT（Write-Read Intensive Trajectory Synthesis）流水线：1. 针对任务的“写入”决策数量和决策所需的“证据负载（Evidence Burden）”两个维度进行合成；2. 生成读密集（Read-heavy）与写密集（Write-intensive）任务；3. 通过用户行为指令多样化增强真实感；4. 在可执行环境中模拟交互，生成完整的训练轨迹数据。

Result: 仅使用2000条合成轨迹训练的4B模型，在$\tau^2$-bench评测中超过了GPT-5.1 no-think的表现，并大幅减少了推理时的Token消耗。结果表明，紧凑的监督微调（SFT）数据可以将昂贵的测试时推理转化为高效的智能体行为。

Conclusion: WRIT框架通过合成兼具“写密集”与“读密集”特征的训练数据，证明了高质量、信息密度大的合成数据能够显著提升智能体在复杂决策任务中的表现，同时降低推理阶段对额外计算资源的需求，实现了小模型在特定任务上对大模型的超越。

Abstract: Multi-turn user-facing agents must infer user intent from incomplete requests, collect missing information through dialogue and tools, and execute valid actions. A training trajectory records this process as an interleaved sequence of user messages, agent responses, tool calls, etc. Synthesizing sufficiently complex trajectory has become a central route to train agents: existing pipelines often increase difficulty by composing multiple user requests into longer tasks, producing write-intensive trajectories that train sequential execution.
  We argue that a single write decision can itself be difficult when the agent must gather and compare substantial read-tool evidence before its arguments become identifiable, a challenge that write-intensive data alone cannot address. Guided by this insight, we propose WRIT (\uline{W}rite-\uline{R}ead \uline{I}ntensive \uline{T}rajectory Synthesis), a pipeline for synthesizing multi-turn agent training trajectories along two complexity axes: the number of write decisions in a task and the evidence burden of each individual decision. WRIT first generates write-intensive and read-heavy tasks. It then diversifies user behavior instructions to reflect realistic conversational variation, and finally simulates agent-user interactions in an executable environment to produce complete training trajectories. The resulting data trains agents not only for longer task execution, but also for robust, evidence-grounded decision making under high information load. With only 2K synthesized trajectories, a 4B model trained on WRIT outperforms GPT-5.1 no-think on $τ^2$-bench and substantially reduces inference-time token usage, showing that compact SFT data can convert part of expensive test-time reasoning into efficient agent behavior.

</details>


### [12] [The Ghost Annotator: a Framework to Explore Human Label Variation in Content Moderation through Conformal Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02911)
*Mirko Lai,Alessandra Urbinati,Simona Frenda,Fabiana Vernero,Marco Antonio Stranisci*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种评估LLM不确定性与标注偏差的“幽灵标注者”框架，发现更大规模的模型在错误分类时往往表现出不合理的过度自信，且模型普遍存在与人类标注在人口统计学特征上的结构性偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前研究过度关注模型性能（准确率），而忽视了不确定性估计，特别是在LLM日益被用于生成标注数据的背景下。研究旨在通过建模LLM与人类标注者之间的行为关系，分析两者间的一致与分歧模式，并揭示模型中的结构性偏见。

Method: 本文结合共形预测（Conformal Prediction）与协同过滤式标注者表示，提出了一种评估LLM行为的框架。具体方法包括：引入非一致性分数（Non-Conformity Scores）来计算“幽灵预测”指标；构建“幽灵标注者”表示以量化模型预测与所有人类标注不一致的情况；通过余弦相似度度量来分析模型在不同社会人口统计学轴向上的行为差异。

Result: 实验评估了四个不同规模和系列的LLM在四个内容审核数据集上的表现。研究发现：1. 所有模型的不确定性均随人类标注者分歧的增加而上升；2. 规模较大的模型在与任何人类标注都不一致的文本分类上，反而倾向于表现出更高的置信度；3. “幽灵标注者”框架识别出了稳健的人口统计学失调模式，证实了模型存在源于预训练语料的结构性偏差。

Conclusion: 本文提出的“幽灵标注者”框架揭示了大型语言模型（LLM）在处理社会人口统计学偏差时的结构性问题。研究指出，模型规模越大，在与人类标注完全不一致的情况下越容易表现出过度的自信，这种现象暗示了预训练数据中存在的深层偏差。

Abstract: Current research primarily focuses on model performance, while comparatively less attention has been devoted to uncertainty estimation, particularly in settings where LLMs are increasingly used to generate annotated data. We introduce a framework combining conformal prediction with Collaborative Filtering-style annotators' representation to model LLM behavior in relation to human annotators and to analyze patterns of agreement and disagreement. Using Non-Conformity Scores, we introduce the Ghost Prediction metric and the Ghost Annotator representation to quantify cases in which model predictions diverge from all available human annotations. We compute cosine similarity measures to explore differences in model behavior across sociodemographic axes. We evaluated four LLMs of different size and families across four content moderation datasets. Our finding shows that while we find that all models uncertainty increases with annotator disagreement, larger models tend to be more confident in the classification of texts that are not aligned with any human annotation. Finally, the Ghost Annotator framework reveals a consistent and robust pattern of demographic misalignment, suggesting a structural bias likely rooted in pretraining corpora.

### [13] [Structures Facilitate Retrieve, Rerank, and Generate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03247)
*Yeqin Zhang,Haomin Fu,Xujie Zhang,Cam-Tu Nguyen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 针对当前文档基础对话系统忽略文档结构信息的问题，本文提出了 SF-Re2G 框架，通过引入段落对比学习和基于文档结构的子图重排序机制，有效提升了检索准确率与对话回复的质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的文档基础对话系统（DGDS）通常将文档切分为独立的段落进行处理，这种做法忽略了文档内部的结构信息，导致检索到的知识缺乏足够的上下文支持，难以在复杂的对话中生成准确且连贯的回复。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SF-Re2G 的框架，包含三个核心步骤：1. 通过对比学习增强段落表征，提升初步检索精度；2. 构建结构增强的重排序器，利用文档的邻近性（同一对话通常关联同一章节内的多个段落），通过子图建模对检索结果进行重排序；3. 在生成阶段利用子图上下文信息，以提高回复的准确性和连贯性。

Result: 在两个基准 DGDS 数据集（涵盖中英文）上的实验结果表明，SF-Re2G 在检索效果和回复生成质量上均优于现有的基线模型，证明了结合文档结构信息对于系统性能的显著贡献。

Conclusion: SF-Re2G 框架通过有效利用文档的层级结构信息，显著提升了文档基础对话系统（DGDS）在知识检索与回复生成方面的性能，为处理结构化外部知识提供了一种稳健且通用的解决方案。

Abstract: Document-grounded dialogue systems (DGDS) utilize knowledge from external documents to answer domain-specific user questions. Existing solutions typically divide documents into independent passages for retrieval and response generation. This approach, however, neither makes good use of structural information within documents nor provides enough (document) context for knowledge selection and responses. This paper proposes SF-Re2G to address such issues systematically. Firstly, we seek to improve a passage representation by contrasting it with others of the same section, thus improving the retrieval performance. Secondly, a structure-enhanced reranker is built, leveraging the fact that multiple grounding passages of one dialog turn tend to be in the same neighborhood. Specifically, candidates from the retrieval are grouped into subgraphs according to the document structure. The reranker will rescore the candidate integrating its group information. Finally, the chosen passages are used for responses, taking into account the subgraph context for better generation. Experimental results on two DGDS datasets validate our method for both Chinese and English.

### [14] [Linguistic Productivity in Large Language Models: Models Coerce, but do not Preempt](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02953)
*Claire Bonial,Claire Benet Post,Laura Michaelis,Harish Tayyar Madabushi*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了大型语言模型是否遵循语言学中的“巩固”与“抢占”机制，发现模型虽能习得构造性生产力，但由于缺乏对负面证据的利用，无法完全避免语义合法但缺乏训练基础的过度泛化错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于使用的语法理论认为语言的创造性生产力受到“巩固（entrenchment）”和“抢占（preemption）”两种频率信号的调节。本文旨在探讨大型语言模型是否同样遵循这些统计力量，以及这些力量如何影响模型在语言生产中的创造性与限制性。

Method: 通过测试不同架构的语言模型，观察其在“强制（coercion）”语境下对无意义词汇（nonce words）的构造性生产力表现（巩固作用），并评估统计抢占机制是否能有效防止模型在语义合法但缺乏先例的情况下产生过度泛化（preemption）。

Result: 研究发现，模型规模越大，越能识别并重现基于巩固作用的构造性生产力；然而，即便最大的模型也无法利用统计抢占来避免对从未观察到但语义合理的模式进行过度泛化。

Conclusion: 研究表明，尽管大型语言模型（LLM）能通过基于使用的方法习得并重现建设性生产力（基于巩固作用），但它们在处理负面证据和统计抢占方面存在局限性，无法有效抑制语义上可行但未在训练数据中出现的过度泛化现象。

Abstract: Usage-based theories of grammars posit that creative productivity of the structures of language is both bolstered and constrained by two distinct frequency signals: entrenchment, stemming from high frequency usage, and preemption, stemming from having never observed a particular linguistic structure in a context where one might expect that structure to appear. Large Language Models are also usage-based, in the sense that the structures of language are learned through exposure to vast amounts of text. Here, we test whether or not the opposing statistical forces of entrenchment and preemption also encourage and constrain linguistic productivity in LLMs. We demonstrate across model architectures that larger models recognize and can reproduce with nonce words constructional productivity (entrenchment) in cases of coercion, wherein the broader constructional context coerces an atypical interpretation of a lexical item. However, we also show that even the largest models do not extend negative evidence to novel language, and statistical preemption does not enable models to avoid overgeneralization of patterns that are semantically felicitous, but never observed in data.

</details>


### [15] [Re-Ranking Through an Attribution Lens for Citation Quality in Legal QA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03728)
*Mohamed Hesham Elganayni,Selim Saleh*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文指出法律问答中语义相似度检索存在缺陷，并提出利用扰动归因分析训练轻量级重排序器，显著提升了RAG系统的引用准确性与专业性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在法律问答任务中，传统的基于语义相似度的检索方法与模型对文档的实际引用行为并不相关，甚至在某些情况下表现不如随机检索，这严重影响了法律问答的准确性和引用忠实度。研究旨在解决这一关键的“检索-生成”错位问题。

Method: 针对现有基于语义相似度的检索在法律问答中表现不佳的问题，研究者提出了一种轻量级重排序器（Re-ranker）。该方法基于持续的扰动归因得分（Continuous perturbation-based attribution scores）对检索出的段落进行重新排序，然后再输入至语言模型进行生成。通过AQuAECHR基准测试，利用两个不同的语言模型进行了五折交叉验证评估。

Result: 实验表明，通过所提出的重排序方法，系统的引用忠实度（Citation faithfulness）和与专家标准答案的一致性均得到显著提升。此外，研究发现不同模型训练出的重排序器能够产生共享的相关性信号，显示出一定的跨模型迁移能力。

Conclusion: 基于扰动的归因分析（Perturbation-based attribution）可以提供一种有效的、模型不可知的训练信号，用于优化法律领域的检索增强生成（RAG）系统，提升引用忠实度。此外，重排序器能够有效过滤模型特定噪声，生成具有跨模型迁移能力的通用相关性信号。

Abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation systems for legal question answering typically retrieve passages based on semantic similarity and provide them to a language model, which then generates cited answers. Prior work assumes that highly ranked passages are most likely to be usefully cited by the model. Perturbation-based attribution methods, such as C-LIME, have been used exclusively for post-hoc explanation. However, on the AQuAECHR benchmark, semantic similarity does not correlate with passage attribution. Within a retriever's candidate pool, similarity-based ranking performs worse than random selection at surfacing gold citation paragraphs. To address this limitation, a lightweight cross-encoder is trained on continuous perturbation-based attribution scores to re-rank passages prior to generation. This approach is evaluated on the AQuAECHR benchmark, using two language models and five-fold cross-validation. The re-ranker substantially improves citation faithfulness and alignment with gold expert answers. Notably, two re-rankers trained independently on different models converge beyond their raw attribution agreement. This finding indicates that the cross-encoder reduces model-specific noise and produces a shared relevance signal that partially transfers across models, although same-model re-ranking remains more effective. These results demonstrate that perturbation-based attribution provides a practical, model-agnostic training signal for citation-aware retrieval.

</details>


### [16] [Fast-dLLM++: Fréchet Profile Decoding for Faster Diffusion LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02955)
*Siva Rajesh Kasa,Yasong Dai,Sumit Negi,Hongdong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: Fast-dLLM++ 是一种针对扩散大语言模型的训练无关解码优化方案，通过引入“Fréchet 概况解码”策略，利用 Token 生成的异质置信度而非最差置信度进行并行提交，从而在不影响准确率的情况下显著提升了推理吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的扩散大语言模型加速方法（如 Fast-dLLM）在并行解码时采用了同质的高置信度假设，即每次并行解码受限于该集合中置信度最低的 Token，这导致了严重的性能浪费。作者旨在通过利用不同生成步骤中存在的异质性置信度分布，进一步提升推理速度。

Method: 提出了一种名为“Fréchet 概况解码（Fréchet profile decoding）”的训练无关方法。该方法不再依赖单一的最差置信度（最弱 Token）作为提交依据，而是根据完整的已排序置信度概况动态选择并行提交集。这种方法将 Fast-dLLM 的选择规则推广至异质置信度场景，并提供了一个可证明的“异质性增益（heterogeneity bonus）”。

Result: 在 GSM8K、MATH、HumanEval 和 MBPP 等多个基准测试中，基于 LLaDA-8B 模型的实验表明，Fast-dLLM++ 在保持相当准确率的前提下，推理吞吐量最高提升了 37%，有效优化了准确率与吞吐量的权衡曲线。

Conclusion: Fast-dLLM++ 通过引入基于 Fréchet 概况的解码策略，成功克服了传统扩散大语言模型在并行生成时的性能瓶颈，在不改变模型架构和训练的前提下，实现了更高的吞吐量与推理效率，证明了考虑 Token 置信度异质性的解码规则具有显著优势。

Abstract: Diffusion large language models promise parallel token generation, yet inference remains bottlenecked by deciding which masked tokens can be safely committed together. Fast-dLLM addressed this with KV caching and confidence-guided parallel decoding, but its decoding theory uses a homogeneous high-confidence assumption that effectively reduces each candidate set to its weakest selected token. We argue that this leaves speed on the table because real decoding steps exhibit heterogeneous confidence profiles. We propose \textbf{Fast-dLLM++}, a training-free extension that introduces \emph{Fréchet profile decoding}: selecting parallel commit sets from the full sorted confidence profile rather than a single worst-case confidence. The resulting rule is a heterogeneous-confidence generalization of Fast-dLLM's factor selector and it recovers the previous rule exactly in the equal-confidence case and adds a provable \emph{heterogeneity bonus} when the selected tokens have uneven confidences. Fast-dLLM++ leaves the model, diffusion process, and cache implementation entirely unchanged, making it a drop-in replacement for existing Fast-dLLM decoding. Experiments on GSM8K, MATH, HumanEval, and MBPP with the LLaDA-8B model show that the theoretical improvement translates directly into empirical gains: profile-aware selection improves the accuracy--throughput frontier by exploiting safe parallelism that weakest-token rules miss, achieving up to 37\% higher throughput at comparable accuracy. Our anonymous code release is at https://github.com/Ringo-Star/FastdLLM_plusplus.

</details>


### [17] [EURO-5K: When Does Domain Pretraining Matter? Benchmarking Transformers for EU Reporting Obligation Extraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02971)
*Marios Koniaris,Vasileios Kotronis,Eugenia Giannini,Panayiotis Tsanakas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出了用于欧盟立法中报告义务自动提取的EURO-5K数据集，并对比分析了BERT类模型与大语言模型在不同微调策略下的表现，证明了领域预训练与高效微调技术在提升法律文本信息抽取效率与准确性方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从复杂的欧盟立法中自动提取报告义务对于降低监管负担至关重要。然而，法律文本的结构复杂性使得现有NLP方法难以精准区分报告义务条款。目前缺乏专门的数据集、明确的标注准则以及对不同提取范式与领域适应策略的系统评估，限制了合规自动化技术的发展。

Method: 1. 构建EURO-5K数据集：包含来自136个欧盟立法文件的句子级报告义务及负样本。
2. 实验对比：对比判别式（BERT系）与生成式（LLM）模型，并评估全量微调与参数高效微调（QLoRA）。
3. 性能评估：将上述方法与传统模式/依赖项匹配及少样本提示词方法进行对比，并进行跨数据集验证。

Result: 1. 判别式模型（BERT）和生成式模型（LLM）在全量微调后均达到约0.89的F1值。
2. 在受限的参数高效微调场景下，预训练的法律模型优于通用模型。
3. 法律预训练显著加速了模型在少量数据下的学习收敛。
4. 模型在外部监管数据集上验证了其作为专业报告义务提取器的泛化能力，且数据量达到3K左右即可收敛。

Conclusion: 研究表明，针对特定法律文本的报告义务提取任务，判别式模型（如BERT）和生成式模型（如LLM）均能达到高精度。尽管通用模型表现不俗，但在数据受限或算力受限的情境下，针对法律领域进行预训练和参数高效微调（QLoRA）具有显著优势。该研究提出的EURO-5K数据集及相关工具为欧盟合规自动化提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Extracting reporting obligations from EU legislation is critical for assessing and reducing regulatory reporting burden. However, distinguishing reporting requirements from structurally similar provisions requires specialised legal understanding. Current legal NLP methods lack specialised datasets with clear guidelines and comparative evaluation of extraction paradigms and domain adaptation strategies. We curate EURO-5K, a corpus of sentence-level reporting obligations and challenging negative examples from 136 EU legislative acts. On this dataset, we train and compare discriminative token-classification models (BERT-style) and generative span-extraction models (LLMs), evaluating both full fine-tuning and parameter-efficient QLoRA against baselines (pattern and dependency-based extraction, few-shot prompting). Results show that fully fine-tuned generic and legal BERT models achieve similar performance (0.89 F1), while fine-tuned LLMs match encoder accuracy for sentence-level extraction. Legal pretraining offers only small gains for generative models. In contrast, it is clearly beneficial when adaptation capacity is constrained, as parameter-efficient tuning of Legal-BERT outperforms its generic counterpart. Learning curve analysis demonstrates that legal pretraining accelerates early learning with minimal data. All approaches converge around 3K samples with diminishing returns thereafter, validating dataset sufficiency. Cross-dataset evaluation on two external regulatory corpora shows that our models behave as specialised reporting obligation extractors rather than generic regulatory classifiers. We release EURO-5K, trained models, and an interactive demo with explainability visualizations and structured RDF export. These demonstrate that both paradigms and parameter-efficient training provide practical tools for regulatory compliance automation.

</details>


### [18] [Chatbots Output Meaningful (but Problematic) Language](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02973)
*Matthew Stone,Una Stojnić*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文主张大语言模型的输出本身即具有意义，无需假设AI具备心理状态或意图；意义的产生机制并不等同于人类的沟通意图，现有的语言理论已可解释AI的文本生成，且这一结论不涉及对AI技术好坏或伦理价值的判断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对当前认知科学、语言学及哲学界对于“AI生成的语言是否具有真实意义”的激烈争议，探讨为何传统意向性理论无法解释AI输出的意义，以及如何在不依赖拟人化假设的情况下，构建一套统一的语言意义理论，以调和普通用户直觉与学术界观点之间的矛盾。

Method: 本文采用了哲学分析与论证的方法。作者挑战了那种认为“必须具备意图和心理状态才能产生意义”的传统意向性（Intentionalist）语言观，通过解构意义与意图之间的必要联系，证明了在无需 anthropomorphism（拟人化）假设的前提下，可以构建一套能解释AI输出具有“意义”的理论框架。

Result: 研究表明，意义的门槛远比人们想象的要低。AI输出的有意义性无需诉诸心理状态、意图、理性或沟通能力。人类语言生产本身有时也会脱离说话者的意图，因此，无需特殊的“去拟人化”修饰，现有的语言理论已足以覆盖AI的文本生成。

Conclusion: 作者认为，将大语言模型（LLM）的输出视为有意义的，并不需要赋予其心理状态或意图。现有的语言理论完全适用于AI，且承认AI输出的意义与对其技术评价或伦理批判是相互独立的。

Abstract: Are utterances by AI chatbots meaningful? Concretely, if a user asks, say, Anthropic's agent Claude, "What is the capital of Spain?" and Claude answers, "Madrid is the capital of Spain," does that sentence have its ordinary meaning -- and does it express a true proposition? Most ordinary users, as well as AI engineers, take the answer to be trivially "yes." However, many cognitive scientists, linguists, and philosophers of language argue that dominant intentionalist accounts of language and meaning deliver the opposite conclusion.
  Theorists more sympathetic to ordinary users' intuitions have therefore advocated a radical "de-anthropomorphization" of language, revising our understanding of mental states, intentions, and semantic content to capture the intuition that the outputs of LLMs are meaningful. We take a different approach. While we, too, argue that LLM outputs are meaningful, we contend that a proper theory of human language already applies, as is, to current chatbots. Meaning is a low bar: claiming that LLM outputs are meaningful does not require positing mental states, intentions, rationality, or the cognitive capacities requisite for communication in LLMs -- or, indeed, making any other anthropomorphic assumptions. People do have communicative intentions (typically successful ones), but nevertheless, even in humans, language production can depart from what the speaker has in mind.
  Our view has important consequences for how we should theorize about -- and critically engage with -- both human linguistic output and synthetically generated text. In particular, to say that chatbots produce meaningful text is not by any means to endorse what they output, or to assume that the technology is (or is not) good, powerful, appropriate, or useful.

</details>


### [19] [Memory Retrieval for Changing Preferences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02976)
*Yuehan Qin,Li Li,Linxin Song,Wei Yang,Jiate Li,Yuqing Yang,Yue Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于贝叶斯因子效用评估的记忆检索新框架，通过衡量历史对话对当前响应的证据强度，解决了长对话中动态用户偏好的精确识别与记忆选择问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文对话系统多依赖启发式检索或全量记忆使用，无法有效应对用户偏好随时间演变及潜在冲突的特性。现有方法多基于浅层语义相似度，缺乏对记忆信息真实有效性的衡量。

Method: 提出了一种基于贝叶斯因子（Bayes factor）的统一框架。该方法通过量化每个历史对话轮次对提升模型生成参考响应似然概率的贡献（即“效用”），来评估该轮次作为用户潜在偏好证据的强度，从而指导系统在何时访问记忆以及选择哪些内容。

Result: 在四个异构记忆基准测试中，该方法在偏好密集型长上下文任务中表现显著优于现有的基于嵌入（embedding）的检索方法，同时在低密度、语义相似度足以解决的任务中仍保持竞争优势。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将记忆检索建模为效用估计，成功解决了长对话系统中用户偏好动态变化导致的记忆选择难题，证明了基于贝叶斯因子的证据强度度量在处理偏好密集型任务中的优越性。

Abstract: Long-context dialogue systems must decide both when to access memory and which parts of the interaction history are relevant. Existing approaches typically rely on heuristic retrieval signals or always-on memory usage, failing to account for the changing and potentially inconsistent nature of user preferences. In this work, we propose a unified framework for memory access and selection based on changing preferences. We formulate personalized memory retrieval as identifying which historical turns provide evidence about a user's latent preference state, rather than relying on surface-level semantic similarity. To this end, we quantify the utility of each memory turn using a Bayes factor, defined as the improvement in the model's likelihood of the reference response when the turn is included in context. This provides a principled measure of evidence strength and a unified signal for both memory access and selection. By framing memory retrieval as utility estimation, the model learns to identify salient turns and regulate memory usage based on expected utility. Experiments on four heterogeneous memory benchmarks show that our approach outperforms existing embedding-based retrieval on long-context, preference-intensive tasks where modeling changing preferences is essential, while remaining competitive in low-density regimes where semantic similarity suffices.

</details>


### [20] [Predicting Inference-Time Scaling Gains from Labeled Validation-Set Output Statistics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02981)
*Luyang Zhang,Jingyan Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通过轻量级统计特征高效预测“最佳N选一”推理增益的方法，通过仅在验证集上采样即可准确估计模型性能提升，无需全量运行奖励模型，大幅降低了推理调优的计算成本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: “最佳N选一”推理扩展虽能有效提升模型精度，但预估其增益通常需要昂贵的端到端全量计算。现有研究虽探索了采样统计量与模型行为的关系，但尚未确立一种稳定且紧凑的预测指标。因此，本文旨在寻找一种轻量级方法，仅通过少量验证集采样即可预测推理性能的提升，从而避免高昂的评分成本。

Method: 研究采用了岭回归（ridge predictor）模型对验证集采样特征进行拟合，利用Bootstrap-Lasso进行特征稳定性分析，并结合集中度分析（concentration analysis）对线性近似残差进行了量化。最终提取出包括模型提示词层面的共识度、标签辅助下的首个正确样本位置以及补全长度方差这三个关键特征。

Result: 实验证明，基于所提取的“三核心特征”加上熵（entropy）辅助指标构建的岭回归预测器，在多种基础模型、后训练方法及数学推理任务中表现出色，其预测值与实际的最佳N选一增益之间的Spearman相关系数（ρ）高达0.90。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过使用少量验证集样本，结合模型的一致性（agreement）、首个正确样本位置（first-correct-sample position）和补全长度方差（completion-length variance）这三个核心特征，可以准确预测“最佳N选一”（Best-of-N）策略带来的推理增益。该方法在无需大规模端到端评估的情况下，即可通过轻量级预测器实现高效的配置筛选，显著降低了计算成本。

Abstract: Best-of-$N$ inference scaling (drawing $N$ candidate answers from a language model and returning the one a reward model ranks highest) improves accuracy by an amount that varies across models, but predicting that amount in advance currently requires running the procedure end-to-end. Prior work links cheap statistics of a model's sampled outputs and validation-set correctness (how often samples agree, how diverse they are, how confident the model is, and where correct samples appear) to model behavior, but does not isolate which of these form a stable, compact predictor of best-of-$N$ gain. We fit ridge predictors on features computed from a single labeled validation-set sampling pass, use bootstrap-Lasso as a stability analysis of the candidate feature set, and give a concentration analysis with an explicit linear-approximation residual. Across three base-model families, six post-training methods, and math and reasoning task domains, the stability analysis identifies a strict three-feature core spanning prompt-level agreement spread, label-assisted first-correct-sample position, and completion-length variance; a compact ridge predictor built from this core plus an entropy add-on reaches Spearman $ρ= 0.90$ with actual best-of-$N$ gain under a reward-model verifier. The intended use is labeled validation-set screening of candidate configurations before paying the full reward-model scoring cost.

</details>

*Feng Li,Yoritaka Iwata*

Main category: cs.CL

Abstract: The correct sequence of courses in the curriculum based on prerequisites between courses is of great importance for students to develop their knowledge and skills holistically. Simultaneously, education institutions encounter difficulties in providing adequate academic advice for the correct sequence due to limited education resources. To address these challenges, we propose a locally deployed RAG-based academic advising system grounded in syllabus information. By combining large language models with retrieval from structured syllabus data, the system is designed to support course selection, prerequisite understanding, and personalized study planning in a privacy-preserving manner.

### [22] [Pretraining Language Models on Historical Text](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02991)
*Xiaoxi Luo,Zachary Shinnick,Niclas Griesshaber,Yixuan Wang,Junchi Yu,Freda Shi,Philip Torr,Yao Lu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文介绍了TypewriterLM，这是一个专门使用1913年前历史文本训练的7.24B语言模型，通过配套的历史语料库、词汇接地指令微调框架及专业评估基准，解决了历史语言建模中的数据泄露与时间一致性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型往往包含现代偏见或跨时间的信息泄露，难以准确模拟和分析特定历史时期的语言与知识背景。因此，作者旨在开发一种完全基于1913年以前英语文本的专用语言模型，以解决历史研究中数据质量、时间一致性和评估困难的问题。

Method: 1. 构建TypewriterCorpus：收集并清洗了54B token的历史语料，并严格进行了时间泄露预防。2. 提出词汇接地指令微调（Lexically Grounded Instruction Tuning）：设计了一种将回复约束在历史原始文档中的微调框架。3. 构建评估基准：推出了History-Event，专门用于测试历史领域的模型能力、时间一致性及数据泄露情况。

Result: 成功发布了7.24B参数的TypewriterLM模型，以及相应的历史语料库、指令微调数据集（History-LIMA和History-SelfInstruct）和评估基准（History-Event），为历史语言建模研究奠定了基础。

Conclusion: 本文通过构建TypewriterLM，证明了在历史文本上训练专用语言模型是可行的，并为历史领域的研究提供了强有力的基准与工具，为理解过去提供了新的计算视角。

Abstract: We introduce TypewriterLM, a 7.24B History language model (LM) trained exclusively on English text predating 1913. Developing History LMs requires addressing challenges in data quality and availability, preventing temporal leakage, designing temporally consistent post-training pipelines, and constructing reliable evaluations. To address these issues, we construct TypewriterCorpus, a 54B-token historical corpus collected from diverse archival and linguistically annotated sources with extensive data cleaning and leakage mitigation procedures. Furthermore, we introduce lexically grounded instructing tuning, a post-training framework that constraints responses to remain directly grounded in historical source documents. Using this framework we construct two historical instruction tuning datasets: History-LIMA and History-SelfInstruct. To evaluate capability and temporal consistency, we introduce History-Event, a benchmark suite for evaluating competence, temporal grounding and data leakage. We release TypewriterLM and all associated resources to support future research on historical language models.

### [23] [Hint-Guided Diversified Policy Optimization for LLM Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03021)
*Zhiyu Cao,Kaixin Wu,Mingjie Zhong,Peifeng Li,Xiaobo Li,Can Ye,Qiaoming Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出HDPO框架，通过引入提示引导机制，使大模型能够在推理前探索多种解题路径并选择最优方案，从而显著提升了模型的推理能力与决策多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）方法往往局限于单一的结论正确性，缺乏对解题过程多样性的考量，未能模拟人类“评估多种方法并选择最优方案”的认知过程，导致模型推理能力受限。

Method: 提出“提示引导的多样化策略优化”（HDPO），包含两个阶段：1. 结构化推理冷启动；2. 提示引导的多样化强化学习。模型首先列出多种潜在的解题思路作为“提示”，随后通过策略选择最可靠的路径进行深入推理。

Result: 实验结果表明，HDPO不仅显著提升了大模型的推理准确率，还增强了模型生成解题思路的多样性，并有效提高了模型识别最可靠解决方案的能力。

Conclusion: HDPO框架通过引入“提出-选择-思考”的决策范式，有效地弥补了传统RLVR在探索多样性解决路径方面的不足，为提升大模型复杂推理能力提供了一种高效且具备鲁棒性的新方案。

Abstract: Recent developments in Large Language Models (LLMs) have showcased impressive reasoning capabilities, with Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) being a promising enhancement strategy. However, existing reward mechanisms are constrained to the outcome-level correctness and lack explicit signals to guide the model to consider diverse solutions. In contrast, human problem solving typically involves evaluating multiple potential approaches and selecting the most reliable solution, a cognitive process that current RLVR frameworks do not explicitly incentivize. Inspired by this, we propose Hint-Guided Diversified Policy Optimization (HDPO), allowing the model to first list all potential candidate solution outlines as hints and then select the most reliable one for further reasoning. HDPO comprises two stages of Cold Start for Structured Reasoning and Hint-Guided Diversified Reinforcement Learning to incentivize the model to generate diverse and reliable solutions following the ``propose-select-think'' trajectory. Experimental results show that HDPO effectively boosts LLM reasoning and enhances the diversity of candidate solutions as well as the LLM's ability to identify reliable solutions.

</details>


### [24] [Hallucinations as Orthogonal Noise: Inference-Time Manifold Alignment via Dynamic Contextual Orthogonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03022)
*Mingkuan Zhao,Wentao Hu,Tianchen Huang,Yuheng Min,Suquan Chen,Yide Gao,Yanbo Zhai,Shuangyong Song,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本论文提出了“动态上下文正交化”（DCO）方法，通过将幻觉视为模型残差流中的正交噪声，在推理阶段通过动态正交分解抑制幻觉，在显著提升输出忠实度的同时保留了模型的核心知识储备。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在部署过程中面临严重的幻觉问题（生成与事实或逻辑不符的内容）。现有研究缺乏对幻觉内在几何机制的理解，且常见的减缓幻觉方法往往以牺牲模型参数化知识为代价，难以在幻觉抑制和性能维持之间取得平衡。

Method: 提出了一种名为“动态上下文正交化”（DCO）的推理时干预方法。该方法基于线性表示假设，将幻觉视为残差流中相对于语义流形的正交噪声。DCO利用输入残差流作为动态上下文锚点，对注意力头的输出进行正交分解，并结合分层Z-score抑制机制，选择性地减弱偏离语义子空间的离群正交分量。

Result: 在Llama-3-8B和70B模型上，针对XSum、NQ-Swap和IFEval等基准测试的实验表明，DCO在上下文忠实度方面优于现有的干预基线，同时在TriviaQA和TruthfulQA等知识密集型任务中保持了高性能，有效缓解了幻觉抑制与知识保留之间的权衡冲突。

Conclusion: 该研究通过验证大语言模型幻觉的几何性质，证明了基于语义流形对齐的干预方法（DCO）能够有效提升模型输出的忠实度，同时维持参数化知识的保留，为解决模型幻觉提供了一种高效且具备理论支撑的方案。

Abstract: Hallucination in Large Language Models (LLMs), characterized by the generation of content inconsistent with contextual facts or logical constraints -- remains a persistent challenge for reliable deployment. In this work, we address this issue through a geometric framework rooted in the linear representation hypothesis. We propose that hallucinations manifest as orthogonal noise relative to the semantic manifold of the residual stream. Specifically, we hypothesize that while attention heads ideally propagate information congruent with the context subspace, hallucinations arise when specific heads introduce components orthogonal to this subspace, disrupting the coherence of the latent representation. Based on this formulation, we introduce Dynamic Contextual Orthogonalization (DCO), an inference-time intervention method. DCO utilizes the input residual stream as a dynamic context anchor to perform orthogonal decomposition on attention head outputs. To distinguish between context-aligned semantic updates and divergent noise, DCO employs a layer-wise Z-score suppression mechanism that selectively attenuates outlier orthogonal components based on statistical distributions. Evaluations on Llama-3-8B and 70B across benchmarks such as XSum, NQ-Swap, and IFEval demonstrate that DCO achieves superior contextual faithfulness compared to state-of-the-art intervention baselines. Furthermore, DCO maintains high performance on knowledge-intensive tasks like TriviaQA and TruthfulQA, effectively mitigating the trade-off between hallucination suppression and parametric knowledge retention often observed in existing methods. Our findings validate the geometric interpretation of hallucinations and establish DCO as a computationally efficient approach for enforcing manifold alignment.Our code is available at https://github.com/Harry-Miral/DCO

### [26] [Conditional Hypothesis Generation for LLM-Based Text Analysis with Researcher-Specified Covariates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03029)
*Paiheng Xu,Jing Liu,Wei Ai*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种名为“条件假设生成”的框架，通过引入协变量控制与计量经济学技术，使大语言模型在计算社会科学中能够排除混淆干扰，更准确地发现不同子群下的实质性语言模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 计算社会科学中，现有基于LLM的假设生成方法往往忽略了协变量对语言模式的影响，导致生成的假设容易受到混淆变量干扰，无法反映研究者真正关心的实质性差异。该研究旨在通过引入协变量控制，引导模型生成更具解释性且在相关子群内成立的假设。

Method: 研究提出了“条件假设生成”框架，结合两项计量经济学方法：一是引入特征-协变量交互项（Feature-Covariate Interactions）以检测符号反转现象；二是通过层内去均值（Within-stratum Demeaning）和逆频率重加权（Inverse-frequency Reweighting）来缓解层级分布不均及样本不平衡问题。

Result: 合成实验表明，该方法在处理特定混淆情况时优于全局基准模型。在两个真实世界数据集上的专家评估结果证实，引入协变量感知的生成方法能够更有效地从相关子群中挖掘出具有研究价值和实际意义的假设。

Conclusion: 该研究通过引入条件假设生成框架，成功解决了LLM在社会科学应用中因忽略协变量而产生的混淆偏差问题。研究证明了利用计量经济学方法处理分层不平衡和符号反转现象，能有效提升假设生成的解释力与可靠性，为计算社会科学提供了一种更具针对性和稳健性的研究工具。

Abstract: A core goal of computational social science is to discover interpretable differences in how language varies across outcomes of interest, such as political affiliation or instructional quality. Recent LLM-based hypothesis generation methods describe such differences in natural language, but select for globally discriminative patterns without accounting for covariates that shape the data based on researchers' domain knowledge. When covariates are ignored, selected patterns can reflect confounds rather than differences of substantive interest. We introduce conditional hypothesis generation, a framework that incorporates researcher-specified covariates to steer hypothesis discovery toward differences that hold within relevant subgroups. Two challenges arise: the target subgroup may be underrepresented (stratum imbalance), and the direction of a difference may reverse across subgroups (sign reversal). We propose two econometrics-inspired methods: one introduces feature--covariate interactions to detect sign reversals, and the other applies within-stratum demeaning and inverse-frequency reweighting to equalize underrepresented strata. Synthetic experiments show each method outperforms global baselines in its targeted setting, and expert evaluation on two real-world datasets confirms that covariate-aware generation surfaces more useful hypotheses within relevant subgroups.

### [27] [The Deliberative Illusion: Diagnosing Factual Attrition and Stance Homogenization in Multi-Agent LLM Deliberation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03032)
*Herun Wan,Jiaying Wu,Minnan Luo,Fanxiao Li,Ningnan Wang,Nancy F. Chen,Min-Yen Kan*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了多智能体LLM系统存在的“审议错觉”：讨论过程会导致关键事实的大量流失和立场强制趋同，使得智能体在信息极度匮乏的情况下达成虚假共识。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多智能体LLM系统通常将“达成共识”视为成功互动的标志。然而，对于需要深思熟虑的问题，可靠性取决于系统能否保留解释问题所需的关键事实和多元观点。作者旨在揭示并量化多智能体讨论中可能存在的盲目共识问题（即“审议错觉”）。

Method: 作者提出了DelibTrace评估框架。该框架将复杂议题分解为原子级事实，识别其中的关键事实，并将这些事实分配给不同智能体，进而追踪在讨论回合中这些事实的留存情况。研究在伦理和新闻类议题上对三个主流LLM系列进行了测试。

Result: 多智能体讨论导致了严重的“事实损耗”（高达72%的关键事实丢失）和“立场同质化”（多元观点崩溃）。这种信息损失不仅导致最终共识基于极少的信息，且容易被恶意智能体误导，最终立场往往仍受模型原始偏差的影响。结论是：智能体可能在“知之甚少”的情况下却达成更多共识。

Conclusion: 多智能体LLM系统的讨论往往会导致“审议错觉”，即虽然达成了共识，但系统却损失了关键事实且立场趋于单一。该研究强调，在评估多智能体系统时，不能仅以共识作为成功的指标，必须关注互动过程中关键事实、不确定性和合法分歧的保留情况。

Abstract: Multi-agent LLM systems often treat consensus as evidence of successful interaction. For deliberative problems, however, reliability depends on whether agents preserve the facts and viewpoints needed to interpret an issue. We identify the deliberative illusion: discussion produces (1) factual attrition, the progressive loss of issue-critical facts, alongside (2) stance homogenization, the collapse of diverse positions toward consensus. To measure this process, we introduce DelibTrace, a framework that decomposes each issue into atomic facts, labels issue-critical ones, distributes them across agents, and tracks their survival across discussion rounds. Across ethical and news-based deliberation with three representative LLM families, multi-agent discussion erases up to 72% of issue-critical facts. This loss is consequential: retained evidence can reconstruct the issue misleadingly, final stances remain anchored in base-model priors, and a single malicious agent can inject misinformation into the shrinking shared context. These results reveal a sharper risk: agents can agree more while knowing less. We call for evaluations that measure which facts, uncertainties, and legitimate disagreements survive interaction.

### [28] [The Geometry of LLM-as-Judge: Why Inter-LLM Consensus Is Not Human Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03043)
*Sourabrata Mukherjee,Hamna Hamna,Kalika Bali,Sunayana Sitaram*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究通过几何分析揭示了“大模型作为评判者”在主观任务中普遍存在与人类评价正交的“共同偏见”，证明了模型间的一致性并不代表人类对齐，主张必须进行几何检查以验证评价子空间的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前“大模型作为评判者”已成为标准范式，但研究者发现模型间的高一致性与低人机一致性并存。研究旨在探究这种现象究竟是源于模型捕捉到了真实的评价信号，还是仅仅因为模型间存在某种“共同偏见”。

Method: 研究采用几何分析方法，跨越4个印度语言社区数据集、8种语言及41个模型，测量了四个关键几何指标：得分分布（score spread）、有效秩（effective rank）、与人类子空间的夹角（principal angle）以及模型间与人机间的堆叠相关性（stacked correlations），并使用自举法（bootstrap）计算置信区间。

Result: 结果显示：1. 主观评价中，模型使用的评分范围不足人类的一半，评价轴向与人类几乎正交（87°-89°）；2. 模型间的相关性高于人机相关性；3. 在事实性任务中，评估表现接近人类；4. 微调和偏好优化虽能改善得分分布，但无法显著改变评估轴向；5. 后验校准能显著优化评价性能，甚至使小模型超越顶级模型，但距离人类的一致性仍有差距。

Conclusion: 研究得出结论：大模型作为评判者（LLM-as-judges）之间的高一致性并不等同于与人类对齐。当评估主观任务时，模型倾向于在高度受限且与人类正交的子空间内达成共识，反映的是共同的偏见而非对真实人类偏好的捕捉。评估结论在涉及事实性问题时更接近人类，但对于主观 rubric，仅靠微调无法改变模型的评价轴向，只有通过少量人工标注进行后验校准才能有效提升模型对齐度。

Abstract: LMs-as-judges are now standard, yet judges agree strongly with one another while agreeing only weakly with humans. We test whether this reflects shared signal or shared bias by measuring four geometric quantities on the standard LLM-as-judge stack across four community-built Indic datasets, eight Indic languages, and 41 LLM judges: score spread, effective rank, principal angle to the human subspace, and stacked correlations among judges and humans, all with bootstrap confidence intervals.
  On subjective rubrics, judges use less than half the human score range ($σ_J / σ_H \approx 0.3$--$0.5$). Their evaluation axis is nearly orthogonal to the human one and noticeably further from humans than humans are from each other ($87^\circ$--$89^\circ$ versus $78^\circ$--$81^\circ$). Inter-LLM agreement exceeds LLM--human agreement ($r_{LL} \approx 0.35$ versus $r_{LH} \approx 0.27$--$0.32$).
  On a rubric with a verifiable factual answer, the same diagnostics fall back into the human range (axis $58.5^\circ$; $r_{LH} = 0.519$). Fine-tuning and preference optimization recover spread ($0.32 \rightarrow 1.08$) but barely move the axis (still $87^\circ$--$88^\circ$). Only post-hoc calibration on a small human-anchored set improves all four community-health rubrics together, placing a calibrated 24B Indic judge ($r = 0.184$) ahead of GPT-5.5 ($r = 0.123$), yet still short of human reliability (human-human $r = 0.474$ on the verifiable rubric).
  We argue that inter-LLM agreement should be considered evidence of human alignment only when a direct geometric check on the judge's score subspace passes; otherwise, the consensus reflects agreement within a collapsed subspace.

</details>


### [29] [G^2C-MT: Graph-Guided Context Selection for Document-Level Machine Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03078)
*Baijun Ji,Zixuan Zhou,Xiangyu Duan,Yu Liu,Longbo Sun,Rupu Wei,Bohong Zhao*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 G^2C-MT 的新型框架，将文档级翻译中的上下文选择转化为语篇图上的路径发现问题，利用深度偏置随机游走为大模型提供结构化的语篇引导，从而显著改善了跨段落的翻译一致性与质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文档级机器翻译方法在处理远距离段落间的结构化语篇依赖时能力不足，且往往依赖高昂的大语言模型推理成本或非结构化的上下文获取方式。

Method: 1. 构建轻量级语篇图：将段落视为节点，综合语义相似度、邻接关系和关键词重叠度来建模节点间关系；2. 深度偏置随机游走：在该图上执行采样，为目标段落生成高质量的后向上下文路径；3. 多路径采样：支持通过多路径采样并聚合不同翻译候选，增强模型面对语篇歧义时的鲁棒性。

Result: 实验表明，G^2C-MT 在多种主流大语言模型（如 DeepSeek-V3、Gemini-2.5-Flash-lite、Qwen-2.5/3 系列）上均超越了现有的强基线方法，在多领域语料上实现了翻译质量的显著提升。

Conclusion: 本文提出的 G^2C-MT 框架通过图结构引导的路径发现，有效解决了文档级机器翻译中长距离语篇依赖建模的难题，证明了结构化上下文选择在提升大语言模型翻译性能方面的有效性和通用性。

Abstract: Effective document-level machine translation (DocMT) requires capturing long-range discourse dependencies. Recent work has explored retrieval-based and discourse-aware context selection. However, these approaches often lack an explicit mechanism for modeling structured discourse dependencies between distant paragraphs in a document. In this paper, we propose G^2C-MT (Graph-Guided Context for Machine Translation), which views DocMT context selection as a structured path discovery problem on a lightweight discourse graph, rather than retrieving unstructured context sets or relying on expensive LLM-based discourse modeling. In detail, we represent each paragraph as a node and model the relationship between each pair of nodes, considering their semantic similarity, adjacency, and keyword overlap. Furthermore, we propose a depth-biased random walk over the graph to sample a backward context path for each target paragraph. The context path will be used to prompt a large language model (LLM) for translation. This framework naturally supports multi-path context sampling, which can improve robustness by aggregating diverse translation candidates for discourse-ambiguous inputs. Experiments conducted across various domains show that G^2C-MT outperforms strong baselines on multiple LLMs, including DeepSeek-V3, Gemini-2.5-Flash-lite, and the Qwen-2.5/3 series.

</details>


### [30] [Regret Pre-training: Bridging Prior and Posterior Views for Enhanced Knowledge Grounding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03080)
*Mingkuan Zhao,Xiayu Sun,Wentao Hu,Suquan Chen,Jiaxuan Li,Xiaoyan Zhu,Xin Lai,Jiayin Wang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 Regret Pre-training 的框架，通过在训练期间利用未来上下文信息（作为特权信息）来监督因果语言模型，显著提升了模型的性能，且在推理阶段无需额外计算开销。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的因果语言模型在训练时仅利用当前序列的前向上下文，完全忽略了训练数据中本身存在的未来信息，导致模型表征学习不够充分。作者试图通过引入未来上下文作为“特权信息”，在保持推理阶段因果属性的前提下，增强模型的表征学习效率。

Method: 该研究引入了基于 LUPI（利用特权信息学习）范式的 Regret Pre-training 框架。采用双视图架构：Student（仅利用前向上下文的因果模型）和 Teacher（利用未来信息的模型）。训练时引入“Regret Loss”（遗憾损失），通过最小化 Teacher 分布到 Student 分布的 KL 散度，将未来感知信号蒸馏给因果模型。实验配置包括 LocalRegret（扩展一个未来 token）和 GlobalRegret（双向上下文且掩码目标位置）。

Result: 在 OLMoE-1B-7B 架构上经过 40 亿 token 训练后，GlobalRegret 和 LocalRegret 的平均准确率分别达到 33.9% 和 32.2%，均优于基线的 30.2%。其中 GlobalRegret 在 BoolQ 任务上表现尤为突出，性能提升了 18.1 个百分点。该方法无需增加额外的推理参数。

Conclusion: Regret Pre-training 是一种有效的自监督学习框架，通过利用“特权信息”（即训练数据中可用的未来上下文），在不增加推理参数量的情况下，显著提升了因果语言模型的表征能力和下游任务性能。该方法证明了在训练过程中整合未来信息能够有效弥补单纯因果建模的局限性。

Abstract: Causal language models factorize sequence probabilities using only preceding context, leaving future information unexploited during training despite its availability in the training data. This paper introduces Regret Pre-training, a self-supervised framework grounded in the Learning Using Privileged Information (LUPI) paradigm. The framework employs a dual-view architecture in which a single model generates both a causal Student distribution and a future-conditioned Teacher distribution. The training objective augments standard language modeling with a regret loss that minimizes the KL divergence from teacher to student, transferring future-aware signals to the causal representations. We investigate two teacher configurations on the OLMoE-1B-7B architecture:LocalRegret, which extends attention by one future token, andGlobalRegret, which conditions on bidirectional context with the target position masked. Experiments on nine downstream tasks following 4 billion tokens of training demonstrate that both configurations consistently outperform the baseline. On average,GlobalRegret andLocalRegret achieve 33.9% and 32.2% accuracy respectively, surpassing the baseline's 30.2%. Most notably,GlobalRegret improves BoolQ performance by 18.1 percentage points (61.0% vs 42.9%). The framework introduces no additional parameters and requires only one extra inference-mode forward pass per training step.

</details>


### [31] [Can Factual Opinions Be Edited (Manipulated) in Large Language Models?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03096)
*Yuanpu Cao,Ziyi Yin,Fenglong Ma,Jinghui Chen*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文揭示了操纵大模型中公众人物观点所带来的安全威胁，并发布了FOE基准数据集及一种旨在保持观点-证据一致性的编辑对齐方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型知识编辑研究多关注原子事实，忽略了对公众人物事实观点（如社会立场）进行操纵的潜在安全风险及对舆论的影响；现有编辑方法在处理这类观点时往往难以保持逻辑一致性。

Method: 1. 构建了包含261位公众人物、19个议题类别和2178条观点记录的Factual Opinion Editing with Evidence (FOE)基准测试；2. 提出了“自生成证据对齐”（Self-Generated Evidence-Aligned）方法，在无需显式指令的情况下，确保模型修改后的观点与其生成的支持证据保持一致。

Result: 实验表明，现有主流编辑技术在处理事实观点时效果较差，难以保持观点与证据的逻辑一致性；而作者提出的新方法能有效实现观点与证据的对齐。

Conclusion: 本文提出了针对LLM事实观点编辑的安全评估基准与对齐方法，强调了操纵公众人物观点所带来的社会影响和安全风险，为该领域的研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into various domains, making knowledge editing techniques crucial yet potentially hazardous. Current editing methods primarily target atomic facts, overlooking the significant risks associated with manipulating factual opinions, e.g., documented stances of public figures on societal issues. Such manipulation could reshape public images, influence elections, and alter societal views. To systematically assess this threat, we introduce the Factual Opinion Editing with Evidence (FOE) benchmark, which encompasses 261 public figures, 19 issue categories, and 2,178 complete opinion records. Our evaluations demonstrate that current editing techniques struggle significantly with factual opinions, often achieving only superficial changes while failing to preserve consistency between the edited opinion and the supporting evidence generated by the model. To address this limitation, we further propose a simple yet effective Self-Generated Evidence-Aligned method that achieves opinion-evidence alignment without relying on explicit instructions. Together, our benchmark and method provide a foundation for understanding the emerging security implications of factual opinion editing in LLMs.

### [32] [PhotoCraft: Agentic Reasoning with Hierarchical Self-Evolving Memory for Deep Image Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03099)
*Kailin Lyu,Zhiqiang Yuan,Jianwei He,Qiwei Yan,Xuanbo Su,Nanxing Hu,Yang Liu,Ce Hao,Shengqian Qin,Lianyu Hu,Jinchao Zhang,Jie Zhou*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: PhotoCraft 是一种为图像检索智能体设计的无需训练的分层记忆系统，通过引入工作、情景和语义记忆，解决了大模型在多步图像推理中的上下文遗忘和逻辑断层问题，显著提升了检索精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体通常是无状态且反应式的，缺乏持久性记忆，无法处理复杂的深层图像检索任务中所需的时间、地点和事件等多步推理逻辑，导致推理过程出现偏差和经验孤岛现象。

Method: 提出了 PhotoCraft 框架，这是一种无需训练的分层记忆系统。该系统模拟人类认知机制，为多模态大模型（MLLM）引入了工作记忆（Working Memory）、情景记忆（Episodic Memory）和语义记忆（Semantic Memory），使其能在多步推理过程中动态调用这些记忆以保持逻辑一致性和知识迁移。

Result: 在 DISBench 基准测试中，PhotoCraft 在多种多模态大模型后端上均显著提升了上下文感知检索能力，性能提升最高达 18.5%，有效缓解了无记忆架构在深层图像检索中的关键瓶颈。

Conclusion: PhotoCraft 通过引入分层记忆系统，成功解决了当前多模态大模型在深层图像检索中缺乏长期记忆和上下文关联的瓶颈，为构建更可靠、更具泛化能力的智能体提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Deep Image Search requires multi-step reasoning over rich contextual cues, such as time, location, and event relations. However, most existing LLM-based agents are stateless and reactive, lacking persistent memory to maintain long-horizon context or transfer experience across tasks, which often leads to execution drift and experience isolation. To address these limitations, we propose PhotoCraft, a training-free, hierarchical memory system for photo-search agents. Inspired by human cognition, PhotoCraft equips MLLMs with working, episodic, and semantic memory, which are dynamically invoked during reasoning to preserve logical consistency and knowledge transferability throughout multi-step reasoning and answer generation. Extensive experiments on DISBench demonstrate that PhotoCraft consistently improves context-aware retrieval across diverse MLLM backbones, achieving gains of up to 18.5\% and effectively mitigating key bottlenecks in memoryless deep image search, offering a practical path toward reliable and generalizable multimodal search agents.

### [33] [Small RL Controller, Large Language Model: RL-Guided Adaptive Sampling for Test-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03102)
*Runpeng Dai,Tong Zheng,Rui Liu,Chengsong Huang,Hongtu Zhu*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于强化学习的自适应采样框架，通过轻量级控制器动态平衡大模型推理的准确性与计算开销，有效解决了现有方法依赖启发式规则的局限性，在推理成本与性能之间取得了更好的平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时缩放（test-time scaling）技术虽能提升大型语言模型的推理性能，但伴随着高昂的计算成本与延迟。现有的自适应采样方法多依赖于启发式规则或分布假设，缺乏灵活性和鲁棒性。因此，需要一种更具适应性且成本可控的方法来优化推理效率。

Method: 本文将自适应采样建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP），通过强化学习（RL）训练一个轻量级的采样控制器。该控制器基于最终答案的统计信息，在每一轮采样中动态决策是停止采样还是继续获取样本。此外，该方法通过拉格朗日松弛法，将推理目标转化为具有显式预算约束的优化问题。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法在准确性、采样轮数和总样本数之间的权衡表现上，优于ASC和ESC等强基线模型。此外，该控制器非常轻量，仅依赖最终答案的统计数据，且支持在CPU上进行训练和部署。

Conclusion: 本研究通过将自适应采样转化为马尔可夫决策过程，并利用强化学习训练轻量级采样控制器，成功在大型语言模型的推理准确性、延迟和计算成本之间实现了更优的权衡，证明了该方法在资源受限场景下的实用性与有效性。

Abstract: Test-time scaling improves the reasoning performance of large language models but incurs substantial cost in both total computation and latency. Existing adaptive sampling methods partially mitigate this issue by dynamically deciding when to stop sampling, yet they typically rely on heuristic rules or rely on distribution assumptions. In this work, we formulate adaptive sampling as a Markov decision process (MDP). We train a lightweight sampling controller with reinforcement learning (RL) to jointly balance answer correctness, latency, and computation cost. At each round, the controller decides to stop sampling or to acquire additional samples. Our method is lightweight which only relies on statistics of final answers, and can be trained and deployed on CPU. We further show that the resulting framework admits an interpretation as the Lagrangian relaxation of a constrained optimization problem with explicit budget constraints. Experiments against strong baselines such as ASC and ESC show that our method achieves improved trade-offs among answer correctness, sampling rounds, and total samples required.

### [34] [Coherence Maximization Improves Pluralistic Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03110)
*Taslim Mahbub,Yiding Pei,Shi Feng*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该论文提出利用“内部一致性最大化（ICM）”生成高质量的上下文示例，在无需大量人工监督的前提下，有效实现了AI系统与多元人类价值观的对齐，并证实了示例的“内部一致性”是提升模型泛化能力的核心要素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将AI系统与多元化的人类价值观对齐需要基于具体示例的价值规范，但如何在缺乏大规模人工监督的情况下高效生成这些高质量示例，仍是一个亟待解决的挑战。

Method: 提出了一种称为“内部一致性最大化（Internal Coherence Maximization, ICM）”的方法。该方法通过最大化标签间的相互可预测性（mutual predictability）来推断标签，从而生成特定角色的示例。此外，研究还引入了基于模型不确定性的针对性人类反馈策略，以优化对代表性不足群体的价值对齐。

Result: 在涵盖分类、偏好和开放式生成等四个基准测试中，ICM推断出的上下文示例表现与金标准标签相当。实验证明，在准确率相同的情况下，更高内部一致性的示例具有更好的泛化能力；此外，针对模型不确定性最高的问题进行反馈，比随机选择问题进行反馈能带来更优的泛化表现。

Conclusion: 一致性（Internal Coherence）是实现可扩展价值规范的关键设计原则。通过利用预训练模型中已有的多样化人类视角，该方法证明了在无需大量人工监督的情况下，通过最大化示例间的内部一致性，可以有效地对齐AI系统并实现更好的泛化效果。

Abstract: Aligning AI systems with diverse human values requires value specifications grounded in concrete examples, but generating such examples without extensive human supervision remains an open challenge. We investigate what makes these examples effective, using Internal Coherence Maximization (ICM) -- which infers labels by maximizing their mutual predictability -- to generate persona-specific examples that steer a model toward a target group's values, without human supervision. Across four benchmarks spanning classification, preference, and open-ended generation, ICM-inferred in-context examples match the performance of gold labels. Crucially, coherence matters beyond individual label accuracy: with accuracy held constant, more coherent examples generalize substantially better than incoherent ones. For personas underrepresented in pretraining data, targeted human feedback on the questions where the model is least certain about a persona's values yields better generalization than the same number of labels on arbitrary questions. These results identify coherence as a key design principle for scalable value specification, leveraging the diverse human perspectives already encoded in pretrained language models.

### [35] [DMT-CBT: Longitudinal Therapeutic State Modeling for CBT Counseling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03132)
*Chang Liu,Shuyi Zhang,Changsheng Ma,Yongfeng Tao,Minqiang Yang,Bin Hu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了DMT-CBT框架，该框架采用动态建模方式处理不断演变的治疗状态；构建了DMTCorpus数据集，支持多模态（图像）行为基础和跨会话干预连续性；模型整合了工具增强型干预和结构化状态维护，以克服单次响应生成在心理治疗中的局限。

Result: 实验表明，DMT-CBT在咨询保真度、治疗联盟构建以及长期情感轨迹引导方面均优于传统的后处理提取方法，能够更准确、持续地保持治疗状态。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) have shown growing potential for Cognitive Behavioral Therapy (CBT) counseling. However, most existing approaches still formulate counseling as a local response generation problem, focusing on empathetic replies within short, text-only, or single-session interactions. We argue that this formulation fundamentally mismatches the nature of real psychotherapy. In clinical CBT, therapy is a longitudinal process in which therapists continuously infer, update, and intervene on evolving therapeutic states across sessions. Realistic CBT further involves multimodal inference and delayed cross-session intervention effects, requiring models to capture longitudinal therapeutic state evolution under partial observability. We propose DMT-CBT, a framework for Dynamic Modeling of evolving Therapeutic states in CBT counseling. DMT-CBT maintains structured therapeutic states across sessions while incorporating multimodal behavioral grounding and tool-augmented intervention to support adaptive therapeutic reasoning. Based on this framework, we construct DMTCorpus, a synthetic multi-session multimodal CBT counseling dataset featuring evolving therapeutic states, image-grounded client behaviors, and cross-session intervention continuity. Experimental results show that DMT-CBT improves counseling fidelity and therapeutic alliance, produces more favorable longitudinal affective trajectories, and preserves therapeutic states more faithfully than post-hoc extraction approaches.

Conclusion: 该研究发布了一个大规模、版本化的热带物种跨领域数据集，为生物多样性管理、商业贸易及监管提供了统一的标准化资源。通过构建跨领域本体和完善中文命名层，该数据集显著提升了物种数据在多学科背景下的可互操作性和应用价值，并为未来的数据描述论文和生态科研奠定了基础。

Abstract: We describe a versioned cross-domain dataset of 410,499 active tropical species (working snapshot 2026-04-20) spanning three applied subdomains -- tropical_plants, tropical_aquatic, and tropical_pets -- that share a commercial and regulatory life cycle but are distributed across kingdom-organised biodiversity infrastructures. The resource joins taxonomic identifiers from GBIF, Plants of the World Online, iNaturalist, NCBI Taxonomy, the Catalogue of Life and the Encyclopedia of Life, and adds three original layers: a cross-domain ontology that re-segments taxa along trade and husbandry contexts; a Chinese vernacular layer with explicit per-name provenance under a typology that excludes unverified machine-generated proposals; and a CITES source-linkage layer connecting each taxon to its Species+ entry. Chinese vernacular coverage -- the proportion of taxa carrying a CJK Chinese name distinct from the scientific binomial -- reaches 99.50 percent (408,456 of 410,499; full-population count). Coverage characterises completeness, not name-translation accuracy; the latter is bounded by the four-level provenance typology and is the subject of a preliminary internal review reported here, with a blind external audit identified as the principal open item. Upstream content is referenced by stable identifier only for the original-contribution layers, supporting CC-BY 4.0 reuse. The dataset is deposited on Zenodo (10.5281/zenodo.20377811). This preprint is the canonical v1.0 description of the dataset's current state; future Data Descriptor submission is anticipated but is contingent on the validation and release-engineering items listed in the Limitations.

### [37] [Fully Automated Identification of Lexical Alignment and Preference-Stage Shifts in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03165)
*Thomas Stephan Juzek,Xiaoyang Ming,Jose A. Hernandez*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无需人工干预的自动化评估框架，通过词汇对齐分数和三角偏好偏移两个指标，系统性地量化并分析了大模型在人类偏好学习阶段产生的语言使用偏差，为提升模型对齐效果提供了新路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字聊天助手（如ChatGPT）生成的语言常偏离人类预期（即对齐失效/错位）。尽管已有研究揭示了此类偏差及其与人类偏好学习（RLHF等）的关联，但现有的研究方法高度依赖人工整理，难以大规模扩展。因此，需要开发无需人工干预的自动化评估框架来系统研究这一现象。

Method: 提出了两种无需人工干预、假设较少的评估指标：1. 词汇对齐分数 (Lexical Alignment Score)，用于识别词汇过度使用情况；2. 三角偏好偏移 (Triangulated Preference Shift)，用于量化词汇偏移与人类偏好学习之间的关联。作者基于PubMed摘要数据，在六个模型家族（Falcon, Gemma, Llama, Mistral, OLMo, Yi）上进行了实证研究。

Result: 实验成功识别出如“suggest”、“additionally”、“strategy”等被模型过度使用的词汇，并定量估计了它们与人类偏好学习之间的联系。研究结果在不同参数设置、随机种子及数据集下表现出高度稳定性，验证了该方法的有效性和可靠性。

Conclusion: 本文提出的自动化、免人工干预的评估指标能有效识别大模型在人类偏好学习阶段产生的词汇对齐偏差。该方法具有良好的可扩展性和跨模型适用性，为未来模型对齐研究及理解偏好学习的本质提供了重要工具。

Abstract: The language used by digital chat assistants such as ChatGPT can diverge from human expectations (misalignment). Research, mostly on Scientific English, has described both what divergences occur and, to some extent, why, linking them to the training stage of human preference learning. Yet, existing approaches rely on manual curation. This paper introduces two curation-free, assumption-light evaluation metrics: the Lexical Alignment Score, which identifies lexical overuse, and the Triangulated Preference Shift, which quantifies how much of such shifts can be attributed to human preference learning. Using PubMed abstracts, continuations were generated and measured using windowed document prevalence across six model families (Falcon, Gemma, Llama, Mistral, OLMo, Yi). The procedure identifies, without manual intervention, overused items such as 'suggest', 'additionally', and 'strategy', and estimates their link to preference learning. Our findings replicate prior work and remain stable across parameter settings, random seeds, and evaluation on further data. The approach scales readily and enables systematic study of lexical (mis)alignment beyond Scientific English and across languages, and as such, the metrics have the potential to contribute to improved alignment for future models and understanding of its origins.
