### [77] [AI Rater Discrimination Depends on Scoring Protocol in Complex Clinical Decision-Making](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03198)
*Sangwon Baek,Kyu Yeon Hur,Kyunga Kim*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 该研究定量分析了利用大语言模型评估临床AI系统的有效性，指出使用基于具体标准（Rubric）的评分协议比无标准评分更能准确区分临床决策的质量，且能更好地体现模型间的行为差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管临床人工智能（AI）评估越来越依赖大语言模型（LLM）作为评估者，但目前缺乏对LLM在不同评估条件下评分行为的定量特征描述，特别是在涉及复杂决策的临床任务中。本研究旨在填补这一空白，明确不同评分协议对评估质量的影响。

Method: 本研究采用因子设计法，以成人2型糖尿病（T2D）药物治疗随访作为临床评估任务。研究选取了四种开源大模型（LLM）同时扮演临床决策支持系统（CDSS）和评分者（AI Rater）。研究对比了两种评分协议：基于标准的评分协议（GR，包含患者特异性准则）和无标准的评分协议（Non-GR）。通过线性混合效应模型，评估了CDSS模型、提示词配置、评分者模型等五种设计因素对评分结果的影响及交互作用。

Result: 研究发现，在Non-GR协议下，AI评分普遍偏高且波动范围极窄（74-78分）；而在GR协议下，评分显著降低（低7.69至49.64分）且离散度更高。GR协议将AI评分在不同CDSS输出之间的区分度提高了1.76至5.10倍，并揭示了Non-GR所掩盖的模型间行为差异。

Conclusion: 基于评价标准的评分协议（GR）在临床AI评估中至关重要，它能有效提高评估的区分度并揭示模型间的行为差异。无标准的评分协议（Non-GR）无法胜任需要患者特异性或特定临床准则的评估任务，不应作为评价临床决策支持系统的替代方案。

Abstract: Clinical AI evaluation increasingly delegates scoring to large language models (LLMs) acting as AI raters, yet their scoring behavior across evaluation conditions has not been quantitatively characterized. We address this gap through a factorial study of AI rater behavior in adult type 2 diabetes (T2D) pharmacotherapy at 12-month outpatient follow-up, a clinical task involving complex decision-making operationalized across seven evaluation questions. Four open-source LLMs served simultaneously as clinical decision support system (CDSS) models and AI raters. Each CDSS output was scored under two scoring protocols: a rubric-anchored Gold Rubric (GR) protocol incorporating a patient-specific rubric, and a rubric-free Non Gold Rubric (Non-GR) protocol. Linear mixed effects models crossed the scoring protocol factor with five design factors -- CDSS model, CDSS prompt configuration (document-referenced generation [DRG] vs.\ Baseline), rater model, prompt character, and prompt type -- and estimated main effects together with their protocol interactions. Across all questions, AI raters yielded consistently higher scores within a very narrow range (74--78 points on average) under Non-GR compared to those under GR (7.69 to 49.64 points lower mean scores; 1.68 to 3.67 times wider interquartile ranges). Within each question, GR amplified the AI rater's discrimination between DRG and Baseline CDSS outputs by factors of 1.76 to 5.10, while also revealing substantial behavioral variation across rater models that Non-GR suppressed. These findings support rubric anchoring as the scoring protocol that preserves discriminative power in clinical AI evaluation; rubric-free scoring cannot substitute when questions require patient-specific or jurisdiction-specific criteria that rater models cannot infer from parametric knowledge alone.

</details>


### [78] [WebRISE: Requirement-Induced State Evaluation for MLLM-Generated Web Artifacts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03220)
*Yuxin Meng,Yuhan Suo,Junjie Wang,Yuhan Sun,Yiyao Yu,Ruixu Zhang,Ruining Hu,Yubin Wang,Shouwei Ruan,Bin Wang,Yuxiang Zhang,Yujiu Yang*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: WebRISE是一个新的网页生成模型基准，通过交互契约图（ICG）量化模型在交互状态转换和需求满足方面的能力，揭示了当前MLLM即便视觉表现良好，其交互逻辑与功能正确性依然存在严重不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态大模型（MLLM）网页生成基准测试主要关注局部视觉证据，忽略了网页正常运行所必需的需求驱动状态转换和隐含的产品级约束，导致评估结果无法准确反映模型的交互能力。

Method: 提出了WebRISE基准测试框架，通过将任务需求编译为“交互契约图”（ICG），包含可观测状态、用户意图转换及DOM/视觉断言，实现对网页生成任务的实施不可知浏览器执行评估。该框架涵盖442个任务及五种输入模态，并引入了基于ICG的得分机制以检测状态错误。

Result: 对14种MLLM的测试显示，性能最强的模型在转换有效性（65.6%）和需求覆盖率（66.3%）方面仍有较大提升空间；视频输入在提升交互信号方面表现最佳；基于ICG的评分系统在发现状态错误方面的效率比传统检查点评估方式高出2至16倍。

Conclusion: WebRISE证明了视觉质量与功能正确性之间存在显著脱节，单纯依赖基于视觉的评估指标不足以衡量MLLM的网页生成能力。交互契约图（ICG）提供了一种更严谨的评估框架，能够有效识别现有模型在遵循复杂交互逻辑和隐含产品约束方面的重大缺陷。

Abstract: Existing benchmarks for MLLM-generated web artifacts assess interaction through local evidence and miss the requirement-induced states and transitions that determine whether a page works. We introduce WebRISE, which compiles task requirements into Interaction Contract Graphs (ICGs) of observable states, user-intent transitions, and DOM/visual assertions for implementation-agnostic browser execution. WebRISE spans 442 tasks across five input modalities (Text, Markdown, Sketch, Image, Video), with 5,495 transitions and 5,271 requirement checks that separate user-stated functions from implicit product-level constraints. Across 14 MLLMs, even the strongest model reaches only 65.6% transition validity and 66.3% requirement coverage, and visual quality is no proxy for behavior (Qwen3.6-35B-A3B on Markdown: V=80.8 yet T=15.5). Video gives the strongest interaction signal (+10.6 pp implicit coverage over Text), while implicit constraints persist; defect injection shows ICG-based scoring detects state errors at 2-16x the rate of checkpoint-style evaluation.

</details>


### [79] [Safety Measurements for Fine-tuned LLMs Should be Grounded in Capability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03648)
*Krishnapriya Vishnubhotla,Hillary Dawkins,Isar Nejadgholi,Svetlana Kiritchenko*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文指出大模型微调会导致安全性受损及输出连贯性问题，且现有的自动化安全评估手段在面对微调模型时存在不可靠性，强调了建立标准化、目标导向的微调安全评估框架的必要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对于微调如何影响大模型安全性缺乏系统性实验，往往基于随机设置，导致结论缺乏普适性和可比性。本文旨在通过将微调锚定在特定的能力目标上，更严谨地探讨微调对模型安全性及其行为产生的深层影响。

Method: 本文采取了多维度的评估方法，将微调过程锚定在特定的能力目标上，而非随机实验。研究团队对比分析了微调对模型能力与安全性的双重影响，并重点探讨了不同安全基准和安全评估器对实验结论的影响差异。

Result: 研究发现：1. 微调后的模型在处理安全相关提示时可能输出语义不连贯的内容；2. 现有的自动化安全评估机制在面对此类混乱输出时表现不可靠；3. 实验结论会随安全基准和评估器的不同而发生显著变化。

Conclusion: 研究表明，微调不仅会损害大模型的安全性，还可能导致模型在处理安全提示时产生逻辑混乱。此外，评估结果受限于安全基准选择和评估器偏差，因此在评估微调影响时必须建立基于特定能力目标的标准化框架，并对评估方法的可靠性进行审慎考量。

Abstract: Adapting foundation large language models to a user's task or preferred style through fine-tuning can result in compromising the model's safety. Previous works examined the effects of fine-tuning on model safety in limited and seemingly random experimental settings. We argue that anchoring fine-tuning to a specific capability goal is essential for avoiding arbitrary empirical choices, allowing us to draw meaningful conclusions about safety impacts, and to compare mitigation methods on a consistent basis. We conduct a multi-dimensional evaluation of the effects of fine-tuning on model behavior by focusing on capability as well as safety. Our results surface important issues that (1) fine-tuned models can produce incoherent generations in response to safety prompts, (2) automated safety judgments are unreliable for such incoherent outputs, and (3) the conclusions about the effects of fine-tuning can change depending on the choice of safety benchmark as well as the safety evaluator.

</details>


### [80] [CoEval: Ranking Language Models for Custom Tasks Without Labeled Data or Trustworthy Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03650)
*Alexander Apartsin,Yehudit Aperstein*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: CoEval 是一种无需人工标签的自动化大模型评测框架，通过动态生成全新的测试数据并利用多元化的评审团进行打分，彻底解决了数据污染和评估成本高昂的问题，实现了对特定领域模型能力的精确、廉价且可复用的评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的公共基准测试存在严重的数据泄露（预训练污染）问题，导致模型评分仅反映了对测试集的记忆而非实际能力；同时，缺乏特定应用领域的标签数据使得模型评估难以开展，现有的评估方式往往依赖昂贵且难以扩展的人工标注。

Method: 1. 任务驱动的数据合成：利用教师模型根据任务描述自动生成无人工标注、无污染的全新测试集。
2. 跨模型家族集成评审：构建由不同厂商模型组成的评审团（Panel），对候选模型的输出进行评分，通过多元化的评审组合抵消单一模型的偏见。
3. 动态验证机制：通过控制评审团构成（关注供应商多样性而非数量）来提升评估的可信度，并验证了其在无标注情况下的准确性（与真实标签的相关性 ho=0.86）。

Result: 1. CoEval 能准确还原真实模型排名，其评估结果与真实标签的相关系数达到 0.86。
2. 测试集与现有主流基准测试几乎无重复（0% 的 13-gram 重复率），完全规避了数据污染。
3. 具有极高的经济性，在四个任务的实验中，生成近 8000 次评估仅花费 5.89 美元。
4. 有效消除了单一评审模型的偏见和“同家族偏好”问题。

Conclusion: CoEval 提供了一种低成本、可复用且高度自动化的模型评估方案，通过动态生成无污染的测试集和跨模型家族的集成评审，有效解决了现有大模型评测中数据污染和人工标注依赖的问题，为特定应用场景下的模型选择提供了可靠的量化依据。

Abstract: Choosing or ranking language models for a specific application is hardest when no task-specific labeled data exists, and standard public benchmarks cannot be trusted, their items having likely leaked into pretraining, so scores reflect memorization rather than fitness. We present CoEval, an open-source, reusable framework that closes this gap end to end: from only a description of a task or domain, teacher models synthesize a fresh, attribute-controlled benchmark with no human labels, contamination-free because items are generated anew on each run, and a cross-family judge ensemble ranks candidate models with no human raters. Validated where ground truth exists, CoEval recovers the true model ranking and tracks ground-truth correctness at ho=0.86. The label-free judging needs no human calibration because judge-panel composition (vendor diversity), not size, drives reliability: a small, well-chosen cross-family panel is most reliable, while a single judge can be anti-correlated with ground truth (judge-choice regret 0.35) and the ensemble never is. Generated items show zero verbatim 13-gram overlap with five major public benchmarks; the panel cancels verbosity bias and precludes same-family self-preference. A four-task study produced 7,978 evaluations for USD 5.89. The same declarative pipeline applies to any domain and is cheap enough to re-run on every model release: a label-free, contamination-free leaderboard any team can regenerate for its own application.

</details>


### [81] [Expert-Aware Causal Tracing of Factual Recall in Sparse MoE Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03780)
*Yuetian Lu,Ali Modarressi,Yihong Liu,Hinrich Schütze*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种针对稀疏混合专家（MoE）模型的事实追踪方法，揭示了模型处理事实知识的机制存在模型特异性：有些模型通过单一专家处理事实，而另一些模型则依赖专家联合作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的因果追踪研究主要集中在稠密Transformer模型上，而稀疏混合专家（MoE）模型具有独特的路由机制。研究者旨在探究当事实预测由特定专家处理时，如何精确识别出真正贡献于该预测的专家，以深化对MoE模型内部知识存储机制的理解。

Method: 提出了一种“专家感知因果追踪”（expert-aware causal tracing）方法。具体步骤包括：首先对受试模型的“主语词嵌入”添加噪声以破坏其事实预测能力，随后通过在受损模型中注入“干净”的MoE块输出或特定的“专家级更新”，测试模型恢复对事实预测准确性的能力，以此定位关键的专家及其贡献。

Result: 通过在Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base模型上的测试，成功定位了单一关键专家；而在Mixtral-8x7B-v0.1模型上，研究发现事实信息并非局限于单一专家，而是分布在多个专家的协作输出中。这表明MoE的知识定位机制在不同模型间表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“专家感知”因果追踪在稀疏混合专家（MoE）模型中是可行的。然而，专家层面的定位能力并非普遍存在，而是高度依赖于具体的模型架构、训练方式及任务协议。在某些模型中，事实性知识可能分散在多个专家的协作中，而非单一专家。

Abstract: Causal tracing of factual recall has been studied predominantly in dense transformer language models, where interventions localize information flow to layers or feed-forward modules. Sparse mixture-of-experts (MoE) language models introduce a sharper question: when a factual prediction is mediated by a routed MoE block, which routed expert contributions matter? We formulate expert-aware causal tracing for sparse MoE language models. Using CounterFact facts, we first corrupt the model's factual preference by adding noise to subject-token embeddings, and then test whether clean MoE-block outputs or clean expert-level updates restore the true-vs-foil logit contrast. For Qwen3-30B-A3B-Base, a layer sweep selects and validates layer 44, and expert-level tracing identifies L44E069 as an expert repeatedly selected in the clean run whose held-out patch outperforms other active same-layer expert patches. For Mixtral-8x7B-v0.1, layer-level tracing validates a mid-layer signal, but the signal is not localized to the selected singleton expert; a coalition check instead recovers it with routed multi-expert updates. These results suggest that MoE factual tracing can be made expert-aware, while also showing that expert-level localization is model- and protocol-dependent rather than universal.

</details>

### [82] [Human-in-the-Loop Contextual Bandits for Short-Term Rental Dynamic Pricing: Structural Equivalence of Historical Warm-Up and Approval-Gated Live Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02595)
*Oleg Miroshnichenko*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种“人在回路门控强盗”（HITL-GB）框架，通过将人类审核员的介入作为统计预热的资产，成功解决了短期租赁市场动态定价中在线学习算法面临的冷启动慢、财务风险高和反馈稀疏的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短期租赁市场（STR）的动态定价面临巨大财务风险，且市场反馈稀疏（单晚反馈），传统在线学习算法难以直接应用。此外，操作员需要定价方案具备可解释性。因此，需要一种能够利用历史数据、支持人工干预并能快速适应市场变化的定价框架。

Method: 提出了“人在回路门控强盗”（HITL-GB）框架，通过将上下文强盗算法生成的定价建议交给人类操作员审核，利用历史确定性策略产生的定价数据，将其转化为算法的“策略内”（on-policy）预热数据。并采用正则化岭回归程序来初始化强盗算法的后验分布，有效缓解冷启动问题。

Result: 在真实STR生产数据上的实验表明，该方法将HF-TS算法的有效冷启动周期从约150个周期缩短至约30个周期。该方法论证了强制性人工干预与统计预热之间的结构等价性，适用于医疗、信贷等多个受监管的高风险领域。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，在需要人工审批的决策场景中，强制性的人工监督不仅是操作上的约束，更是一种统计资产。通过利用历史数据进行热启动，可以显著缩短强化学习算法在稀疏反馈市场中的冷启动周期，使其在实际应用中更具可行性和安全性。

Abstract: Dynamic pricing in short-term rental (STR) markets presents a distinctive challenge for online learning algorithms: pricing decisions carry significant financial risk, operators require explainability, and market feedback is sparse (one booking outcome per listed night). We introduce the Human-in-the-Loop Gated Bandit (HITL-GB) framework, in which a contextual bandit algorithm generates price recommendations but a human agent retains authority to accept, modify, or reject each recommendation before it is applied. We show that under this approval constraint, historical pricing data -- collected under a prior deterministic policy -- is structurally equivalent to on-policy warm-up data for initialising the bandit's posterior, bypassing the weeks-to-months cold-start period that renders pure online bandit learning impractical in sparse-feedback markets. We formalise the approval-gated reward signal, derive a regularised ridge-regression warm-up procedure from historical episodes, and validate the approach on real STR production data (anonymised urban market, 2 rooms, April 2022 -- April 2026, 1,461 nightly pricing episodes). Our warm-up procedure compresses effective cold-start from ~150 episodes to ~30 episodes when initialising agents from the Hierarchical Factored Thompson Sampling (HF-TS) family. We further argue that the structural equivalence result is domain-agnostic: any high-stakes domain where human approval is legally or operationally required -- including clinical drug dosing, credit origination, content moderation, and radiological diagnosis -- satisfies the same conditions and benefits from the same warm-up strategy. In regulated industries, mandatory human oversight is thus a statistical asset rather than a deployment constraint.

</details>


### [83] [Spectral Asymptotics of Neural Network Loss Landscapes: An Exact Decomposition of the Curvature Exponent](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02596)
*Anherutowa Calvo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了神经网络层中曲率指数α与梯度奇异值之间的深层几何联系，通过谱对齐分解和谱传递恒等式成功预测了不同架构下的Hessian行为，并据此提出一种优于AdamW的新型自适应预处理优化算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 神经网络中Hessian特征值与梯度奇异值之间的缩放关系（曲率指数α）在不同层类型（如卷积层、Transformer注意力层、MLP层）间存在显著差异。现有研究缺乏对这种变异性的深层几何解释，因此亟需从理论上揭示曲率指数α的成因及其对优化过程的影响。

Method: 1. 提出了谱对齐分解（Spectral Alignment Decomposition）公式：α = 2 + dlogΦ_k / dlogσ_k，将曲率指数与梯度奇异向量间的对齐度联系起来；2. 导出了谱传递恒等式 s = αγ，将曲率、梯度秩衰减和Hessian衰减联系在一起；3. 应用zeta函数界限分析曲率的集中特性；4. 设计并实现了基于架构自适应的预处理器——谱牛顿法（Spectral Newton）。

Result: 1. 证明了曲率指数α的变化由梯度与Kronecker因子特征基之间的对齐度决定；2. 谱传递恒等式在93个层、5种架构及3个数据集上实现了约2%的预测误差；3. 发现曲率主要集中在每一层的单一方向上；4. 谱牛顿法在α≈2的任务（如视觉基准）中展现出优于AdamW的训练性能。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提出的谱对齐分解（Spectral Alignment Decomposition）成功量化了Hessian谱与梯度奇异值之间的结构性关系，验证了该理论在多种架构中的普适性，并利用导出的自适应预处理器“谱牛顿法”在特定任务中超越了传统优化器，为理解神经网络的损失景观几何提供了基础理论支持。

Abstract: The curvature exponent $α$ in $h_k \propto σ_k^α$ -- governing how Hessian eigenvalues scale with gradient singular values -- varies systematically across layer types ($α\approx 2$ for convolutions, $\approx 1$ for transformer attention, $< 1$ for MLP up-projections). Why? We prove the Spectral Alignment Decomposition: $α= 2 + d\logΦ_k / d\logσ_k$, where $Φ_k$ measures alignment between Kronecker factor eigenbases and gradient singular directions. This reduces "why does $α$ vary?" to a geometric question we answer for LayerNorm, residual connections, and softmax heads. The decomposition implies a spectral transfer identity $s = αγ$ linking curvature exponent, effective gradient rank-decay $γ$, and Hessian decay exponent $s$. The identity is algebraic; its empirical content is that $α$ and $γ$, fit on independent data (HVPs vs. SVD), recover $s$ to ~2% median error across 93 layers, five architectures, and three datasets -- with no free parameters. A zeta-function bound on participation ratio shows curvature concentrates onto effectively one direction per layer. As a proof of concept, we derive the architecture-adaptive preconditioner $T(σ;α)$ and show that Spectral Newton -- implementing $T$ in the gradient singular basis -- outperforms AdamW on vision benchmarks where $α\approx 2$.

</details>


### [84] [Making Brain-Computer Interfaces More Secure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02597)
*Md Fahimul Kabir Chowdhury,Gahangir Hossain*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对脑机接口系统易受对抗攻击影响的问题，本文提出了一种轻量化卷积神经网络架构，实验证实其在对抗性环境下展现出比现有经典模型更强的鲁棒性与分类表现，增强了脑机接口的实际应用安全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前脑机接口（BCI）研究多关注分类准确率，但忽视了系统的安全性与鲁棒性。研究发现基于 EEG 的 BCI 系统极易受到细微对抗攻击的干扰，从而导致错误诊断。因此，亟需评估并提升 BCI 模型在对抗环境下的稳健性，以确保其在临床及实际场景中的可靠部署。

Method: 研究提出了一种轻量化的自定义卷积神经网络（CNN）架构，并将其与 EEGNet、DeepConvNet 和 SleepEEGNet 三种专为 EEG 设计的经典模型进行对比。评估过程采用梯度驱动的对抗攻击场景，并在两个公开的 EEG 数据集上测试了各模型在对抗扰动下的鲁棒性表现。

Result: 实验结果表明，该研究提出的轻量化 CNN 模型在面临对抗性扰动时，其分类性能表现始终优于对比的基准模型。这证明了所提架构在复杂攻击环境下具备更强的鲁棒性，能够有效提升脑机接口系统的整体可靠性。

Conclusion: 轻量化卷积神经网络架构在提高脑机接口系统对抗鲁棒性方面具有显著优势，通过精简模型结构，可以在保持分类性能的同时有效抵御针对性对抗攻击，为实际应用中脑机接口的安全部署提供了可行路径。

Abstract: The development of brain-computer interfaces (BCIs) based on electroencephalograms (EEGs) has advanced significantly mainly to machine learning. Although the majority of earlier research has been on increasing classification accuracy, relatively little focus has been placed on security and robustness. According to recent research, EEG-based BCIs are susceptible to adversarial attacks, which can cause misdiagnosis due to minute, well-crafted disturbances. Evaluating model robustness against such perturbations is therefore critical for ensuring reliable deployment. In this study, we propose a lightweight custom Convolutional Neural Network (CNN) architecture to investigate adversarial robustness in EEG-based BCIs. The suggested method is assessed using two EEG datasets and contrasted with three novel CNN models tailored to EEG, namely EEGNet, DeepConvNet, and SleepEEGNet, under gradient-based adversarial attack scenarios. According to experimental findings, the suggested model continuously performs better in classification under adversarial perturbations compared to baseline models, indicating improved robustness. These findings highlight the potential of lightweight architectures for enhancing the reliability of EEG-based BCI systems under adversarial conditions.

### [85] [Assessing Region-Level EEG Contributions to Cognitive Workload Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02598)

This paper presents a region-level evaluation framework for EEG-based workload prediction in which models are trained and evaluated using features extracted exclusively from electrodes belonging to anatomically defined scalp regions. We perform a large-scale analysis across four publicly available EEG workload datasets spanning diverse task demands, recording hardware, and electrode montages. Region importance is quantified using a model-agnostic, performance-based approach under both mixed-subject and subject-independent evaluation protocols, with results aggregated using a rank-based strategy to ensure robustness across experimental configurations. Across all datasets and subject-independent evaluations, frontal electrode groups outperform the full-scalp baseline by approximately 15-20% in relative rank position while using substantially fewer electrodes. Fronto-central regions exhibit the most stable predictive utility, whereas posterior and occipital regions contribute less consistently across experimental conditions. These findings indicate that workload-relevant EEG information is most consistently retained within frontal and fronto-central electrode groups, supporting the design of efficient and generalizable EEG-based workload monitoring systems.

### [86] [Testing the Test: Score-Direction Instability in Class-Split Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02601)
*Alejandro Ascarate,Leo Lebrat,Rodrigo Santa Cruz,Clinton Fookes,Olivier Salvado*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究指出当前主流的“类分割”异常检测评估方法存在逻辑漏洞：当异常类别与正常分布在特征空间发生重叠时，模型表现会失效。作者提出了“邻域类泄露”诊断工具，建议学术界将此类基准测试视为几何压力测试，而非模型通用能力的度量标准。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前学术界广泛使用“数据集内类分割（within-dataset class-split）”评估方案作为无监督异常检测的代理指标。然而，作者指出当被留出的异常类与正常数据分布在表征空间存在重叠时，该协议会导致评估失效，甚至出现异常分数倒置或坍缩现象，使得评估结果丧失客观性。

Method: 作者引入了一种名为“邻域类泄露（neighborhood class leakage）”的无需训练（training-free）的诊断指标，通过量化表征空间内的类重叠情况，分析其对异常检测分数方向不稳定性的预测能力。研究在Fashion-MNIST、CIFAR-10和Imagenette数据集上，对比了像素空间和VAE潜空间的表现。

Result: 实验证明，邻域类泄露指标能够有效预测分数方向的不稳定性。在多种数据集和表征空间下的实验结果均显示，当类重叠严重时，基于类分割的异常检测性能会显著波动，证明了该协议在特定几何布局下存在严重的评估偏差。

Conclusion: 本文的研究表明，基于类分割的异常检测评估协议存在局限性，在异常类与正常类在表征空间存在重叠时，评估结果会变得不可靠。研究强调这类基准测试应被视为一种依赖于几何分布的“压力测试”，而非衡量模型通用异常检测能力的绝对指标。

Abstract: Within-dataset class-split evaluation is widely used as a proxy for fully unconditional out-of-distribution anomaly detection. We show that this protocol can become ill-posed when the held-out anomaly class overlaps the normal mixture in representation space. In this regime, anomaly scores may collapse toward chance or even invert, and the preferred score direction can depend on the unknown anomaly class. We introduce a simple training-free diagnostic, neighborhood class leakage, and show that it predicts score-direction instability across Fashion-MNIST, CIFAR-10, and Imagenette, in both pixel and VAE latent spaces. Our results suggest that class-split AD benchmarks should be treated as geometry-dependent stress tests rather than unconditional evidence of anomaly-detection ability.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In computational pathology, Whole Slide Images (WSIs) survival analysis is crucial for patient prognosis assessment, but it faces multiple technical challenges. Although the Transformer captures long-range dependencies through its self-attention mechanism, its $O(N^2)$ time complexity causes a severe computational bottleneck in large-scale WSIs graph structures. The Mamba model breaks through the Transformer's computational bottleneck with linear complexity. But, owing to Mamba's high sensitivity to the order of input data, traditional node sorting methods in Graph Mamba, such as those based on node degree or subgraph size, fail to adequately account for the topological connectivity of graph data. This inadequacy consequently restricts the performance of Mamba's sequential modeling. Moreover, its unidirectional architecture cannot leverage the bidirectional spatial structure of images. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel Graph Mamba survival analysis framework based on topology-aware ordering (TopoMamSurv) to adapt to the sequential sensitivity of Mamba. Our visualization experiments further confirmed that the nodes extracted through the topology-aware ordering (TAO) strategy indeed exhibit higher similarity. Furthermore, we designed a bidirectional Mamba module and integrated a Graph Convolutional Network (GCN) to achieve bidirectional spatial context modeling of images, forming a hierarchical feature learning architecture for "local aggregation - global capture." This framework effectively reconciles the contradiction between long-range dependency modeling, computational efficiency, and spatial structure utilization in WSIs analysis through its systematic design of TAO, bidirectional semantic modeling, and hierarchical feature fusion. This framework has been validated for its comprehensive performance advantage on five TCGA datasets.

### [90] [ReLoRA: Knowledge-Reusing Adaptation for Fast Rollout of Evolving LLM Services](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02606)
*Yang Xu,Zihuai Xu,Hongli Xu,Yunming Liao,Zhiwei Yao,Xitong Fu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对 LLM 更新导致 LoRA 适配器失效的问题，ReLoRA 通过知识重用、自适应初始化和计划正则化微调，实现了低开销、高性能的快速适配器恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型（LLM）的频繁更新，现有的 LoRA 适配器往往会失效。若为每次模型更新都重新训练适配器，计算开销巨大；若直接复用旧适配器，则会导致性能下降。因此，亟需一种能够高效恢复适配器服务能力并保持性能的方法。

Method: 该论文提出了 ReLoRA 框架，包含两个核心步骤：1) 自适应 LoRA 初始化：利用贝叶斯优化，通过融合旧适配器和新基模型的信息构建兼容的初始化点；2) 带有计划正则化的微调：通过先强后弱的正则化策略，快速引导适配器进入高质量区域并进行针对性的微调。

Result: 实验结果表明，与基线方法相比，ReLoRA 可将重新适配的准备时间缩短至原来的 1/8.9，同时在特定任务上的准确率最高提升了 4.6%。

Conclusion: ReLoRA 是一种高效的知识重用框架，能够解决大语言模型更新时 LoRA 适配器失效的问题，显著降低了重新适配的计算成本并提升了任务性能，对于持续演进的 LLM 服务具有重要实践意义。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed as continuously evolving services, where frequent base-model updates may invalidate previously deployed task-specific Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) adapters. For service providers managing numerous downstream model services, retraining each LoRA adapter from scratch for every updated base model is computationally prohibitive and delays service rollout. Meanwhile, the simpler alternative, i.e., naively applying the original LoRA adapter to the updated base model, often leads to degraded service quality due to adapter-backbone incompatibility. To address this problem, we propose ReLoRA, a knowledge-reusing re-adaptation framework that efficiently restores service-ready LoRA adapters for evolving LLM services while preserving or improving task performance. Specifically, ReLoRA comprises two key optimization steps: 1) Adaptive LoRA initialization leverages Bayesian optimization to construct a compatibility-aware starting point by fusing information from both the previously deployed task adapter and the base model's evolution; 2) Fine-tuning with scheduled regularization first rapidly steers the adapter to a high-quality region via strong regularization, followed by relaxed regularization for task-specific refinement. This design enables rapid service-quality recovery with reduced re-adaptation overhead. Extensive experiments demonstrate that ReLoRA reduces time-to-readiness by up to 8.9$\times$ and improves accuracy by up to 4.6\% compared to baselines.

### [91] [Geometry-Aware Tabular Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02607)
*David Turtora Zagardo*

TL;DR: GATD通过引入成对的角度和长度信息作为显式约束，增强了表格扩散模型捕捉列间关系的能力，在大幅减少参数量的同时显著提升了生成数据的质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种几何感知表格扩散模型（GATD），该方法通过计算列值差异产生的成对角度和长度作为扩散去噪器的额外输入和辅助目标，引入了对表格数据的几何关系感知。

Conclusion: 显式的关系监督（Pairwise relationships）是一种有效的、可移植的归纳偏置，能够显著提升表格扩散模型的生成质量和参数效率。

Abstract: Tabular synthesis is critical for privacy-preserving sharing and augmentation, yet diffusion models rely on implicit mechanisms to capture inter-column relationships. We introduce Geometry-Aware Tabular Diffusion (GATD), which augments tabular diffusion denoisers with pairwise angles and lengths computed from column value differences and used as inputs and auxiliary targets. Our MLP instantiation achieves state-of-the-art benchmark performance while using 3.5x fewer parameters on average (up to 25x for classification tasks): on ten datasets, it wins 8/10 Shape, 7/10 Trend, and 9/10 downstream utility (F1/RMSE), reducing Shape and Trend error by 27% and 20%. Default loss weights transfer to GNN and Transformer denoisers, improving Shape on 27/30 and Trend on 25/30 architecture-dataset cells. A matched ablation shows supervision (not extra inputs or capacity) drives the gain. This shows explicit relational supervision is a portable inductive bias for tabular diffusion.

### [92] [Pruning Deep Neural Networks via the Marchenko--Pastur Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02608)
*Leonid Berlyand,Theo Bourdais,Houman Owhad,Yitzchak Shmalo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用Marchenko--Pastur随机矩阵定律进行深度神经网络剪枝的新方法，通过理论计算确定最佳剪枝层级，实现了在几乎无需额外训练的情况下，高效保留模型精度并大幅提升硬件推理速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度神经网络剪枝方法通常需要漫长的微调或重新训练过程才能恢复精度，这在计算资源受限或时间敏感的场景下不可行。本文旨在寻找一种能够以极低微调预算实现高精度保持的剪枝策略，并从随机矩阵理论角度为剪枝的有效性提供数学支撑。

Method: 提出了一种基于Marchenko--Pastur (MP) 随机矩阵理论的剪枝方法。该方法利用MP谱分布的边界（σ+）作为确定层级剪枝预算的信号，并推导出确定性的数据路径证书（deterministic data-path certificates）。通过结合弹性网（elastic-net）正则化目标函数，在无需长时间微调的情况下，即可在维持样本判别边界的同时实现高效剪枝。此外，还引入了“剪枝-恢复”（prune--restore）模型以及针对卷积层和Vision Transformer架构的重排列（permutation）优化技术。

Result: 实验表明，该方法在极短的校准和微调周期（如ImageNet上仅需3个蒸馏轮次）内取得了优异性能。在ViT-B/16上实现了约60%的MAC计算量缩减且仅损失1.70%的Top-1准确率，并在特定硬件（A40/A100）上获得了显著的推理加速。在多种架构（ViT、ConvNeXtV2、ResNet）上均验证了其在结构化稀疏性下的鲁棒性，准确率下降极小（部分模型仅下降约0.3%）。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于Marchenko--Pastur定律的随机矩阵理论可以为深度神经网络的结构化剪枝提供高效的理论指导。这种方法不仅能够实现极低计算成本下的高精度保持，还通过硬件友好的稀疏模式显著提升了推理速度，打破了传统剪枝依赖长周期重训练的限制。

Abstract: We study a Marchenko--Pastur (MP) random-matrix approach to pruning deep neural networks with very small post-pruning fine-tuning budgets. The main practical contribution is accuracy retention under short calibration and fine-tuning schedules, rather than a long post-pruning reoptimization pipeline. The theory gives deterministic data-path certificates: if the removed component $R$ has small propagated logit effect $L_s \| R ψ_1(s) \|_\infty$, pruning decreases an elastic-net objective and preserves samples whose dense margin exceeds twice the perturbation. The zero-budget case gives perfect pruning; a prune--restore extension models weight restoration inside a fixed sparse-execution pattern; and an additive $L_2$-regularized model shows admissible random-like components vanish at the training limit, with persistent spikes stabilizing as the MP bulk collapses. Under iid-Gaussian sufficient conditions, the fitted MP edge $σ_+$ gives a high-probability layerwise budget signal.
  On ImageNet-1k, after only three distillation epochs, ViT-B/16 $2{:}4{+}$ToMe reaches $83.41\%$ top-1 ($-1.70$ pp from dense) at $59.81\%$ sparse-execution MAC reduction, with $1.388\times$ best-observed A40 native-$2{:}4$ backend speedup for the same checkpoint and ToMe graph; a separate no-ToMe A100 endpoint gives $2.705\times$. At structured sparsity, ViT-B/16 $6{:}12$ reaches $83.74\%$, ViT-L/16 $8{:}16$ dense+permutation reaches $85.33\%$ ($-0.51$ pp), and ConvNeXtV2-Base $12{:}16$ reaches $86.35\%$ ($-0.37$ pp). For CNNs, ResNet50 $8{:}16$ dense+permutation reaches $75.87\%$ ($-0.26$ pp), and ResNet152d CAST-conv+permutation reaches $81.33\%$ ($-1.53$ pp) at ${\sim}50\%$ MAC accounting with a $1.62\times$ A40 im2col$+2{:}4$ sparse-GEMM audit.

</details>

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对激活预言机（AO）存在的幻觉和评估难点，通过改进训练机制和构建评估基准 AObench，提升了AO的实用性与评估规范化，旨在推动端到端可解释性的研究。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Activation Oracles (AOs) are promising methods for interpreting residual stream activations. However, current AOs face important issues, such as hallucinations and vagueness. Additionally, text-inversion confounds make them hard to evaluate. To this end, we improve the Activation Oracle (AO) training regime in four ways: training on on-policy rollouts, improving the conversational dataset, feeding more layers and an improvement to the injection formula. The capability improvements are marginal, but quality of life improvements are quite substantial. In addition, we open source the first comprehensive evaluation suite for AO quality, which we call AObench. Overall, we hope that our work sets a foundation that helps improve AOs and other models in the paradigm of scalable, end-to-end interpretability.

### [94] [Hallucination Is Linearly Decodable from Mid-Layer Hidden States in Quantized LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02628)
*Aizierjiang Aiersilan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究发现开源大语言模型的隐藏层中存在高度线性的“真实性”信号，通过在中层使用简单的线性探针，即可极其准确地检测模型幻觉，效果远超基于采样的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探索开源大语言模型的隐藏状态中是否编码了可线性分离的“真实性”信号，并确定该信号在网络中的最强表现层，以解决现有检测方法在识别模型幻觉方面的有效性争议。

Method: 研究使用了三个7B-8B参数的指令微调模型（Llama-3.1, Mistral, Qwen2.5），在四个幻觉基准测试数据集上提取隐藏状态。采用了四种检测方法：线性探针、MLP探针、INSIDE EigenScore、自洽性（self-consistency）和注意力熵。通过评估这些方法在不同网络深度的分类准确率（AUROC）来比较其性能。

Result: 线性探针在模型中层取得了高达0.904-1.000的AUROC，表现优异；MLP探针并未显著提升性能，验证了真实性信号的线性本质。相比之下，基于采样的检测方法表现不佳（AUROC < 0.541）。在知识导向任务中，第一层的注意力熵表现出了显著的补充识别能力（0.866-0.941 AUROC）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，开源大语言模型在隐藏层中确实编码了线性可分的真实性信号。线性探针在模型中层表现极佳，远超基于采样的检测方法。此外，早期层的注意力熵可作为有效的辅助指标，且无需额外计算开销。研究强调了真实性信号具有高度的线性特征，并定位了这些信号在不同模型架构中的峰值分布区间。

Abstract: We investigate whether open-source LLMs encode a linearly separable truthfulness signal in their hidden states, and at which network depth this signal is strongest. Across three $7$B--$8$B instruction-tuned models (Llama-3.1-8B, Mistral-7B, Qwen2.5-7B) loaded in $4$-bit NF4 quantization, we extract per-layer hidden states on four hallucination benchmarks (TruthfulQA, HaluEval-QA, FEVER, and a controlled synthetic set) and compare four detection approaches: linear and MLP probes, INSIDE EigenScore, self-consistency, and attention entropy. A linear probe on a single mid-network layer achieves $0.904$--$1.000$ AUROC on held-out splits, while sampling-based detectors do not exceed $0.541$ AUROC under the same protocol. The truthfulness signal is approximately linear: MLP probes rarely surpass linear probes by more than $0.01$ AUROC. Peak probing layers fall in a consistent band across model families on natural-language benchmarks -- blocks~$13$--$18$ of~$32$ for Llama and Mistral, and blocks~$19$--$25$ of~$28$ for Qwen. First-block attention entropy provides a complementary signal in knowledge-grounded settings ($0.866$--$0.941$ AUROC on HaluEval-QA) at no additional inference cost. The low discriminability of sampling methods under this protocol reflects a structural mismatch between paired-label evaluation and the information these methods access, rather than an inherent limitation of those methods. Code and data are released for full reproducibility on a single $8$\,GB GPU.

### [95] [Regime-Arrival Uncertainty in Generalization Bounds under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02657)
*Prince Poudel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量化政权切换环境下的泛化风险框架，通过分离“政权失配”与“政权敏感度”来修正泛化界，有效提升了对金融市场等非平稳数据环境下的风险评估能力，而非依赖于对政权转换时间的预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的泛化界假设训练集和部署集分布相同或保持静态，忽略了金融市场等环境下常见的“政权切换（regime switching）”现象（如平稳期与危机期的比例波动）。现有方法难以量化由于政权构成比例差异引起的泛化误差。

Method: 作者提出了一种基于马尔可夫切换（Markov-switching）分布的泛化界框架。通过将额外风险分解为“政权失配（regime mismatch）”和“政权敏感度（regime sensitivity）”两部分，并利用修正了谱间隙（spectral gap）的有效样本量将泛化界扩展至 $\beta$-混合数据。此外，使用全球股票指数数据进行了实证分析。

Result: 研究得出了政权失配风险的精确分解公式，并提供了针对合成数据及25年全球股票指数数据的极小极大（minimax）下界。结果表明，所提出的惩罚项能有效反映事后的实际泛化差距，而仅基于训练数据的估计器则表现不佳；同时发现模型特征几何结构可捕捉危机特征，但难以预测政权到来的时点。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，通过对政权（regime）构成的偏差进行建模，可以更准确地评估模型在金融等非平稳环境下的泛化风险。尽管该框架无法预测政权转换的时间，但能有效量化由于政权分布失配带来的额外风险，为政权敏感型模型的鲁棒性评估提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The standard generalization bounds assume that the training and deployment distributions are the same, or are static, and don't consider regime switching environments where the ratio of calm vs crisis states is different. This paper proposes a framework that generalizes regime-aware models by quantifying the extra risk due to regime composition mismatch, when distribution shifts are Markov-switching. We obtain an exact decomposition, separating regime mismatch from regime sensitivity; we extend the bound to beta-mixing data using the effective sample size corrected for the spectral gap; and we show a minimax lower bound for synthetic data and on 25 years of global equity indices. The proposed penalty is an ex post realized generalization gap, whereas the training-only estimator does not show significant correlation: the feature geometry of crises can be detected, but not the temporal arrival. Thus, the framework is not a forecast machine. Forecasting the composition of the future regime is an open question in the rare cases of regime change.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有处理结构化多模态数据的模型通常假设模态完整，且在面对缺失模态时往往过于关注局部信息，忽略了模态间的全局互补性。为了应对真实场景中模态缺失和不确定性的问题，研究者旨在开发一种更鲁棒的动态融合模型。

Method: 1. 提出一种跨特征和模态维度的双重注意力机制，用于计算可靠的注意力权重；2. 设计实体质心对比学习模块（entity-centroid contrastive learning），通过构建基于实体的正样本来增强表征的判别能力；3. 引入自适应融合模块，以实现对不同模态输入的高效动态融合。

Conclusion: 本文提出的CL-DMDF模型通过创新的注意力机制、基于实体的对比学习模块和自适应融合策略，有效解决了多模态数据缺失和不确定性带来的挑战，为鲁棒的多模态融合提供了新的技术路径。

Abstract: Multimodal data fusion involves integrating and analyzing information from multiple modalities to uncover latent correlations and complementary patterns, thereby enhancing data processing and decision-making. While existing methods for structured multimodal inputs are typically designed around specific tasks and assume fully observed modalities, real-world applications often suffer from uncertain or missing modality inputs due to various factors. Some traditional models overly emphasize local interactions within missing modalities, neglecting the global complementary cues embedded in multimodal representations. To overcome these limitations, we propose a Dynamic Multimodal Data Fusion model based on Contrastive Learning (CL-DMDF). CL-DMDF introduces a novel attention mechanism that operates across both feature and modality dimensions to compute reliable attention scores, effectively reflecting importance at each level. The CL-DMDF further incorporates an entity-centroid contrastive learning module that constructs centroid-based positive samples from entity features to enhance discriminative learning. Additionally, an adaptive fusion module is employed to improve the efficiency and accuracy of dynamic fusion strategies. Extensive experiments conducted on three datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of the CL-DMDF across diverse multimodal fusion tasks.

### [97] [Improvise, Adapt, Overcome: An On-The-Fly Multifidelity Algorithm for Efficient Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02662)
*Vivin Vinod,Peter Zaspel*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入了一种自适应多保真度机器学习框架，通过在训练过程中动态确定各层级数据的需求量，显著减少了高昂计算成本的浪费，在保持高预测精度的同时，将量子化学数据生成效率提升了数倍。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种自适应的即时（on-the-fly）多保真度学习框架。该框架摒弃了传统方法中预定义缩放因子的做法，改为在训练过程中动态查询各保真度下的样本。算法遵循“饱和原则”，即在尝试更高保真度参考计算之前，先在低保真度下使模型精度饱和，从而自主决定最优的训练集构成，消除数据冗余。

Result: 数值实验表明，该自适应算法在预测耦合簇能量（计算化学金标准）及激发能量等多种化学属性时，表现优异。与单保真度方法相比，数据生成成本最高可降低30倍；与标准MFML方案相比，效率提升最高可达5倍。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种自适应多保真度机器学习框架，能够通过动态查询机制有效平衡数据生成成本与模型精度。该方法显著降低了对高昂高保真度数据的依赖，证明了在量子化学计算中通过策略性数据采集实现高效建模的可行性，为可持续的计算化学机器学习提供了一条高精度、低成本的路径。

Abstract: Machine learning has accelerated quantum chemistry but is hindered by the prohibitive cost of generating high fidelity training data. Multifidelity machine learning (MFML) mitigates this overhead by systematically combining abundant low fidelity data with sparse high fidelity data. In spite of its success, standard MFML schemes rely on pre-defined scaling factors to determine sparse data ratio across fidelities, often generating redundant multifidelity data resulting in a loss of efficiency. Here, we introduce an adaptive on-the-fly multifidelity framework for machine learning that autonomously determines training dataset composition. By dynamically querying training samples at each fidelity, the algorithm saturates model accuracy at lower fidelities before moving up to more expensive reference calculations. We benchmark the novel adaptive-MFML across diverse chemical properties including the computational chemistry gold standard coupled cluster energies, and the more chemically challenging excitation energies. In our numerical experiments we show that our adaptive algorithm reduces data generation costs by up to a factor of 30 compared to single fidelity methods and improves upon standard MFML by up to a factor of 5. The mitigation of data redundancy establishes a high-accuracy low-cost pathway for sustainable cost-aware machine learning in quantum chemistry.

### [98] [AdaWeather: Adaptively Mixing Probabilistic Weather Forecasts with Logarithmic Regret](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02663)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习天气预报模型发展迅速，但单一模型难以在所有时空维度上保持最优，且性能表现高度依赖于具体情境。因此，需要一种能够自适应地结合多种预测结果以提升预报精度与鲁棒性的通用框架。

Method: 提出了一种名为 AdaWeather 的自适应框架，该方法结合了机器学习技术与专家混合（Mixture of Experts）模型，旨在通过加权融合多个不同的概率天气预报模型，并针对该方法推导了其在事后最佳静态专家混合模型下的对数遗憾界。

Abstract: Recent advances in machine learning have produced probabilistic weather forecasting models comparable to state-of-the-art numerical weather predictors. But no model consistently dominates spatio-temporally, and relative performance is highly context-dependent. This motivates adaptive methods for combining multiple forecasts to obtain improvements and robustness. While combined forecasts have been proposed in the literature, these are achieved either through supervised learning or through prediction with expert advice methods. We introduce AdaWeather, an adaptive framework that combines many probabilistic forecasts using both machine learning as well as mixture of experts to arrive at a unified improved probabilistic forecast. While traditional expert methods develop the regret bounds with respect to the best single expert in hindsight, we extend the algorithm and analysis to show our method has logarithmic regret compared to the best static mixture of experts in hindsight. Empirically, we focus on forecasting temperature, and observe improvements over existing methods.

### [99] [Anomalies in Multivariate Time Series Benchmarks Are Mostly Univariate](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02670)
*Marc Pinet,Julien Cumin,Samuel Berlemont,Dominique Vaufreydaz*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文研究发现，当前主流的多变量时间序列异常检测（MT-SAD）基准测试存在局限性，由于绝大多数异常表现为明显的单变量偏差，导致通道间建模（CD）相比于简单的通道独立建模（CI）并无优势，现有的基准无法有效评估跨通道建模的能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前许多MT-SAD模型倾向于整合跨通道建模，假设异常会通过通道间的相关性变化体现。研究者质疑这一假设在现有基准测试中是否真实成立，并试图探究现有的多变量异常检测模型是否真的从跨通道建模中获益。

Method: 作者引入了一个基于分段的诊断框架，用于分析异常发生时是否存在“单变量偏差”或“跨通道相关性结构变化”。此外，作者还利用相位偏移的正弦波合成了包含特定跨通道结构破坏的数据集，并对比了通道依赖（CD）模型与通道独立（CI）模型在真实基准与合成数据上的表现。

Result: 研究发现，在现有的八个公开基准测试中，几乎所有的异常都伴随着单变量偏差，不存在仅表现为跨通道结构变化的情况。此外，对于大多数数据集，通道独立（CI）模型与通道依赖（CD）模型的检测性能没有显著差异，表明现有的MT-SAD模型并未真正利用跨通道信息。

Conclusion: 现有的多变量时间序列异常检测（MT-SAD）基准测试并不足以验证跨通道建模的有效性。作者呼吁开发具有更丰富结构多样性的评估数据集，以便真正衡量模型处理复杂异常的能力。

Abstract: Many recent multivariate time series anomaly detection (MT-SAD) models incorporate cross-channel modeling, under the implicit assumption that the structure of anomalies may be spread across multiple channels. We evaluate this assumption on eight widely used public benchmarks by introducing a per-segment diagnostic framework that flags, for each labeled anomaly, whether at least one channel deviates individually from its normal history, whether the cross-channel correlation structure changes, or both. The framework shows that no crosschannel rupture occurs without an accompanying univariate deviation across a range of reasonable thresholds. A complementary metric also reveals that on six of the eight benchmarks, at least half of the labeled anomaly segments deviate univariately on 79% to 100% of their timesteps, reaching 100% on three of these datasets. To verify that our framework captures cross-channel structure when present, we construct synthetic data of phase-shifted sinusoidal channels with shared noise. Each anomalous segment is altered through one of two channelwise corruptions that preserve the per-channel marginal distribution while breaking cross-channel structure, and our framework correctly characterizes these segments as cross-channel-only. On these data, channel-dependent (CD) models successfully exploit the cross-channel signal whereas channel-independent (CI) ones fail. The CI/CD comparison of a recent SOTA detector on real benchmarks further confirms that CD modeling brings no measurable gain. We conclude that current MTSAD benchmarks are unsuitable for validating cross-channel modeling capabilities, and we call for the development of more structurally diverse evaluation sets. The code for this study is publicly available.

</details>


### [100] [Aligning Data-Driven Predictors with Allocation: A Decision-Focused Approach to Survival Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02671)
*Itai Zilberstein,Ioannis Anagnostides,Tuomas Sandholm*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文揭示了优化传统统计指标在决策应用中可能失效的问题，提出了一种以NDCG为目标的决策导向型学习框架，显著提升了器官移植分配的决策效率与临床结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前机器学习预测模型通常与其实际应用决策任务相脱节，主要关注统计准确性指标（如C-index），这在诸如器官分配等高风险决策场景中会导致性能极差，甚至不如随机选择。因此，研究旨在弥合生存预测与政策优化之间的鸿沟。

Method: 1. 理论层面：论证了使用传统的生存分析指标（如C-index）在分配任务中无法保证最优性，并证明了NDCG在生存分析中能够转化为分配性能保障。

Abstract: Machine learning predictors have become essential tools for guiding automated decision making. However, a major misalignment persists: predictive models are typically optimized in terms of standard statistical metrics in isolation from the algorithmic tasks they inform. We highlight this incongruity in the high-stakes domain of organ allocation by demonstrating that any algorithm relying on (even highly accurate) survival predictors optimized for standard metrics -- such as the Concordance index (C-index) -- can yield arbitrarily poor outcomes when used for allocation, failing to guarantee utility better than a uniform random selection. To bridge the gap between survival analysis and policy optimization, we introduce a decision-focused learning approach based on optimizing normalized discounted cumulative gain (NDCG), a mainstay metric in information retrieval. We establish the utility of NDCG in survival analysis by proving that it translates to guarantees on the performance of allocation. Empirically, we propose a bootstrapping approach to optimize the NDCG of existing survival models. Unlike prior work, we also address the challenge of right censorship when evaluating ranking. On historical heart transplant data from the US, our method dramatically boosts the NDCG of baseline models by 50-100%, which translates to tens of thousands of additional life years gained annually when deployed for transplant allocation. We anticipate that our framework will find broader applications in decision making with predictions.

### [101] [Before Fusion, Ask What to Keep: Contextual Calibration of Multimodal Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02679)
*Jiyuan Liu,Liangwei Nathan Zheng,Wei Emma Zhang,Xinpei Wang,Weitong Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态系统往往直接合并各模态信息，但不同模态之间可能存在冲突或干扰，导致有用信息被掩盖，因此需要一种机制在融合前对模态表示进行调整，以滤除噪声并强化可靠信息。

Method: 开发了一种紧凑的校准模块（Calibration Module），通过在概要层面对不同模态进行比较，提取跨模态的支持与冲突线索，并将其转化为实例级（instance-wise）和维度级（dimension-wise）的调制信号，用于在融合前对原始模态特征进行抑制或增强。

Conclusion: 本文提出的预融合校准策略能够有效减少多模态系统中的干扰，提升不同模态间的协同效应，证明了在融合前对模态特征进行自适应调节对于构建鲁棒的多模态系统至关重要。

Abstract: Multimodal systems often benefit from combining information across language, sound, and visual streams, but this benefit is not guaranteed. A modality that is useful for one input may become distracting for another, and local feature responses within the same modality can disagree with evidence from other sources. This work investigates how to adjust multimodal representations before they are merged by a downstream predictor. We develop a compact calibration module that compares each modality with the others at the summary level, extracts cues of cross-source support and conflict, and converts these cues into instance-wise and dimension-wise modulation signals. The calibration is applied to the original modality features rather than to already fused representations, enabling the model to suppress misleading components, preserve weak but useful evidence, and emphasize responses that are better supported by the current multimodal context. The module is designed as a plug-in component and can be attached to different fusion backbones without changing their prediction heads. Across five benchmarks covering sentiment understanding, action recognition, audio-visual event detection, and audio-visual emotion classification, the proposed pre-combination calibration strategy improves performance under both sequence-based and convolutional fusion settings. Additional analyses under modality removal, synthetic corruption, training dynamics, and feature-level visualization show that calibrating signals before fusion can reduce interference from unreliable modalities and produce more stable multimodal optimization.

### [102] [Locality Does Not Imply Reachability: Boundary Repair in Block-Sparse Causal Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02680)
*Zhibo Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了稀疏分块因果注意力中“局部性”与“可达性”失配导致的性能瓶颈，通过形式化分析揭示了边界处的通信限制，并提出了一种轻量级的边界桥接修复方案，为优化长序列注意力结构提供了理论支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的稀疏因果注意力机制通常依赖于序列局部性，但作者发现固定块因果注意力（Fixed block causal attention）存在“序列局部性”与“注意力图可达性”之间的不匹配。即相邻的token在注意力图中可能因分块限制而无法通信，导致模型无法有效处理跨块信息，造成性能损失。

Method: 1. 形式化分析：引入结构依赖集（Structural Dependency Sets）来量化固定分块因果注意力中的边界人工制品；2. 数学推导：通过相位条件下的覆盖函数（Phase-conditioned coverage functions）分析可达性与距离及偏移量的关系；3. 实验验证：设计K-way边界复制任务验证理论界限；4. 构造修复：提出Boundary Bridge Attention，通过共享投影在块边界增加辅助因果边，无需额外参数；5. 验证测试：进行1024 token受控实验及Qwen2.5-7B大模型探测实验。

Result: 1. 证明了在固定分块配置下，目标表示仅能依赖于其所属块前缀中的token，且在K-way边界复制任务中存在明确的准确率上界（1/K）和交叉熵下界（log K）；2. 揭示了可达性不仅依赖于距离，还受目标在块内偏移量的影响；3. 实验显示，通过边界桥接注意力机制，可以显著提升模型在覆盖对齐任务中的表现，并证实该失配问题在如Qwen2.5-7B等大规模模型中同样存在。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种针对分块因果注意力中局部性与可达性失配问题的理论诊断框架，并证明了边界桥接注意力（Boundary Bridge Attention）作为一种无需额外参数的修复机制，能够有效改善跨边界的信息流传递。通过对Coverage函数及其相位条件的研究，揭示了分块注意力机制在处理跨块信息时的本质限制，为设计更高效的稀疏注意力结构提供了理论指导。

Abstract: Sparse causal attention is usually described by sequence locality: nearby tokens should remain easy to access, while distant tokens may be dropped to reduce cost. This paper studies a mismatch between sequence locality and attention-graph reachability. In fixed block causal attention, two adjacent tokens can be disconnected in the attention graph at every depth. We formalize this boundary artifact through structural dependency sets: if every attention layer uses the same fixed block causal mask and all remaining operations are positionwise, a target representation can depend only on tokens in its own block prefix. This yields an architecture-level boundary-copy separation for a constructed K-way boundary-copy distribution, with top-1 accuracy upper bound 1/K and expected cross-entropy lower bound log K. We then derive phase-conditioned coverage functions showing that reachability depends on both source-target distance and the target's offset within its block. These coverage laws predict when a sparse pattern should fail, when a repair can help, and why sliding-window attention and boundary repair are not interchangeable. Boundary Bridge Attention is treated as a constructive witness: it preserves the fixed block path and adds zero-additional-parameter auxiliary causal edges near block boundaries using shared projections. Controlled 1024-token experiments show that gains concentrate in coverage-aligned diagnostics. As secondary external-validity evidence, a fixed-checkpoint 8K-token Qwen2.5-7B probe shows the same coverage-incomparability pattern. The contribution is a theory-guided diagnostic framework for locality-reachability mismatch in block-sparse causal attention, together with phase-conditioned coverage analysis and a minimal constructive repair.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的在线策略蒸馏（OPD）方法逐渐从全轨迹 KL 监督转向更具选择性的训练范式，但仍缺乏对优化粒度的深度整合。为了解决这一问题，研究旨在通过同时在轨迹和令牌层面优化监督信号，以提高学习效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为 FiRe-OPD（过滤与重加权）的方法，包含两个阶段：首先，通过过滤机制剔除低质量的样本轨迹；其次，在保留的轨迹中应用软重加权机制，根据令牌的信息量动态调整其监督信号的权重。

Abstract: On-Policy distillation (OPD) in large language models is shifting from full-trace KL supervision toward more selective training paradigms. Recent OPD methods increasingly focus on selecting which trajectories to learn from, which tokens are most informative, and which supervision signals are most reliable. Motivated by this trend, we rethink optimization granularity of OPD and propose \fireicon\ FiRe-OPD (Filter, then Reweight), which jointly adjusts supervision signals at both trajectory and token levels. In details, FiRe-OPD first filters trajectories to remove low-quality rollout samples, and then applies soft reweighting within the retained trajectories to emphasize informative tokens. Compared with hard token selection, FiRe-OPD leverages a soft-weighting mechanism to effectively mitigate information loss and enhance optimization stability, thereby achieving finer-grained OPD optimization. We validate the effectiveness of FiRe-OPD across strong-to-weak, single-teacher, and multi-teacher settings, and demonstrate its superiority over recent token-level OPD methods ( (e.g., +6.25 on AIME 2024 in strong-to-weak, +18.81 on Miner in multi-teacher). Our code is available at https://github.com/YuYingLi0/FiRe-OPD.

To address this challenge, the correlation between vehicle signals and road surface condition during cruising needs to be uncovered using machine learning. ### [106] [Representational Capacity: Geometric Limits on Feature Representation in Transformer Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02765)
*Alexander Guha*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文探讨了 Transformer 模型维度对特征表示的几何限制，通过修正 Johnson-Lindenstrauss 引理，建立了一个能精准预测模型表征容量的新框架，并揭示了大模型在特征正交性与容量之间的权衡策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管模型维度是 Transformer 的核心超参数，但其在几何层面限制特征表示的作用尚不明确。现有理论（如线性表示和叠加假设）认为特征以近乎正交的方向存在于潜在空间中，本文旨在量化模型究竟能支持多少个这样的方向，并揭示维度与表征能力之间的数学关系。

Method: 本文构建了一个基于嵌入矩阵的分析框架，利用两两余弦相似度分布中的边界来度量模型对正交性的偏差容忍度（$\varepsilon$）。在此基础上，对传统的 Johnson-Lindenstrauss 引理进行了修正，引入了矢量与维度的比例（$k/d$）作为核心变量，从而更准确地估算模型的表征容量。

Result: 研究发现，将 $k/d$ 比例引入容量计算后，预测误差降低了两个数量级。此外，实验表明存在两类模型：高 $\varepsilon$ 类（嵌入缺乏正交结构）和低 $\varepsilon$ 类（维持了良好的正交结构）。大模型通常倾向于维持更严格的正交约束，而非一味最大化原始容量。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一种新的表征容量评估框架，指出模型通过收紧正交性约束（降低容差 $\varepsilon$）来优化表征质量，而非单纯追求容量最大化。模型在表征容量与特征可区分性之间存在权衡，这一发现为理解大语言模型在不同规模下的特征表示机制提供了重要理论依据。

Abstract: Model dimension ($d_{model}$) is a fundamental hyperparameter in transformer language models, yet its role in setting the geometric limits of feature representation remains under-explored. Grounded in the Linear Representation and Superposition Hypotheses - which propose that models encode features as near-orthogonal directions in latent space - we develop a framework for estimating how many such directions a model can support. We first establish the embedding matrix as a measurable proxy for near-orthogonality constraints across the latent space: the boundary between meaningful token relationships and incidental similarity in the pairwise cosine similarity distribution gives a concrete estimate of the model's accepted deviation $\varepsilon$ from perfect orthogonality. Applying this metric across dozens of open-source models reveals two classes: models with high $\varepsilon$ whose embeddings lack near-orthogonal structure, and models with low $\varepsilon$ that maintain it. We then show that the standard Johnson-Lindenstrauss lemma greatly underestimates the packing efficiency of trained representations, and derive an adjusted capacity formula in which the number of near-orthogonal directions depends on the ratio of vectors to dimensions ($k/d$) rather than the raw count - a single modification that cuts prediction error by two orders of magnitude with no extra parameters. Combining these results, we define representational capacity as an upper bound on the number of distinguishable directions available for features and embeddings in a model's latent space. Capacity is exponentially sensitive to $\varepsilon$, and larger models favor tighter orthogonality constraints over maximizing raw capacity - a pattern compatible with several explanations (a stability-capacity trade-off, a ceiling on usable concepts, or confounds with model scale) that we leave to future work.

</details>


### [107] [QUIVER: Quantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations in Large ML Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02785)
*Aritra Bal,Michael Binder,Markus Klute,Benedikt Maier,Michael Spannowsky*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 QUIVER 范式，通过提取变分量子线路的量子费希尔信息作为特征增强，为机器学习模型引入量子几何视角，在不同领域基准测试中显著提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型机器学习模型在多模态输入下表现更好。现有方法大多依赖经典数据增强，而量子力学中的几何结构（如量子态流形的内在几何）包含的复杂高阶相关性难以通过传统的经典模型学习。因此，作者旨在通过引入量子信息论视角下的量子费希尔信息，为机器学习模型提供一种非冗余的、互补的特征模态。

Method: 提出 QUIVER (QUantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations) 范式。该方法利用变分量子线路 (VQC) 捕捉数据的量子费希尔信息矩阵 (Quantum Fisher Information Matrix)，将其作为一种几何基准无关的特征向量，补充到经典机器学习模型中，从而融合量子几何信息。

Result: 在 QM9（分子性质预测）和 JetClass（大型强子对撞机喷注味预测）两个跨领域基准测试中，集成 QUIVER 范式的模型在标准性能指标上均取得了提升，验证了该方法在捕捉传统方法难以学习的统计结构方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了即使在容错量子硬件出现之前，通过模拟变分量子线路提取的“量子几何特征”也能为机器学习任务带来显著的性能提升。QUIVER 提供了一种与领域无关的通用增强框架，为未来量子-经典混合机器学习的研究开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Large machine learning models benefit substantially from multimodal inputs that provide a complementary view of the same example. We introduce QUIVER (QUantum-Informed Views for Enhanced Representations, a paradigm that enriches classical data-driven features with a quantum Fisher view: a geometrically motivated, basis-independent summary of higher-order correlations captured by a variational quantum circuit (VQC) trained to perform the same task. Unlike classical feature augmentation, the quantum Fisher information matrix encodes the intrinsic geometry of the learned quantum state manifold. While this feature map, motivated by quantum information theory, is ordinarily non-trivial to model classically, it can surface statistical structure that additional classical data or model capacity finds difficult to learn. This makes the quantum Fisher view a genuinely complementary modality rather than a redundant one. We demonstrate that QUIVER improves standard performance metrics on two benchmark datasets from very different fields: QM9 for predicting molecule properties, and JetClass for predicting jet flavor at the Large Hadron Collider (LHC). The core contribution, however, is domain-agnostic: the quantum Fisher view can be fused into a broad class of model architectures via targeted modifications to the base architecture, to incorporate information about the quantum geometry of the problem. These results demonstrate that quantum-geometric features, extracted from simulated variational circuits, can deliver measurable value for standard machine learning tasks, well before the advent of fault-tolerant quantum hardware.

</details>


### [108] [Qift: Shift-Friendly No-Zero W2 Post-Training Quantization for Rotated W2A4/KV4 LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02823)
*Chi-Wei Huang,Chia-Chi Tsai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文针对 W2A4 量化性能下降问题，提出了一种名为 Qift 的无零对称量化方案。通过分析 Hadamard 旋转后的权重分布，设计了最优化的固定量化水平集，在无需额外训练和复杂计算的条件下，显著提升了 LLM 在极低位宽下的推理精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在极低位宽（W2A4/KV4）推理场景下，传统的 {-2, -1, 0, +1} 量化水平集会导致性能严重崩溃，现有的量化方案往往过于复杂且难以部署，因此需要一种更优、更高效的 W2 量化水平集设计。

Method: 1. 分析 Hadamard 变换后权重分布的几何特性，发现其趋向于零中心的高斯分布。
2. 提出 Qift 方案，采用非零对称水平集（如 {+/-0.5, +/-1.5} 或 {+/-1, +/-3}），利用标度不变比率分析确定了最优的内外质心比（0.25-0.33）。
3. 构建了一个无需训练、无需学习码本、无需零点偏移的固定 W2 量化框架，并保留了标准的逐通道缩放机制。

Result: Qift 在 LLaMA-2-7B 和 LLaMA-3.1-8B 上显著改善了 W2A4 量化的困惑度（Perplexity）及下游任务准确率，特别是在混合精度设置下大幅缩小了与 W3A4 的性能差距。

Conclusion: Qift 证明了通过重新设计无零（non-zero）的 W2 量化标量水平集，可以在无需额外训练或复杂码本的情况下，显著提升极端低位宽量化（如 W2A4/KV4）下的推理性能，为 LLM 的高效部署提供了一种简单且鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Two-bit weight quantization is attractive for memory-efficient LLM inference, but the standard W2 level set {-2,-1,0,+1} often collapses under aggressive W2A4/KV4 settings. We study the scalar level-set geometry of two-bit weights in a Hadamard-rotated quantization pipeline. Conventional asymmetric W2 substantially improves over the standard level set, indicating that W2A4 failure is not only a bit-width problem but also a reconstruction-level problem. Across all 224 linear modules in each of LLaMA-2-7B and LLaMA-3.1-8B, pretrained weights are already nearly zero-centered, while Hadamard rotation primarily Gaussianizes their standardized shape: excess kurtosis and Q-Q error drop by orders of magnitude. Based on this approximate zero-centered Gaussian-like source model, we propose Qift, a fixed no-zero W2 level set for rotated W2A4/KV4 inference. The main level set is {+/-0.5, +/-1.5}, equivalently {+/-1, +/-3} under a half-scale reparameterization; a power-of-two variant uses {+/-1, +/-4} for sign-and-shift decoded weight application. Qift redesigns the fixed two-bit code-to-level mapping and is training-free, learned-codebook-free, group-grid-free, and zero-point-free, retaining the standard per-channel scale. A scale-invariant ratio analysis identifies an effective inner/outer centroid ratio range of 0.25 to 0.33, explaining why mirror no-zero (MNZ), Lloyd, NF2, and PoT-MNZ perform well while {+/-1, +/-2} does not. On both models, the no-zero level sets consistently improve pure W2A4 perplexity, L-layer mixed W2/W4 perplexity, downstream accuracy, and GPTQ residual behavior over the standard W2 level set. At L=16 mixed precision, they substantially narrow the gap to W3A4 while keeping half of the transformer layers at two-bit precision, giving a simple, source-aware, and deployment-friendly alternative to more complex learned W2 codebooks.

</details>


### [109] [Mitigating Spurious Correlations with Memorization-Guided Dataset De-Biasing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02830)
*Arda Fazla,Abolfazl Hashemi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种无需组标签的两阶段样本选择方法，通过解耦核心特征与虚假特征的学习动态，仅需极少量训练数据即可显著降低模型对虚假相关性的依赖，提升模型鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实世界数据集中常包含导致模型过度拟合的虚假相关性，而现有的子集选择或核集（coreset）方法往往依赖这些虚假特征，且通常需要难以获取的组标签信息。作者旨在解决模型对虚假特征的过度依赖问题，并消除对已知组标签的依赖。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段样本评分函数：首先通过分析模型对核心特征与虚假特征的学习动态，将二者进行解耦；随后分别评估这两类特征的难度。基于此度量标准，设计了一种新的算法，用于在存在或不存在虚假相关性的数据集中查找并优先选取最具信息量的样本，从而引导模型学习因果相关特征。

Result: 实验表明，使用该方法筛选出的仅占原始训练集10%的样本进行标准经验风险最小化（ERM）训练，其性能优于当前最先进的去偏差（debiasing）技术。

Conclusion: 本文提出的两阶段样本评分函数通过解耦核心特征与虚假特征的学习动态，无需预先获知组标签即可有效识别并优先级排序关键样本，为解决虚假相关性问题提供了一种高效、轻量级的通用方案。

Abstract: Real-world datasets often contain spurious correlations that are not causally related to the target label. When such correlations dominate the majority of training samples, models tend to rely on them, leading to misclassification of minority samples that do not exhibit the same spurious patterns. While a potential approach is to select subsets of data to better represent the minority samples, this may require access to group labels, which are typically unknown. Furthermore, as we demonstrate, widely used sample scoring functions in the invariant subset or coreset selection literature largely depend on spurious features and therefore fail to accurately capture the importance or difficulty of core, causally relevant features. Accordingly, we propose to mitigate spurious correlations by developing a two-stage sample scoring function that disentangles the learning dynamics of core and spurious features and evaluates their difficulty separately. Based on our proposed metric, we introduce a new algorithm to find and prioritize informative samples both with and without spurious correlations. Extensive experiments demonstrate that a standard ERM model trained on our selected samples achieves superior performance compared to state-of-the-art debiasing techniques, while requiring as little as 10\% of the original training data.

Conclusion: RESCAST-100K 作为一个全面且结构化的基准测试，为跨域住宅能源预测提供了标准化的评估框架。实验表明，基于交叉注意力（Cross-attention）和 MLP-mixer 的架构在处理域偏移时优于传统的循环神经网络和 Transformer 模型，为实现更稳健的住宅能源管理和智能电网应用奠定了基础。

Abstract: Accurate short-term forecasting of residential energy load and indoor temperature is essential for home energy management systems, grid-level demand response, and community energy efficiency efforts. However, progress is limited by the lack of comprehensive residential datasets: existing benchmarks are narrow in target coverage and rarely support structured cross-domain evaluation. We introduce RESCAST-100K, a large-scale residential forecasting benchmark for studying cross-domain generalization. It provides a configuration-driven interface that instantiates source and target domains along interpretable axes, including geography, climate zone, wall construction, and heating equipment, enabling systematic evaluation of transfer learning, domain adaptation, and zero-shot generalization under controlled domain shifts. The benchmark covers approximately 100,000 EnergyPlus-simulated U.S. homes derived from ResStock, with 15-minute time series for three coupled targets per home: total load, HVAC load, and indoor temperature. These are paired with weather channels, HVAC setpoints, and over 40 static building covariates. RESCAST-100K also integrates five real-world residential datasets under a unified schema, supporting sim-to-real evaluation on the same tasks. We benchmark recurrent, attention-based, and MLP-mixer architectures for zero-shot performance across domains, missing-input conditions, and forecasting tasks. Cross-attention and MLP-mixer models consistently outperform recurrent and classical transformer baselines under domain shift. RESCAST-100K is intended to aid the machine learning and building analytics communities advance cross-domain residential forecasting at home, community, and grid scale.

### [111] [GRZO: Group-Relative Zeroth-Order Optimization for Large Language Model Fine-Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02857)
*Liyan Tan,Yequan Zhao,Yifan Yang,Ruijie Zhang,Xinling Yu,Zheng Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: GRZO 是一种新型的零阶优化器，通过组相对归一化技术有效降低了梯度估计方差，在保持低显存占用的同时，显著提升了大型语言模型微调的准确率与收敛速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的零阶（ZO）优化方法（如 MeZO）在微调大规模语言模型时，由于梯度估计的方差过高，导致训练效率和收敛性能受到限制，且无法有效利用批量训练带来的潜在收益。

Method: GRZO 引入了一种基于分组相对标准化的零阶优化策略。该方法通过在每个小批量样本中应用伪独立扰动，并利用组内相对归一化来聚合损失，从而在不增加前向传播成本的前提下，有效提高了梯度方向估计的统计量，显著降低了估计方差。

Result: 在 RoBERTa-large、Llama3-8B 和 OPT-13B 等多个模型上的实验表明，与 MeZO 相比，GRZO 在 Llama3-8B 上的平均准确率提高了 3.0 个百分点，同时显存占用降低了 23%。作为 MeZO 的直接替代方案，它能使各种稀疏化、低秩和量化变体性能平均提升 6.0 个百分点。

Conclusion: GRZO 提供了一种高效、低显存占用的微调方法，不仅在理论上证明了其比 MeZO 更优的收敛边界，还在大规模模型实验中验证了其显著的性能提升和通用性。

Abstract: Zeroth-order (ZO) optimization is a memory-efficient alternative to backpropagation for fine-tuning large language models, but its deployment is limited by the high variance of gradient estimation. We propose GRZO, a Group-Relative Zeroth-Order optimizer that draws one pseudo-independent perturbation per mini-batch example and aggregates the per-example losses through group-relative normalization, raising the effective gradient-direction count from one to the batch size at no additional forward cost while preserving inference-level memory. We prove that GRZO is directionally unbiased with variance shrinking proportionally to the batch size, yielding a tighter nonconvex convergence bound than MeZO. Across RoBERTa-large, Llama3-8B, and OPT-13B over multiple tasks, GRZO improves average accuracy on Llama3-8B by $+3.0$ over MeZO at $23\%$ lower peak GPU memory; as a drop-in replacement for the MeZO core, it lifts sparse, low-rank, and quantized ZO variants by $+6.0$ on average.

### [112] [RRISE: Robust Radius Inference via a Surrogate Estimator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02876)
*Jong-Ik Park,Shreyas Chaudhari,Carlee Joe-Wong,José M. F. Moura*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: RRISE 是一种新型随机平滑框架，通过训练代理模型替代实时采样，将昂贵的认证过程转化为单次前向传递，在保持高认证准确率的同时实现了极高的推理效率，适合重复部署环境。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的随机平滑（Randomized Smoothing）方法在推理时严重依赖针对每个输入的蒙特卡洛采样，计算开销巨大，无法满足实时系统的需求。该研究旨在通过在部署流中共享信息，打破这种依赖，从而显著降低认证成本。

Method: RRISE 框架通过预先计算的蒙特卡洛（MC）类计数目标，训练一个代理模型以逼近平滑分类器；随后引入一次性共形校准（Conformal Calibration）步骤，将代理模型的预测转换为具有统计保证的保守认证半径。这种方法将原本针对每个输入的多次采样推理简化为单一的前向传递过程。

Result: RRISE 在图像分类基准测试中，以单次前向传递替代了高达 $10^4$ 次的噪声基模型评估，同时认证准确率仅比固定预算的 MC 方法低约 0.84 个百分点；在 CIFAR-100 和 Tiny ImageNet 上，其认证准确率比现有的离线代理方法高出 1.23 到 1.91 倍。

Conclusion: RRISE 证明了通过学习型代理模型进行高效随机平滑是可行的，不仅显著降低了推理成本，还在处理复杂数据集时展现出优于现有离线代理方法的鲁棒性，为在重复部署场景下实现认证鲁棒性提供了实用路径。

Abstract: Randomized smoothing (RS) uses a smoothed classifier to provide architecture-agnostic certificates of $\ell_2$ classification robustness, but its dependence on per-input Monte Carlo (MC) sampling undermines its use in real-time systems. We argue that this cost is structural rather than fundamental, such that it can be significantly reduced by sharing information across the deployment stream. We introduce RRISE, an RS framework that compresses certification into a single forward pass through a learned surrogate. RRISE trains the surrogate against precomputed MC class-count targets via a soft-label cross-entropy loss and converts surrogate predictions into provably conservative certified radii through a one-time conformal calibration step. The resulting certificate is deployment-verifiable: whenever the calibrated radius is positive, the surrogate's prediction provably matches the smoothed classifier's and the smoothed classifier is constant on a ball of that radius around the input. Across image classification benchmarks, RRISE matches fixed-budget MC certified accuracy within $0.84$ percentage points while replacing up to $10^4$ noisy base-model evaluations per query with a single surrogate forward pass, recouping MC training cost after $\approx 10^5$ deployment queries. On CIFAR-100 and Tiny ImageNet, where the only prior offline-surrogate method collapses, RRISE achieves $1.23$ to $1.91\times$ higher certified accuracy, establishing efficient randomized smoothing as a practical path to certified robustness in repeated-deployment settings.

</details>


### [113] [Outsmarting the Chameleon: Counterfactual Decoupling for Tactical OOD Shifts in Live Streaming Risk Assessment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02946)
*Yiran Qiao,Jing Chen,Jiaqi Xu,Yang Liu,Qiwei Zhong,Xiang Ao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对直播平台中恶意用户不断改变表达方式以规避检测的难题，本文提出了LPCD框架，利用潜在因果建模和反事实一致性约束，从动态的叙事包装中提取稳定的恶意意图，实现了更鲁棒的风险评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直播平台面临严重的“战术性分布外（OOD）偏移”问题，即恶意主体通过不断变换叙事包装来规避检测，而现有的OOD泛化方法在应对这种意图与策略紧密耦合且缺乏清晰因果关系的环境时存在明显局限。

Method: 提出了一种名为LPCD（潜在预测反事实解耦）的插件式框架。该方法在潜变量空间对“恶意意图”和“叙事策略变体”进行建模，强制执行潜在反事实一致性以聚焦于稳定的恶意意图，并在推理阶段应用轻量级的无参数校准来进一步消除策略偏移。

Result: 在工业级大规模数据集及线上生产流量的实验中，LPCD在风险识别准确率和泛化能力上均显著优于现有的前沿基准方法，有效提升了直播内容风控应对进化型对抗风险的能力。

Conclusion: LPCD通过引入潜在因果视角和潜变量层面的反事实推理，成功解决了直播风控中因恶意策略变体导致的分布外偏移问题，为处理复杂的对抗性风险提供了一种鲁棒的解决方案。

Abstract: Live streaming has emerged as a primary medium for social interaction and digital commerce, yet it is increasingly plagued by sophisticated risks. A fundamental challenge in this domain is \emph{tactical out-of-distribution (OOD) shift}: while malicious actors maintain stable underlying objectives, they continuously redesign narrative packaging to evade detection. Such adversarial shifts expose critical limitations of existing OOD generalization paradigms, whose assumptions are difficult to satisfy in the presence of tightly coupled intent-tactic evolution and ill-defined raw-level counterfactuals.
  In this paper, we tackle this issue from a \emph{latent causal} perspective and propose \underline{L}atent-\underline{P}redictive \underline{C}ounterfactual \underline{D}ecoupling~(LPCD), a plug-in framework for robust live streaming risk assessment. LPCD enables counterfactual reasoning under adversarial tactical re-packaging by modeling intent and narrative variation at the latent level, and enforces \emph{latent counterfactual consistency} to anchor risk prediction on causally stable malicious intent. At inference time, LPCD applies a lightweight, parameter-free calibration to further mitigate tactic-induced distribution shifts. Extensive experiments on large-scale industrial datasets and online production traffic demonstrate that LPCD consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines, validating its effectiveness in moderating evolving adversarial risks in real-world live streaming. The project page is available at https://qiaoyran.github.io/LiveStreamingRiskAssessment/.

</details>


### [114] [BYORn: Bootstrap Your Own Responses to Defend Large Vision-Language Models Against Backdoor Attacks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02947)
*Ivan Sabolić,Marin Oršić,Josip Šarić,Sven Lončarić*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对视觉语言模型在微调阶段易受后门攻击的问题，本文提出 BYORn 框架，通过识别并动态修正语义不一致的训练样本来切断触发器与后门输出的关联，在保障正常任务性能的前提下有效提升了模型的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视觉语言模型在监督微调阶段极易遭受后门攻击，且现有的防御手段在开放式生成场景下效果不佳。作者观察到后门攻击的目标响应通常与图像-文本输入及预训练模型的预期语义不匹配，因此试图通过利用这种语义偏差来防御攻击。

Method: 提出了一种名为 BYORn 的微调框架。该方法利用预训练模型评估输入与目标输出之间的语义一致性，自动识别并替换语义上不合理的（即中毒的）目标响应，从而切断触发器与错误输出之间的相关性，并通过优化人口风险上界的经验估计来实现鲁棒微调。

Result: 实验表明，BYORn 在显著提升模型对后门攻击防御能力的同时，几乎不损失模型在正常任务上的性能，在鲁棒性和泛化能力之间建立了新的平衡点，且对专门针对该防御设计的自适应攻击具有强抵御作用。

Conclusion: BYORn 提供了一种对抗视觉语言模型后门攻击的有效框架，通过修正语义不一致的标注，显著改善了模型在保持正常任务性能的同时对后门攻击的鲁棒性，并在面对自适应攻击时展现了卓越的防御能力。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning is the predominant approach for adapting autoregressive vision-language models to downstream tasks. Recent work has shown that this paradigm is highly vulnerable to backdoor attacks, and that existing defenses are ineffective in open-ended generation settings. In response, we propose BYORn, a backdoor-robust fine-tuning framework motivated by the observation that poisoned target responses are often semantically implausible given the corresponding image-text inputs and a pretrained model. BYORn identifies such misaligned responses and dynamically replaces them with alternative responses generated by the model, thereby breaking the correlation between triggers and target outputs. The resulting objective gradient corresponds to the gradient of the empirical estimate of the population risk upper bound over the clean data distribution. Empirically, BYORn consistently improves robustness to backdoor attacks while preserving clean-task performance, establishing a new trade-off frontier between generalization and attack success rate. Finally, we demonstrate that BYORn remains effective against adaptive attacks specifically designed to circumvent the proposed defense.

### [115] [From Non-Convex to Strongly Convex: Curvature-Adaptive FTPL for Online Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02948)
*Moses Charikar,Chirag Pabbaraju,Ambuj Tewari*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种曲率自适应的FTPL算法，通过动态调整扰动尺度，使得在线非凸优化在保持$O(\sqrt{T})$最差情况性能的同时，能够根据累积曲率实现更快的$O(\log T)$收敛速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的FTPL算法在非凸优化中虽能实现$O(\sqrt{T})$的遗憾，但无法利用损失函数的曲率信息。该研究旨在实现一种无需预先知道曲率积累情况即可在非凸设定下达到曲率自适应的优化方法。

Method: 提出了一种改进的FTPL（Follow-the-Perturbed-Leader）算法。该方法用随时间变化的扰动尺度替代了标准FTPL中的固定尺度，并引入了一种基于“追随领导者”（Follow-the-Leader）原则的调节规则，仅依赖历史信息来动态更新该尺度。

Result: 该算法在任意非凸Lipschitz损失下均能达到$O(\sqrt{T})$遗憾；当累积曲率线性增长时，在充足的预言机精度下可达到$O(\log T)$遗憾。此外，文中给出了对应的下界，证明了该性能权衡的本质属性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了在非凸优化框架下，基于FTPL的曲率自适应算法在理论上是可行的，并确立了非凸损失函数下的遗憾界限与曲率驱动的快速收敛速率之间的内在权衡关系。

Abstract: Curvature adaptivity is a classical theme in online optimization: for convex Lipschitz losses, adaptive methods interpolate between the optimal $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret for general convex losses and $O(\log T)$ regret under strong convexity. Recent work has shown that Follow-the-Perturbed-Leader (FTPL) achieves optimal $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret even for online non-convex Lipschitz losses, assuming access to an approximate offline-optimization oracle, but these guarantees do not exploit curvature. We show that FTPL can be made curvature-adaptive in the non-convex setting, without knowing in advance how curvature will accumulate over time. Our algorithm replaces the fixed perturbation scale of standard FTPL with a time-varying scale chosen using only past information. We give a simple follow-the-leader tuning rule for this scale and show that it competes, up to constants, with the best choice in hindsight. The resulting method achieves $O(\sqrt{T})$ regret for arbitrary non-convex Lipschitz losses and improves as cumulative curvature grows; with sufficiently accurate oracle calls, it achieves $O(\log T)$ regret when cumulative curvature grows linearly, which includes the classical strongly convex regime. We complement these upper bounds with matching lower bounds for prescribed cumulative-curvature sequences, already for one-dimensional convex losses, showing that the tradeoff between worst-case non-convex regret and curvature-driven fast rates is intrinsic.

</details>


### [116] [Gate AI: LLM Security Benchmark Evaluation Methodology and Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02959)
*Ryle Goehausen,Marcus Sousa*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对当前LLM安全检测器评估中常见的“针对性阈值优化”偏差，本文提出了一种基于全局标准化阈值和多维度交叉验证的评估框架，显著提升了跨数据集性能评估的客观性与公平性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有大语言模型（LLM）的提示注入和越狱检测器评估存在两项系统性缺陷：一是过度依赖针对特定数据集的阈值优化（导致过拟合），二是工作点（operating points）不透明，导致难以客观衡量检测器的通用性能。

Method: 研究提出了一套全面的评估工具（harness），核心包括：1. 采用5折交叉验证（StratifiedKFold及考虑近重复数据的StratifiedGroupKFold）；2. 强制使用跨数据集的单一全局工作点（基于FPR ≤ 1%的最大F1值）；3. 实施包含留一法交叉验证、对抗验证、长度偏置分析等在内的多维度诊断电池。

Result: 该方法在16个基准测试（共12,111个样本）上实现了标准化评估，通过严格的阈值对齐确保了与同类检测器在相同误报率下的公平对比，有效揭示了现有模型在泛化能力及鲁棒性上的真实性能。

Conclusion: 该研究通过建立严谨的评估框架，纠正了当前大语言模型安全检测器评估中存在的阈值调优偏差和数据泄露问题，为评估通用安全检测能力提供了一套公平且标准化的范式。

Abstract: Published evaluations of prompt-injection and jailbreak detectors for Large Language Models often suffer from two systematic weaknesses: per-dataset threshold tuning and undisclosed operating points. We describe an evaluation harness that addresses both. The detector under evaluation is scored across 16 public benchmarks (12,111 samples) using 5-fold cross-validation. StratifiedKFold (by row) is the headline pass; a parallel StratifiedGroupKFold pass over a composite key (parent-prompt id plus MinHash + LSH near-duplicate clusters at Jaccard $\gtrsim 0.8$) runs alongside it as a leakage-premium diagnostic. A single global operating point is selected on the held-out folds (max F1 subject to FPR $\leq 1\%$) and applied uniformly to every dataset, so per-dataset results reflect one threshold rather than per-benchmark optimisation. Generalisation is examined through a battery of diagnostics (leave-one-dataset-out cross-validation, a random-label control, adversarial validation, permutation feature importance, length-bias correlation, classifier-head agreement, cross-source near-duplicate detection, threshold transferability, train-vs-OOF agreement, and a paraphrase-invariance probe), most with a quantitative pass threshold and the remainder with a stated failure mode. For every external comparison, the detector's threshold is re-tuned to the competitor's published false-positive rate so head-to-head values are evaluated at matched operating points.
