### [117] [KForge: LLM-Driven Cross-Platform Kernel Generation for AI Accelerators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02963)
*Taras Sereda,Burak Bartan,Ankita Nayak,Tom St. John,Natalie Serrino,Zain Asgar*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: KForge 是一个基于双 LLM 代理协作的自动化内核生成框架，通过迭代反馈闭环，实现了面向多种硬件后端的算子内核自动合成与性能优化，显著提升了推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在生产环境的智能体流水线中，针对异构加速器的算子内核需求日益增长。传统手动编写算子内核耗时耗力且难以扩展，而现有基于 LLM 的自动化方案在低级代码生成和跨后端泛化方面仍存在不足。因此，需要一种能够高效生成高性能、跨平台算子内核的自动化框架。

Method: 提出 KForge 框架，采用两个协作的 LLM 代理：一个是负责生成和迭代优化代码的“生成代理”（通过编译和正确性反馈进行迭代）；另一个是负责解析性能分析数据并给出改进建议的“性能分析代理”。框架通过函数功能校验阶段（确保正确性）和性能优化阶段（通过融合算子、混合精度等手段逼近人工手写性能）交替进行，实现了跨平台的自动内核合成。

Result: 在 NVIDIA B200 上，KForge 在 gpt-oss-20b 推理基准测试中比 TensorRT-LLM 提升了 2.12% 的吞吐量；在 Intel Arc B580 上，对于 KernelBench Level 2 的 37 个负载，KForge 生成的 Triton 内核实现了比 PyTorch Eager 和 torch.compile 快 5.13 倍的几何平均加速。

Conclusion: KForge 证明了基于 LLM 的协作代理机制在自动化内核生成和优化方面的潜力，能够有效降低跨硬件平台的内核开发门槛，并在多后端环境下实现优于人工编写或现有编译器的性能表现。

Abstract: Production inference increasingly targets a heterogeneous mix of accelerators. Agentic pipelines interleave reasoning, tool calls, and multi-agent coordination, each with distinct compute and memory profiles. For optimal efficiency, each stage should run on the accelerator best suited to it. This creates a systems challenge: each pipeline now requires high-performance kernels across a growing set of hardware backends and programming models. Writing these kernels by hand is time-consuming, demands deep low-level expertise, and does not scale as kernel complexity grows. Recently, Large Language Models (LLMs) have been leveraged for automatic kernel generation, but challenges in low-level code generation and cross-backend generalization persist. We present KForge, a cross-platform framework built around an iterative refinement loop driven by two collaborating LLM-based agents: a generation agent that produces and progressively refines kernels using compilation and correctness feedback, and a performance-analysis agent that interprets profiling data, from programmatic APIs to GUI-based tools, and emits recommendations that steer the next round of synthesis. The loop alternates between functional passes, which drive a candidate to correctness, and optimization passes, which close the performance gap to hand-tuned baselines. We evaluate KForge on two backends with very different baseline reference availability. On NVIDIA B200, KForge achieves a 2.12$\%$ improvement in end-to-end throughput compared to TensorRT-LLM on the gpt-oss-20b inference speed benchmark. On Intel Arc B580, KForge generates Triton kernels achieving a 5.13$\times$ geometric mean speedup over the faster of PyTorch eager and torch.compile on 37 GEMM + tail-ops workloads from KernelBench Level 2, primarily via operator fusion and mixed-precision execution.

### [118] [Neural Networks Provably Learn Spectral Representations for Group Composition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02993)
*Jianliang He,Leda Wang,Fengzhuo Zhang,Siyu Chen,Zhuoran Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过表示论分析了神经网络学习群运算的机制，揭示了训练动力学如何引导神经元自发地向不可约表示对齐，并以指数级收敛速率实现低秩特征压缩与多数投票决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解神经网络在训练过程中如何自发形成结构化的内部表示。作者试图通过群论和表示论的视角，揭示神经网络在解决有限群组成任务时，其动力学行为背后的数学机制与特征学习规律。

Method: 1. 将神经网络在有限群组成任务上的投影梯度流提升至傅里叶域。
2. 利用表示论中的能量泛函，分析其黎曼梯度上升动力学。
3. 对阿贝尔群进行人口层级的完整描述，并证明了随机初始化如何诱导哈尔均匀相位分布。

2. 发现了一种矩阵值群表示的新型低秩压缩现象。
3. 对于阿贝尔群，证明了随机初始化能促进不同非平凡表示间的均匀多样化，并通过多数投票机制近似指示函数。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了神经网络在学习有限群运算时，通过傅里叶变换下的黎曼梯度流机制，实现了向不可约表示的自发对齐与竞争。该理论框架不仅阐明了特征学习的表示论基础，还证明了神经网络通过低秩压缩和多数投票机制有效地近似了群的代数结构，并具有指数级的收敛特性。

Abstract: Understanding how structured internal structure emerges during neural network training is central to the study of deep learning. We investigate this phenomenon through the group composition task, where a two-layer neural network is trained to predict $g_1 \star g_2$ for elements of a finite group $G$. By lifting the projected gradient flow to the Fourier domain, we demonstrate that the training dynamics are governed by a Riemannian gradient ascent on a representation-theoretic energy functional. We prove that, under random initialization, this flow drives each neuron to converge almost surely toward a single irreducible representation, while the cross-layer Fourier coefficients achieve a rotational rank-one alignment. This framework provides a representation-theoretic account of feature learning and characterizes a novel low-rank compression phenomenon for matrix-valued group representations. Moreover, for Abelian groups, we provide a complete population-level description: random initialization promotes uniform diversification across nontrivial representations and induces Haar-uniform phases, jointly approximating the indicator via a majority-vote mechanism. We further prove that both phase alignment and representation competition emerge with exponential convergence rates.

### [119] [CoughSense: Five-Class Respiratory Disease Classification via Whisper Encoder Fine-Tuning and Dual-Encoder Cross-Attention Fusion with Balanced Contrastive Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02998)
*Nikhil Vincent*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自动咳嗽分析研究大多局限于二分类（如 COVID-19 检测），缺乏能够区分多种呼吸系统疾病的实用工具；同时，利用通用语音预训练模型（如 Whisper）处理短促的咳嗽录音时，存在音频片段过短导致的“静音稀释”问题。

Method: 1. 采用 OpenAI Whisper 作为特征提取主干；2. 创新设计了“主动帧 QKV 注意力池化”，将注意力限制在编码器输出的前 200 个 token，以应对短音频在长输入窗口中的静音稀释问题；3. 采用了多种处理不平衡数据与领域偏移的技术，包括加权随机采样、SpecAugment、平衡混合增强、监督对比辅助损失、FiLM 症状条件化以及梯度反转领域自适应；4. 构建了双编码器模型，通过交叉注意力融合 Whisper 与 OPERA-CT 呼吸基础模型。

Conclusion: CoughSense 通过引入主动帧 QKV 注意力池化机制（Active-frame QKV attention pooling），有效解决了长音频预训练模型在处理短音频任务时的“静音稀释”问题，证明了利用现有语音大模型底座结合针对性优化，能够以低成本实现多类呼吸系统疾病的精准自动筛查。

Abstract: Automated cough analysis offers a path to low-cost respiratory screening, but most existing work stops at binary COVID-19 detection. A practical tool needs to tell apart several respiratory conditions from one cough recording on a consumer smartphone. We present CoughSense, a system that sorts cough recordings into five classes. These are healthy, COVID-19, asthma or respiratory condition, bronchitis, and pneumonia. We aggregated 18,301 recordings from four public datasets (Coswara, CoughVID, Virufy, and the West China Hospital Pediatric Cough Dataset) and used the OpenAI Whisper encoder as a pretrained backbone for cough disease classification. The main contribution is active-frame QKV attention pooling, which restricts attention to the first 200 of 1500 encoder tokens. This avoids the silence-dilution problem that arises because a 3-second cough fills only 150 tokens of Whisper's 30-second input window. Other training parts handle the 19 to 1 class imbalance and the four-dataset domain shift. These include WeightedRandomSampler, SpecAugment, Balanced Mixup with forced minority pairing, a supervised contrastive auxiliary loss, FiLM symptom conditioning, and gradient-reversal domain adaptation. A dual-encoder model fuses Whisper with the OPERA-CT respiratory foundation model through cross-attention. CoughSense (Whisper-tiny, 8.6M parameters) reached 82.3 percent balanced accuracy on five-fold cross-validation (macro-F1 of 0.817, AUC of 0.941). It beat an ImageNet-pretrained EfficientNet-B2 by 11.1 points and a ViT trained from scratch by 29.6 points. All five classes passed 74 percent recall and four of five passed 80 percent. The dual-encoder model reached 85.4 percent balanced accuracy. Active-frame pooling is the largest single contributor across all ablation components at 5.1 points, which should help any short-audio task using Whisper as a backbone.

### [120] [How Quantization Changes Interpretable Features: A Sparse Autoencoder Analysis of Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03002)
*Evan Duan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了大模型量化会对模型内部的可解释性特征造成隐蔽性损伤，即便模型在外部任务指标（如困惑度）上表现良好，其内部结构也可能已发生退化。因此，仅基于行为层面的性能评估不足以保证模型在量化后仍保持原有的可解释性，必须进行特征层面的审计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量化是部署大语言模型的标准方法，通常仅关注困惑度或下游准确率。然而，这些指标无法反映模型内部的可解释性特征（如SAE提取的特征）在量化后是否依然有效，这对于依赖特征工程的安全审计和模型干预至关重要。本文旨在探究全精度模型中的稀疏特征在量化后是否仍具备鲁棒性。

Method: 以稀疏自编码器（SAE）作为固定的测量基准，通过皮尔逊相关系数对比全精度模型与量化模型（RTN，INT4-INT8范围）在相同输入下的激活特征。研究使用Pythia-70M和Gemma-2-2B模型，并分析了特征存活率与全精度模型统计数据之间的关系，以及量化与模型剪枝之间的关联。

Result: 1. 特征存活呈现渐进式退化，而非突然失效；在INT6精度下，Pythia-70M和Gemma-2-2B分别只有62.4%和51.3%的特征存活。2. 存活情况可根据全精度统计数据预测（AUC高达0.92-0.97）。3. 任务指标会误导评估：在某些情况下（如Gemma-2-2B的INT7量化），困惑度提升但仍有18.7%的特征受损。4. 量化与幅值剪枝损害的特征集高度重合，说明两者存在类似的压缩脆弱性。

Conclusion: 单纯依靠困惑度等下游任务指标来评估量化模型的质量是不够的。研究表明，量化过程会破坏模型内部的可解释性特征，即便在困惑度表现良好甚至提升的情况下，大量特征仍会受损。因此，在进行大模型部署的压缩过程中，必须引入特征层面的可解释性审计。

Abstract: Quantization is a standard path to deploying large language models, and a quantized model is typically judged acceptable when its perplexity or downstream accuracy stays close to the full-precision original. Whether the model still computes in the same way, or whether the interpretable features identified in the full-precision model survive weight rounding, is rarely tested, even as safety audits and steering interventions increasingly rely on those features. We ask whether sparse autoencoder (SAE) features extracted from a dense full-precision model remain faithful once that model is quantized. Using a frozen SAE as a fixed measurement basis, we encode full-precision and round-to-nearest (RTN) quantized activations on identical tokens and quantify per-feature survival by Pearson correlation, sweeping bit-widths from INT8 to INT4 on Pythia-70M and Gemma-2-2B. We find that feature survival is graded: features degrade systematically rather than failing all at once, with 62.4 percent of active features surviving at INT6 on Pythia-70M and 51.3 percent surviving at INT6 on Gemma-2-2B, and with most non-survivors blurred rather than destroyed. Survival is predictable from full-precision statistics alone, with cross-validated AUCs of 0.92 to 0.97 and peak activation as the strongest marginal predictor. Critically, task metrics can miss this damage: on Gemma-2-2B, INT7 improves perplexity while degrading 18.7 percent of features. Finally, quantization and matched-perplexity magnitude pruning damage strongly overlapping feature sets, with Jaccard overlap of 0.79 to 0.86 and damage-score Spearman correlation of 0.98, suggesting a shared mode of compression-induced vulnerability. These results show that behavioral parity is insufficient evidence that interpretability findings transfer to quantized deployments, motivating feature-level audits of compression.

### [121] [Exact equivariance, kept through training, buys zero-shot generalisation across the symmetry group](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03003)
*Hongbo Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入等变性（Equivariance）构建潜在世界模型，实现了动力学预测在群变换下的数学精确不变性。相比于依赖暴力计算的传统方法，该方法显著提升了模型在分布外任务的泛化能力和多步预测的稳定性，证明了等变归纳偏置在处理物理动力系统时的核心价值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统世界模型在处理具有群对称性的物理动力系统时，通常需要大量数据和模型参数来“学习”对称性，且在分布外（OOD）表现较差。该研究旨在利用群论中的等变性（Equivariance）作为归纳偏置，实现模型对物理规律的更本质理解，从而提高样本效率、泛化能力及预测精度。

Method: 本文提出了一种由等变编码器（Equivariant Encoder）和等变预测器（Equivariant Predictor）构成的潜在世界模型。该方法利用群 $G$ 在潜在空间上的正交表示 $\rho(g)$，通过在受限的方位切片上拟合动力学，从而在数学上确定整个轨道上的动力学。研究通过引入等变规划器（Equivariant Planner）将该等变性扩展至闭环控制系统。实验对比了包括数据增强、暴力缩放（Scaling）和软等变在内的多种基准方法。

Result: 实验结果表明：1. 等变模型在训练后能保持极高的等变残差（$\sim 10^{-6}$）；2. 在分布外任务上，等变模型表现优于基准模型（2D下误差缩小约13.8倍，3D下达157倍），且模型尺寸更小；3. 在闭环控制中，等变模型保持了几乎浮点精度级别的平移不变性，且在多步（$H$-fold）展开中误差不随步数累积。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了构建等变世界模型（Equivariant World Models）不仅能实现理论上的对称性，还能在实际训练中保持极高的精度。这种方法通过利用动力系统的群对称性，实现了“举一反三”的效果，显著优于传统的非等变基准模型，并在多步预测中保持了极高的稳定性，避开了通过暴力增加数据或参数来补偿对称性缺失的途径。

Abstract: A latent world model built from an equivariant encoder $E$ and an equivariant predictor $f$ inherits a provable symmetry of its training loss: when the world's dynamics genuinely carries a group $G$ acting on latents by an orthogonal representation $ρ(g)$, the one-step prediction relMSE is exactly invariant across the whole group, so fitting the dynamics on a restricted slice of orientations mathematically determines it on the entire orbit (jǔ yī fǎn sān). We verify this end-to-end at laptop scale (CPU/MPS, fully seeded). [A] The symmetry survives a real Muon/AdamW + EMA + VICReg run -- composed encode-then-predict residual $\sim 10^{-6}$ after optimisation, not just at initialisation, and under any optimiser. [B] One-step error is flat to five digits across the group, while a same-hypothesis-class non-equivariant baseline fits the slice but breaks out-of-distribution (VN $\times 1.00$ vs baseline $\times 13.8$ in 2D, $\times 17.2$ in 3D, $\times 157$ over the full $\mathrm{SE}(3)$ ladder), with the equivariant model $4.5$-$7.4\times$ smaller. [C] The same isometry argument lifts to closed loop: under a matching equivariant planner the control trajectory at orientation $g$ is exactly $ρ(g)$ applied to the seen one, so closed-loop error is invariant across the group -- float-floor-exact in 2D/$\mathrm{SO}(2)$ on real PushT and statistically flat in 3D/$\mathrm{SE}(3)$ (disjoint 95% CIs). We stress-test the prior against Sutton's Bitter Lesson: augmentation, brute-force scale, and soft-equivariance each close at most the across-group task metric, never the float-floor exactness. Because equivariance is closed under composition, the $H$-fold rollout stays flat ($\times 1.00$, $\le 2\times 10^{-7}$) at every horizon, while the baseline's residual compounds with $H$. Out of scope: task-success sweeps, planner-free invariance, and scaling.

</details>


### [122] [MOSAIC: Efficient Mixture-of-Agent Scheduling via Adaptive Aggregation and Inference Concurrency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03014)
*Saptarshi Mitra,Yifan Zhang,Rachid Karami,Phyo Pyae Moe Aung,Nazmul Takbir,Sreetama Sarkar,Souvik Kundu,Sitao Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: MOSAIC 是一款针对 MoA（智能体混合）工作负载的调度框架，通过 ILP 优化资源部署与自适应聚合技术，解决了负载不均导致的 GPU 资源瓶颈，在保证精度的前提下显著提升了系统吞吐量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 MoA（智能体混合）系统在 GPU 资源有限时，受制于技能导向路由带来的负载倾斜以及不同模型间差异巨大的生成长度，导致严重的 GPU 空转和吞吐量下降。因此，需要一种专门针对 MoA 工作负载的调度框架以提高资源利用效率。

Method: 1. 基于整数线性规划（ILP）的调度器：根据离线分析的成本数据，优化专家模型的部署位置及任务分配，通过对计算密集型专家进行复制并固定轻量级专家来平衡负载；2. 置信度感知自适应聚合：通过评估专家间的共识程度，跳过昂贵的最终聚合模型，减少不必要的计算开销。

Result: 在 4-GPU 系统测试中，相比基准调度方案，MOSAIC 在专家阶段实现了最高 2.5 倍的加速，聚合阶段实现了 4.23 倍的加速，整体端到端速度提升 1.7 至 2.3 倍，且精度下降不超过 0.1 个百分点。

Conclusion: MOSAIC 通过联合优化调度策略与自适应聚合机制，解决了 MoA 系统中因专家负载不均及推理长度差异导致的资源浪费问题，显著提升了推理吞吐量，同时保持了模型精度，为大规模代理系统的高效部署提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Mixture-of-Agents (MoA) systems improve reasoning accuracy by routing each query to multiple expert LLMs and aggregating their outputs. Efficiently executing this workload on limited GPU resources has bottlenecks. Skill-based routing creates skewed expert demand, and combining instruction-tuned LLMs with long-reasoning models results in extreme variability in generation lengths. Consequently, traditional scheduling strategies suffer from significant GPU idling and throughput collapse due to load imbalances. We present MOSAIC, a scheduling framework to accelerate MoA workloads. First, we formulate an Integer Linear Program (ILP) based scheduler that jointly optimizes expert placement and per-worker prompt assignment from offline-profiled costs, replicating reasoning experts across workers while pinning lightweight ones. Second, MOSAIC uses confidence-aware adaptive aggregation, leveraging inter-expert agreement to bypass the heavy final aggregator LLM for consensus queries. In our 4-GPU system, MOSAIC achieves up to 2.5x expert-stage, 4.23x aggregator-stage and 1.7~2.3x end-to-end speedups over the baseline scheduler, while matching accuracy within 0.1pp.

</details>


### [123] [ConTraIRL: Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03017)
*Yikang Gui,Bikramjit Banerjee,Prashant Doshi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: ConTraIRL 是一种通过对比学习实现环境动力学与目标特征解耦的逆强化学习框架，能够有效支持在未知环境组合下的奖励函数迁移，提升了智能体的泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在现有的逆强化学习方法中，当环境动力学和任务目标发生变化时，奖励函数的迁移表现往往不可靠。为了实现更鲁棒、更具组合性的奖励迁移，需要从潜在空间中解耦并独立建模这两个因素。

Method: 提出了名为“ConTraIRL”的框架，采用双编码器架构，利用双重对比学习目标，分别提取环境动力学特征和任务目标特征。通过时间对齐技术，确保动力学编码器不受目标影响，而目标编码器不受动力学影响，从而实现两者在潜在空间中的解耦。

Result: 在连续控制任务基准测试中，ConTraIRL 在未见的动力学-目标组合上实现了有效的少样本迁移，且在样本效率和奖励恢复指标上均优于现有的迁移逆强化学习基准方法。

Conclusion: ConTraIRL 通过对环境动力学和任务目标进行解耦建模，成功解决了逆强化学习中奖励函数在面对未知环境与目标组合时的泛化难题，为复杂环境下的智能体迁移学习提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Reward transfer in Inverse Reinforcement Learning (IRL) is unreliable when policies must generalize to unseen combinations of environment dynamics and task goals. We propose Factorized Contrastive Abstractions for Transferable IRL (ConTraIRL), a framework that enables compositional reward transfer by learning decoupled latent representations of these two factors. ConTraIRL uses a dual-encoder architecture that maps observations into separate dynamics and goal latent spaces, trained with a dual contrastive objective. Temporal alignment encourages the dynamics encoder to learn goal-invariant structure, while the goal encoder captures dynamics-invariant features. This factorization supports reward inference under recombined dynamics-goal settings. Experiments on continuous control benchmarks demonstrate effective few-shot transfer to unseen dynamics-goal pairings, improving sample efficiency and reward recovery over transfer IRL baselines.

### [124] [Will Accurate Fields Mislead Photonic Design? FromGlobal Accuracy to Port Readout](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03038)
*Yitian Zhang,Yonghong chen,Youming Chen,Yiyang Li,Xing Zhe,Renhe Lu,Shaolin Liao,Yuzhe Ma,Zhong Guan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对光子器件设计中“全局场准确但局部读数失准”的问题，本文提出了PaNO及其变体，通过将模型架构与物理传播和端口读出特性对齐，大幅提升了代理模型对实际设计指标的预测准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经场代理模型在全局场误差评估上表现良好，但在实际光子器件（如MMI分束器和耦合器）设计中，决策往往依赖于局部端口读数。这类模型容易产生“场-设计失配”问题，即全局场预测看似准确，却无法准确反映器件的功率分配和相位特征，导致候选器件排名失真。

Method: 研究提出了“场/中介/读出”（Field/Mediator/Readout）的评估框架，以区分全局复杂场误差与传播剖面及输出窗口误差。基于此，设计了传播对齐神经算子（PaNO），该模型将潜状态组织为局部边界结构、横向模态内容、轴向传播及交叉模态交互。此外，还提出了针对端口区域残余场的输出感知反馈变体PaNO-R2。

Result: 在15波长的3×3 MMI基准测试中，PaNO在cMAE略高的情况下，将端口功率误差从0.2018降低至0.0739。PaNO-R2进一步优化了各项指标，相较于基线模型NeurOLight，将端口功率误差和输出剖面误差分别降低了72.7%和72.5%。

Conclusion: 该研究证明，在光子器件设计中，仅依赖全局场误差指标（如cMAE）不足以评估代理模型的有效性。通过引入针对传播特征和端口输出窗口优化的模型（如PaNO和PaNO-R2），可以显著提升代理模型在实际设计指标（如端口功率）上的预测精度，从而更准确地进行候选器件排名。

Abstract: Neural field surrogates can accelerate photonic design loops, but a surrogate that looks accurate in global field error can still mis-rank candidate devices when the final decision depends on localized output-port readouts. This risk is acute in propagation-dominated MMI splitters and couplers, where port power, splitting, phase, and coupling are determined by accumulated modal interference and output-window aggregation rather than by average field similarity alone. We study this field-to-design mismatch through a Field/Mediator/Readout view that separates dense complex-field error from propagation-profile and output-window errors before port aggregation. To align the surrogate with this chain, we propose PaNO, a propagation-aligned neural operator that keeps the full-field prediction interface while organizing latent states around local boundary structure, transverse modal content, axial propagation, and cross-mode interaction. We also evaluate PaNO-R2, an output-aware feedback variant for residual field components near the port region. On a 15-wavelength tunable $3{\times}3$ MMI benchmark with 4608 held-out fields, PaNO lowers NeurOLight's port-power error from 0.2018 to 0.0739 despite slightly higher cMAE, showing that global field accuracy alone is not sufficient for design-relevant readout fidelity. PaNO-R2 attains the best cMAE, propagation-profile error, output-profile error, and port-power error, reducing NeurOLight's port-power and output-profile errors by 72.7\% and 72.5\%.

*Seungu Kang,Songkuk Kim*

Abstract: Knowledge Distillation (KD) is a powerful tool for model compression, yet the precise mechanisms by which student models acquire feature representations remain underexplored. In this work, we analyze student feature learning using the Interaction Tensor framework. Our analysis reveals that effective KD acts as a regularizer that prunes low-frequency, sample-specific features, encouraging the student to rely on a compact set of highly reusable features. Crucially, we observe that the dataset-level confusion matrix contains structural information analogous to the teacher's "Dark Knowledge." Leveraging this insight, we propose Confusion Distillation (CD), a teacher-free self-distillation method that utilizes the model's own evolving confusion patterns as dynamic soft targets. CD achieves competitive performance on ResNet-34 and ResNet-50 for CIFAR-100, outperforming existing self-distillation methods like CS-KD and PS-KD by 1.2% while offering a computationally efficient alternative to standard KD.

### [126] [Rethinking Molecular Text Representations for LLMs: An Empirical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03057)
*Arun Raja,Garrett M. Morris,Kian Ming A. Chai*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究通过对比 16 个 LLM 在 9 种分子表示法下的表现，揭示了分子表示法对化学任务性能的决定性影响，证明了没有一种“万能”表示法，并建议未来应根据任务类型动态选择表示法，而非仅依赖 SMILES。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管大语言模型在分子任务中的应用日益广泛，但目前学术界对于“哪种分子表示法最适合 LLM 处理化学任务”仍缺乏明确结论。现有的研究往往过度依赖 SMILES，且缺乏跨模型、跨表示法的系统性评估，这限制了 LLM 在化学领域的性能优化和深入应用。

Method: 研究团队通过系统性基准测试，评估了 16 种大语言模型在 9 种不同分子表示法（包括 SMILES、CML、MolJSON、InChI、IUPAC 等）和 8 项化学任务上的表现。此外，通过标记化审计（tokenization audits）、线性探测（linear probes）和注意力机制分析，深入探究了不同分子表示法在模型内部的编码机制和处理差异。

Result: 1. 性能具有高度的表示法依赖性，没有一种表示法能在所有任务中胜出；2. CML 和 MolJSON 在结构任务中表现最优，IUPAC 在语义任务（如分子检索）中表现最为突出；3. 尽管 SMILES 在预训练中最为普遍，但在多数任务中并非最优选择；4. 化学专业模型在处理 SMILES 时性能优异，但面对结构化文本表示时性能显著下降，表明其泛化能力不足；5. 内部机制研究表明，模型处理不同分子表示法时的注意力分配和编码模式存在显著差异。

Conclusion: 本研究强调了在化学任务中不存在“通用的最优分子表示法”。研究指出，依赖单一表示法（如 SMILES）的评估会造成偏差，限制了模型的通用性。未来的 LLM 化学应用应采取“任务感知表示路由”（task-aware representation routing）策略，根据具体任务需求动态选择最合适的分子表示法，以充分发挥模型性能。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly used for molecular tasks, but it remains unclear which molecular representation to use. We present a systematic benchmark evaluating LLM molecular competence across nine representations and eight chemical tasks. We benchmark 16 LLMs across five model families, including reasoning and non-reasoning variants, chemistry-specialized LLMs, and closed frontier models. Performance is strongly representation-dependent and no single representation wins across tasks, though CML is the best, followed by MolJSON, InChI, and then canonical SMILES. Explicit structured text representations (CML and MolJSON) dominate structural tasks; IUPAC dominates semantic tasks, winning molecule retrieval for all 16 LLMs; and SMILES variants are rarely optimal despite their prevalence in pretraining. Chemistry-specialized models perform well with SMILES at the cost of large degradations with structured text representations, suggesting SMILES-only evaluation rewards specialization that does not generalize. Using LLM-as-a-judge, we find that IUPAC produces the highest fraction of correct molecule generations. A mechanistic study via tokenization audits, linear probes and attention shows that representations are encoded differently inside the model; for example, structured representations require higher attention across the molecular span. Our results argue against representation-invariant evaluation and motivate task-aware representation routing for LLM-based chemistry.

### [127] [Learn When and Where to Connect: Adaptive Virtual Nodes for Dynamic Message Passing on Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03068)
*Jaejun Lee,Joyce Jiyoung Whang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对现有MPNN中虚拟节点连接方式固定且受限的问题，本文提出了MAVN框架。该方法通过动态、自适应的节点-虚拟节点连接机制，显著增强了模型的信息传递能力，并在多项基准测试中表现卓越。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于虚拟节点（VN）的消息传递神经网络（MPNN）存在局限性：如连接方式固定且单一、约束所有节点连接相同数量的VN、以及连接过程缺乏对节点间依赖关系的考量。这些限制阻碍了模型捕捉复杂图结构特征的能力。

Method: 提出了一种端到端可微的MPNN框架MAVN。该方法：1. 实现了节点与虚拟节点（VN）之间的非约束连接；2. 在每一层根据节点表征的演变，动态地从候选池中按需选择并引入VN；3. 利用双视角评分机制（衡量节点对VN的偏好以及VN对节点的偏好），实现节点与VN之间的自适应连接。

Result: 在九个真实世界数据集上的实验结果表明，MAVN能持续提升基础MPNN模型的性能，最高提升幅度达46.5%，并在多项任务中优于现有基准方法。理论上，该方法被证明能够模拟任意节点-VN连接模式。

Conclusion: MAVN通过引入动态、非约束的虚拟节点机制，成功克服了传统固定拓扑的局限性，证明了其在增强MPNN表达能力和预测性能方面的显著优势，为复杂图学习任务提供了一种灵活且有效的通用框架。

Abstract: While Virtual Nodes (VNs) are often utilized in Message Passing Neural Networks (MPNNs) to facilitate effective message passing, existing VN-based methods have limitations, such as constraining all nodes to connect to the same number of VNs, fixing the connections before applying MPNNs, and connecting a node to a VN independently of the other nodes that connect to the same VN. We propose MAVN, an end-to-end differentiable MPNN framework that allows non-constrained connections between nodes and VNs and dynamically introduces VNs on demand in response to evolving node representations across layers. Specifically, MAVN learns to adaptively determine when (at which layer) and where (to which nodes) to introduce and connect VNs based on the relative importance of connections. From a pool of candidate VNs, MAVN selects the necessary VNs in each layer, where each selected VN is connected to a nonempty subset of nodes, guided by a dual-perspective scoring mechanism that jointly captures the nodes' preferences for VNs and the VNs' preferences for nodes. We theoretically prove that for any node-VN connectivity pattern, there exists a set of MAVN's parameters that can simulate the pattern. Experiments on nine real-world datasets demonstrate that MAVN consistently improves the performance of backbone MPNNs, achieving up to 46.5% improvement over the backbones and outperforms the baselines.

### [128] [ASymPO: Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization for Asynchronous LLM Post-Training Without Behavior Information](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03070)
*Zehua Liu,Yuxuan Yao,Xiaojin Fu,Tao Zhong,Mingxuan Yuan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 ASymPO 的强化学习算法，通过对损失进行动态尺度归一化，成功解决了异步语言模型后训练中因“陈旧响应”导致的数值不稳定问题，无需依赖复杂的行为策略概率记录。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 异步强化学习虽能提升语言模型后训练的吞吐量，但会引入“陈旧响应”（Stale responses）导致的分布偏移问题。现有的行为纠正方法（如重要性采样或裁剪）对数据一致性要求极高，难以在异步系统中实现。本文旨在探索能否仅利用当前策略的概率来稳定异步强化学习，解决其潜在的尺度不平衡故障模式。

Method: 作者提出了非对称尺度策略优化（Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization, ASymPO）。该方法通过将每个响应的 Token 损失除以该响应在当前策略下的平均 Token 负对数概率进行归一化，从而消除了异步更新中由于策略演进而产生的“尺度不平衡”问题，并重新实现了响应层面的零和优势平衡。此外，文中还引入了固定负缩放基线（Scaled Policy Optimization, SPO）作为对比。

Result: 实验表明，在异步数学推理任务的后训练中，ASymPO 能够成功稳定训练过程，无需行为策略概率即可保持有效的学习信号，并在处理分布偏移时表现出优于传统方法的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: ASymPO 是一种无需行为策略概率即可稳定异步强化学习训练的有效方法。通过将损失项按当前策略的平均负对数概率进行归一化，ASymPO 解决了异步训练中因陈旧响应导致的尺度不平衡问题，为大规模语言模型的高效后训练提供了一种稳健的策略优化方案。

Abstract: Asynchronous reinforcement learning can improve language-model post-training throughput by decoupling response generation from policy optimization, but stale responses introduce distribution drift. Standard behavior-corrected methods control this drift with behavior-policy probabilities, importance ratios, or clipping, which requires token-aligned, versioned, and numerically consistent behavior log-probabilities across rollout and learner systems. We ask whether asynchronous group-relative RL can instead be stabilized using only current-policy probabilities. We identify a scale-imbalance failure mode: when stale responses are evaluated under the current policy, positive and negative loss terms can appear at different negative log-probability scales, so zero-sum advantages no longer imply balanced loss contributions. We propose Asymmetric-Scale Policy Optimization (ASymPO), which normalizes each response's token loss by its current average token negative log-probability. ASymPO requires no behavior-policy probabilities, restores response-level zero-sum balance, and preserves a nonzero learning signal. We also introduce Scaled Policy Optimization (SPO), a fixed negative-scaling baseline, and evaluate both current-policy-only objectives in asynchronous mathematical reasoning post-training.

</details>


### [129] [Efficient Hyperparameter Optimization for LLM Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03073)
*Minping Chen,Bowen Xiao,Du Liang,Chuxuan Zeng,Zeyi Wen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大语言模型强化学习中超参数优化开销巨大的问题，本文提出了 JF-HPO 方法。通过联合调整模型规模与训练预算，并结合代理模型、智能早停和高效检查点技术，大幅提升了优化效率与最终模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型强化学习对超参数高度敏感，但现有的超参数优化方法在面对大规模模型和高昂训练成本时计算效率低下，难以直接应用。

Method: 提出了联合保真度超参数优化 (JF-HPO) 方法，核心包含三个组件：利用目标大模型的轻量级代理模型进行训练评估；基于训练动态的定制化早停策略；以及消除冗余计算的高效检查点机制。

Result: 相比现有方法，JF-HPO 将单次试验的计算效率提升了最高 14.9 倍；在相同时间预算下实现了更好或更具竞争力的准确率，且较 VeRL 配方提升了 5.8% 到 111.6% 的性能。

Conclusion: JF-HPO 证明了联合调整模型规模和训练预算作为保真度，能显著提升大语言模型强化学习中超参数优化的效率。该方法不仅减少了计算开销，还显著超越了现有的超参数调优策略。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs) is highly sensitive to hyperparameter configurations, making hyperparameter optimization (HPO) essential yet computationally expensive. Existing multi-fidelity HPO methods remain inefficient for LLM RL due to the massive model scale and resource-intensive training cycles. In this paper, we propose Joint Fidelity Hyperparameter Optimization (JF-HPO), which simultaneously adapts both model size and training budget as fidelity. JF-HPO is empowered by: (i) it leverages a small proxy model of the target LLM for efficient training and evaluation in each HPO trial; (ii) it integrates carefully designed early-stopping strategies based on training dynamics; (iii) it introduces an efficient checkpointing mechanism to eliminate redundant computations. Compared with existing HPO methods, JF-HPO significantly improves the computational efficiency of each trial (up to 14.9 times), while achieving better or competitive predictive accuracy under the same time budget. Notably, compared with utilizing hyperparameter configurations from the VeRL Recipe, JF-HPO delivers performance improvements ranging from 5.8% to 111.6%.

### [130] [RMPrior: Bridging Propagation Priors and Diffusion Refinement for Efficient Radio Map Construction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03074)
*Zixuan Guo,Xiucheng Wang,Nan Cheng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合物理传播先验与扩散模型的“中间时刻启动”采样策略，在大幅提升无线电地图构建速度的同时，还改善了重构质量并提供了对先验模型质量的评估手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩散模型虽然能够生成高保真的无线电地图，但其迭代去噪的采样过程计算成本极高，难以满足动态无线系统中对地图频繁更新的实时性要求；同时，现有的扩散模型在生成过程中完全忽略了经典的无线传播模型所包含的物理场景信息。

Method: 提出了一种“中间时刻采样”（Mid-start sampling）策略。该方法不再从纯高斯噪声开始去噪，而是将匹配的传播模型先验（Propagation prior）扰动到扩散过程的某个中间时间步，仅利用预训练的扩散模型执行剩余的逆向扩散步骤，从而专注于多径效应的精细化重构。此外，论文还提供了关于初始化误差上界及截断条件下的先验质量敏感性的理论分析。

Result: 在 IRT4HighRes 数据集上的实验表明，当截断比例 $P_{\text{start}}=0.5$ 时，该方法实现了 2.01 倍的推理加速，同时在 NMSE、RMSE、SSIM 和 PSNR 等指标上均优于全步骤基线。实验证实了重建质量与先验质量的正相关性，且该敏感性在截断比例较高时更为显著，与理论推导一致。

Conclusion: 本研究成功证明了将物理传播先验与扩散模型结合的“中间时刻启动”策略是可行的。该方法不仅大幅降低了无线电地图构建的计算开销，还通过有效利用先验知识提高了重建精度，为动态无线环境下的实时地图生成提供了高效解决方案。此外，这种方法还提供了一种评估不同传播模型保真度的新颖度量方式。

Abstract: Diffusion models achieve high-fidelity radio map construction through iterative denoising, yet their sampling cost limits practicality in dynamic wireless systems where radio maps must be refreshed repeatedly. Meanwhile, classical propagation models encode valuable scene-level knowledge that standard diffusion inference discards entirely by initializing from pure Gaussian noise. This paper bridges propagation priors and diffusion refinement through a mid-start sampling strategy. A matched propagation prior is perturbed to an intermediate diffusion timestep, and the pretrained diffusion backbone executes only the remaining reverse steps, focusing computation on multipath-aware refinement rather than full reconstruction from noise. We provide theoretical analysis establishing an upper bound on the initialization gap, a sufficient condition under which truncation improves reconstruction fidelity, and a formal characterization of prior-quality sensitivity under aggressive truncation. Experiments on IRT4HighRes show that, at $P_{\text{start}}=0.5$, the proposed method achieves a $2.01\times$ speedup while simultaneously improving NMSE, RMSE, SSIM, and PSNR over the full-step baseline. A prior-quality ablation across three propagation models of different fidelity confirms that reconstruction quality tracks prior quality, with the sensitivity amplified under shorter reverse trajectories, consistent with the theoretical predictions. These results also suggest that mid-start reconstruction quality can serve as a proxy for ranking the scene-level fidelity of different propagation models.

### [131] [Libra: Efficient Resource Management for Agentic RL Post-Training](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03077)
*Kaiwen Chen,Xin Tan,Jingzong Li,Hong Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Libra 是一个专为智能体强化学习设计的资源管理框架，通过弹性资源分配和因果驱动的调度策略，显著提升了 LLM 在复杂智能体任务中的训练效率与收敛速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大规模语言模型（LLM）的智能体强化学习中，由于 rollout 阶段产生的轨迹具有长尾分布、 rollout 与训练计算模式高度不对称以及轨迹长度随策略演进而漂移等特性，导致传统静态资源分配方案效率低下，难以应对复杂的智能体任务需求。

Method: 1. 全局资源规划器：通过弹性混合池实现 rollout（采样）与训练集群之间的轻量化、非阻塞式 GPU 资源重分配；2. 因果驱动多级反馈队列（C-MLFQ）：基于工具调用结果产生的因果信号而非长度预测，将任务分配到异构 rollout 桶中。

Result: 在 48 张 A800 GPU 的测试环境下，Libra 的吞吐量提升至基准方案的 3.0 倍，奖励模型收敛速度提升至基准方案的 2.5 倍。

Conclusion: Libra 通过动态资源规划和因果驱动的调度机制，有效解决了智能体强化学习（Agentic RL）中计算资源分配不均衡和非平稳性挑战，为大规模语言模型的训练提供了高效的系统架构。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning (RL) has become a standard post-training paradigm for large language models (LLMs), extending beyond preference alignment to complex reasoning and multi-turn agentic behaviors. In agentic RL, the rollout stage generates trajectories while invoking tools, producing long-tailed and non-stationary workloads that challenge conventional resource-management assumptions. Three fundamental challenges arise. First, due to the long-tail distribution, a small fraction of trajectories dominates rollout makespan. Second, rollout and training exhibit strong asymmetry in compute patterns, memory demands, and sensitivity to sequence length. Third, as the RL policy evolves, the trajectory-length distribution drifts over time, rendering any static resource split progressively suboptimal.
  We present Libra, which introduces two core mechanisms. The first is a periodic global resource planner that jointly optimizes GPU allocation across rollout and training clusters. It leverages an elastic hybrid pool to enable lightweight, non-blocking worker reallocation between stages. The second is a causality-driven multi-level feedback queue (C-MLFQ) scheduler, which routes requests to heterogeneous rollout buckets based on causal signals derived from tool-return outcomes, rather than relying on fragile length predictions. Evaluated on 48 A800 GPUs, Libra achieves up to 3.0$\times$ higher throughput and converges up to 2.5$\times$ faster in reward compared to the baselines.

</details>


### [132] [Multi-component Causal Tracing in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03085)
*Zirui Yan,Dennis Wei,Dmitriy A. Katz,Prasanna Sattigeri,Ali Tajer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种统一的因果追踪框架，通过将多组件选择的组合优化问题转化为连续优化问题，能够高效定位影响大语言模型特定行为（如准确性、公平性）的关键组件子集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的因果追踪研究多局限于单个组件或单层分析，难以全面解释大语言模型中多个组件如何共同作用于特定指标（如准确性、公平性）。因此，研究者旨在建立一个能够同时追踪多个组件并识别关键子集的统一框架，以应对复杂的大模型可解释性挑战。

Method: 提出了一种统一的因果追踪框架，通过引入灵活的干预手段，处理多种目标指标。针对多组件选择的组合爆炸问题，设计了一种高效算法：结合软干预（soft interventions）和特定的指标转换，将离散的组合搜索问题转化为连续优化问题，在约束条件下求解，最终生成组件选择的二元决策。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法能够高效地识别出对目标指标具有显著影响的组件子集，且在性能上优于现有的基准方法。该框架不仅适用于多种指标，还能有效地处理复杂的组件交互，验证了所提出算法在处理组合复杂性方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的统一因果追踪框架有效解决了大语言模型内部多组件交互的复杂性问题，通过将组合优化问题转化为连续优化问题，实现了对影响特定指标的关键组件的高效定位，为理解和干预大模型行为提供了强有力的工具。

Abstract: Causal tracing systematically intervenes on a large language model's (LLM's) internal representations to uncover and quantify the causal pathways linking specific inputs or computations to specific metrics of interest, quantifying the LLM's behavior. Building on previous single-component or single-layer studies, this paper presents a unified framework for causally tracing multiple components simultaneously. This framework systematically identifies the subsets of components (e.g., attention heads and multi-layer perceptron neurons) most critical to a desired target performance metric (e.g., accuracy and fairness). This is achieved by incorporating flexible interventions applied to a wide range of desired metrics. To address the combinatorial complexity of the multi-component problem, an efficient algorithm is designed that leverages soft interventions and a carefully designed metric transformation, converting the combinatorial search problem into a continuous one that can be solved efficiently under proper constraints, thereby generating proper binary decisions for selecting components. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method efficiently identifies subsets of the model's components that have a high impact on the target metric, outperforming existing baseline approaches. Our code is available at https://github.com/ZiruiYan/multi-component-causal-tracing.

### [133] [Learning to Solve, Forgetting to Retain: Correct-Set Turnover in RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03087)
*Chuanyu Qin,Chenxu Yang,Qingyi Si,Naibin Gu,Peng Fu,Zheng Lin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型强化学习训练中出现的“性能退化”问题，研究提出了 REMIND 机制，通过周期性复习已掌握知识并利用“修复窗口”原理，实现了在零额外推演开销下的性能持续提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强化学习优化大模型时，虽然整体准确率提升，但往往伴随“正确集周转”现象，即新习得的解会导致之前已解决的问题失效。现有方法缺乏对已掌握知识的有效保留，且修复已遗忘问题的代价随时间推移呈指数增长。

Method: 提出了 REMIND 机制，这是一种保留感知复习策略。该方法通过追踪模型已成功解决的提示词（正确集），并在训练过程中利用预推演批次替换技术，周期性地重新引入这些样本进行训练，从而在不增加额外推演开销的情况下，实现了对已掌握知识的加固和防御性能回归。

Result: 在包含图像-文本、视频和纯文本任务的20个基准测试中，使用 Qwen3-VL 和 Qwen2.5-Math 模型进行验证，结果表明 REMIND 机制在性能上持续优于 GRPO、DAPO 和重放（replay）基线，具有出色的跨模态和跨算法通用性。

Conclusion: 通过在强化学习训练过程中引入“正确集”保留机制，该研究有效解决了大型语言模型在训练后期出现的性能退化问题。研究证明了“修复窗口原则”，即越早复习已掌握的问题，修复回归的代价越低，从而为持续学习和模型优化提供了更高效的训练范式。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) improves the ability of large language model, yet headline accuracy gains often conceal a hidden cost: previously solved problems quietly become unsolvable as training proceeds. We frame this phenomenon as \emph{correct-set turnover}, representing the coupled dynamics of solution acquisition and regression over the mastered set. Under this view, retention becomes an explicit optimization target alongside acquisition. We analytically and empirically establish the \emph{repair-window principle}: the cost of restoring a regressed prompt grows sharply with review delay, defining a low-cost window that standard RLVR pipelines fail to exploit. To address this, we propose \textbf{\method{}}, a retention-aware review mechanism that tracks mastered prompts and periodically reintroduces them to \textbf{remind} the model of previous solutions. By utilizing pre-rollout batch replacement, \method{} incurs zero additional rollout overhead. Evaluated across 20 benchmarks spanning image-text, video, and text-only tasks with Qwen3-VL and Qwen2.5-Math, \method{} consistently improves performance over GRPO, DAPO, and replay baselines, demonstrating robust generalizability across modalities and algorithms.

### [134] [HARVE: Hacking-Aware Reward-Head Vector Editing for Robust Reward Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03131)
*Shuang Liu,Yuxuan Bo,Qiuyang Zhao,Caiyue Huang,Xiaorong Chen,Yanguang Liu,Mengnan Du*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型奖励模型易被攻击的问题，本文推出了 RewardHackBench 基准测试，并提出了一种名为 HARVE 的无需微调防御方法，通过编辑残差流中的攻击子空间，在提升鲁棒性的同时保留了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奖励模型（Reward Models）是大型语言模型（LLM）对齐的核心，但它们极易受到“奖励攻击（Reward Hacking）”的影响。现有的奖励模型往往因捕捉到虚假的表面特征而产生不安全或不符合人类偏好的输出，因此需要一套评估工具和防御机制来提升奖励模型的稳健性。

Method: 研究团队提出了 RewardHackBench 基准测试集，涵盖 13 种奖励攻击模式。针对奖励攻击问题，提出了 HARVE（一种无需训练的奖励头编辑方法）。该方法通过识别与特定攻击类别相关的残差流方向，构建多维攻击子空间，并直接从奖励头向量中移除该子空间分量，从而在无需梯度更新的情况下降低奖励头对攻击特征的敏感度。

Result: 在八个主流奖励模型上的实验表明，HARVE 能够显著提升模型对各种攻击模式的鲁棒性，性能优于传统的微调基线方法，同时保持了奖励模型原有的通用任务能力。分析还证实了奖励攻击本质上是残差空间中的多维结构，而非孤立的表面特征。

Conclusion: 通过将奖励模型攻击（Reward Hacking）建模为残差空间中的多维结构，HARVE 提出了一种有效且无需微调的防御策略。实验证明，该方法在提升奖励模型鲁棒性的同时，能够有效保留其原始的对齐与生成能力，为大语言模型的安全性提供了新的治理视角。

Abstract: Reward models are central to large language model (LLM) alignment, but they remain vulnerable to reward hacking. To evaluate reward-model robustness, we introduce RewardHackBench containing 13 reward-hacking patterns covering real life high-stakes domains and general settings, and we find severe failures on specific subcategories across eight reward models. To mitigate these failures, we propose HARVE, a training-free reward-head editing method for scalar reward models. Instead of fine-tuning the reward model, HARVE identifies a multi-directional hacking subspace from residual stream directions associated with selected hacking subcategories, and removes the component of the reward-head vector aligned with that subspace. This directly reduces the reward head's sensitivity to hacking-related features using only a small set of contrastive gold-hacked examples, without gradient updates or fine-tuning. Comprehensive experiments across eight reward models indicates that \model improves hacking robustness, outperforms fine-tuning baselines, and preserves reward-models' general capability. Further analyses suggest that reward hacking is better captured as a multidimensional residual-space structure than by isolated surface cues.

### [135] [Bayesian Tensor Decomposition with Diffusion Model Prior](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03212)
*Zerui Tao,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: DiffBCP通过将预训练扩散模型作为数据驱动先验融入贝叶斯张量分解，结合高效的分裂吉布斯采样策略，显著提升了张量分解在复杂噪声和缺失场景下的鲁棒性与重建质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统低秩张量分解在处理严重缺失或噪声数据时表现不佳，且手工设计的先验难以捕捉真实数据的复杂统计特性；现有的扩散模型难以直接与张量分解框架及后验推理相结合。

Method: 提出DiffBCP框架，采用混合先验方法：利用累积收缩过程（Cumulative Shrinkage Process）先验实现自动秩选择，并引入预训练扩散模型作为隐式数据先验；开发了一种分裂吉布斯采样器（Split Gibbs Sampler），结合低秩引导的去噪方法实现可处理的后验推理，并通过噪声自适应耦合调度降低了对超参数调整的依赖。

Result: 在图像修复和去噪任务（包括高分辨率分布外图像）中，DiffBCP均超越了现有的贝叶斯、非线性及即插即用型张量分解基准方法。

Conclusion: DiffBCP通过引入扩散模型作为隐式数据先验，结合贝叶斯CP分解，有效地解决了低秩张量分解在严重缺失或噪声干扰下的性能退化问题，在图像修复和去噪任务中表现优异。

Abstract: Low-rank tensor decomposition (TD) is usually effective on clean, fully observed data, but it often degrades under severe missingness or noise. Low-rankness is itself a useful but limited structural prior, and additional handcrafted priors (e.g., sparsity or smoothness) still fall short of capturing the rich statistics of real-world data. To compensate for this weak inductive bias under heavy corruption, one would like to inject a learned, data-driven prior; however, the state-of-the-art diffusion models are not readily compatible with current TD and tractable posterior inference. To address these challenges, we introduce DiffBCP, a hybrid-prior Bayesian CP decomposition framework that couples a cumulative shrinkage process prior over the CP factors for automatic rank selection with an off-the-shelf pre-trained diffusion model as an implicit data prior on the reconstructed tensor. To make posterior inference tractable despite the coupling among the likelihood, low-rank constraint, and diffusion prior, we develop a split Gibbs sampler: CP factors admit conjugate updates, while the diffusion block is sampled via low-rank-guided denoising. A noise-adaptive coupling schedule further reduces sensitivity to hand-tuned annealing. Experiments on image inpainting and denoising, including high-resolution out-of-distribution images, show consistent gains over Bayesian, nonlinear, and plug-and-play TD baselines.

</details>


### [136] [When RLHF Fails: A Mechanistic Taxonomy of Reward Hacking, Collapse, and Evaluator Gaming](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03238)
*Zelalem Abahana*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过对RLHF训练过程的实证研究，证明了“奖励黑客”并非单一的终点故障，而是一种可被分类、定位和预测的动态过程，并验证了不确定性惩罚机制（如UP-PPO）在减轻此类失败方面的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RLHF（从人类反馈中进行强化学习）通过引入可扩展的代理目标来替代难以明确的人类目标，但这种替代导致了结构性的失败风险，如奖励提升但模型实际质量下降（奖励黑客）。本文旨在深入探究并实证分析这些失败模式，以超越简单的“最终模型故障”视角。

Method: 研究人员构建了一个精简的RLHF流水线，包含了PPO、DPO、不确定性惩罚PPO (UP-PPO) 等多种方法，并结合了奖励模型不确定性、策略漂移分析、多样性诊断以及外部LLM评判。通过对61个检查点和1920次训练转换进行实证分析，利用奖励分数、评判分数及其变化趋势对“奖励黑客（reward hacking）”行为进行了分类和定位，并构建了逻辑回归模型来预测失败。

Result: 实验发现，攻击性（aggressive）PPO的奖励黑客发生率最高（14.45%），而UP-PPO在相同设置下能有效降低该比例；逻辑回归模型能以0.821的ROC-AUC准确预测奖励黑客行为；此外，行级分析揭示了许多被检查点平均值所掩盖的局部失败模式。

Conclusion: RLHF的失败并非仅仅是最终模型的病理现象，而是一种可以通过分类、定位和部分预测的训练动态过程。研究强调了对训练过程进行更细致监控的必要性。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning from human feedback (RLHF) makes large-scale post-training possible by replacing an underspecified human objective with learned and scalable proxies. The same substitution creates a structured failure surface: optimization can raise the learned reward while external quality falls, degrade both proxy and judge scores, reveal proxy under-alignment, or produce evaluator-specific disagreement. We present an empirical failure-mode study of a compact RLHF pipeline with proximal policy optimization (PPO), direct preference optimization (DPO), uncertainty-penalized PPO (UP-PPO), reward-model uncertainty, approximate policy drift, diversity and repetition diagnostics, and two external LLM judges. Rather than treating reward hacking as a single terminal event, we classify matched transitions between checkpoints using the directions of the learned reward, judge scores, and average judge score. Across 61 checkpoint rows and 1920 row-level transitions, aggressive PPO has the highest localized reward-hacking rate (14.45%; bootstrap 95% CI: 10.16-18.75), while UP-PPO yields lower rates in the same aggressive regime (11.33-10.94%). A pre-transition logistic model predicts future row-level reward hacking with ROC-AUC 0.821, and row-level analysis finds localized reward hacking that checkpoint averages miss in 3 of 12 settings. The central conclusion is methodological: RLHF failures are not only final-model pathologies, but training dynamics that can be classified, localized, and partially anticipated.

### [137] [EqGINO: Equivariant Geometry-Informed Fourier Neural Operators for 3D PDEs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03260)
*Sungwon Kim,Juho Song,Seungmin Shin,Guimok Cho,Sangkook Kim,Chanyoung Park*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: EqGINO 是一种新型 3D 偏微分方程替代模型，通过在谱域强制执行等变性，解决了现有方法难以兼顾全局交互与几何变换泛化的痛点，实现了高效、稳健的坐标无关物理模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的深度学习偏微分方程替代模型（如 FNO）难以兼顾全局感受野与几何等变性，导致在处理 3D 几何变换时泛化能力较差，计算成本过高。

Method: 提出了一种名为 EqGINO 的框架，通过在谱域（Spectral Domain）实施各向同性约束来强制执行对离散计算域对称性的精确等变性（Equivariance），并利用这种结构先验实现对任意连续旋转的有效泛化。

Result: 该方法能够在仅需少量 SE(3) 变换训练样本的情况下，实现对任意连续方向的有效泛化，并在复杂非规则 3D 几何体上稳健地模拟坐标无关的物理定律。

Conclusion: EqGINO 通过在谱域引入各向同性约束，成功解决了 3D 偏微分方程替代模型在几何变换下的泛化难题，为建模坐标无关的物理规律提供了一种高效且具备几何鲁棒性的新方案。

Abstract: Deep learning surrogates for 3D Partial Differential Equations (PDEs) often fail to generalize across geometric transformations because they depend heavily on specific coordinate systems. While equivariant networks offer a solution, they typically rely on local operations in the spatial domain, making the global receptive field, which is essential for PDE dynamics, computationally expensive. Conversely, Fourier Neural Operators (FNOs) efficiently capture global interactions, yet establishing 3D equivariance within them remains impractical due to the prohibitive cost of spectral group convolutions. To bridge this gap, we introduce EqGINO, a geometrically robust framework that enforces isotropy in the spectral domain. By design, EqGINO guarantees exact equivariance to the discrete symmetries inherent to the discretized computational domain. Beyond this discrete guarantee, our structural prior enables effective generalization to arbitrary continuous orientations even with a limited number of SE(3)-transformed training samples. Consequently, our method robustly models coordinate-invariant physical laws on complex irregular 3D geometries. Our code is available at https://github.com/sung-won-kim/EqGINO

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基础模型在多模态领域取得了巨大成功，但图数据中结构的可迁移性及其背后的理论基础仍不明确。作者旨在探讨常见的图子结构是否具有可迁移性，并尝试通过函数行为的视角解析表示空间的内在几何结构。

Method: 提出了“神经向量丛”（Neural Vector Bundle）框架，利用局部坐标解析图的内在几何结构；设计了GAUGE架构，通过平坦化几何兼容的局部坐标实现结构迁移，并引入了一种新的狄利克雷（Dirichlet）损失函数来度量迁移难度。

Result: 实验结果表明，GAUGE框架在零样本链路预测和图同构等高难度任务中表现出卓越的表达能力，验证了该方法在学习可迁移结构方面的有效性。

Abstract: Foundation models have sparked a revolution via a pretraining-adaptation paradigm, with recent efforts extending this success to graphs. Unlike other modalities, graphs contain rich structural patterns, yet their structural transferability remains poorly understood. Prior studies consider common substructures in the discrete realm, and we are motivated by a fundamental question: Are common substructures transferable? The underlying theory is largely underexplored. In this work, we shift toward learning transferable structures through the lens of functional behavior. Theoretically, we connect transferable substructures to intrinsic geometry of the representation space. However, characterizing such intrinsic geometry has rarely been touched. Grounded in Riemannian geometry, we develop a graph intrinsic geometry learning framework called Neural Vector Bundle, which enables parsing intrinsic geometry with local coordinates. Building on this, we design GAUGE, a pretrainable neural architecture that constructs the vector bundle, flattening geometrically compatible local coordinates, and a new Dirichlet loss, which also measures the transfer effort. We empirically validate its superior expressiveness in challenging tasks including zero-shot link prediction and graph isomorphism.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者构建了一种局部几何理论，分析了潜在空间中由熵模型、物理观测值及失真度量诱导的敏感性，并引入了“局部切空间速率-失真定律”（local tangent-space rate-distortion law）。此外，提出了一种基于主特征空间重叠（dominant eigenspace overlap）的对齐诊断方法，用于量化不同目标函数之间的冲突程度。

Result: 实验证实了该理论的有效性，证明了当物理观测值与失真度量的敏感性方向失调时，确实存在无法同时优化的物理上限。提出的对齐诊断指标能够准确反映不同科学领域数据中观测到的数据空间与物理空间的性能折中现象。

Conclusion: 本文通过局部几何视角揭示了物理信息压缩中“重建保真度”与“物理观测值准确性”之间的权衡是本质性的。这种权衡源于熵模型、物理观测函数和失真度量在潜在空间中诱导的敏感性方向不一致。研究提出的对齐诊断指标能有效预测压缩过程中的性能权衡，为科学数据压缩的优化提供了理论指导。

Abstract: In AI for Science, physics-informed losses are increasingly used to train learned compressors for scientific data, but their rate-distortion implications remain poorly understood. At fixed bitrate, these objectives often improve preservation of a target physical observable while degrading standard reconstruction fidelity. We develop a local geometric theory showing that this tradeoff is governed by the interaction of latent-space sensitivities induced by the entropy model, the physical observable, and the distortion metric. At each operating point, these induce preferred directions along which compression noise should be suppressed, yielding an anisotropic error-allocation mechanism. When these directions are misaligned, improving the observable at fixed rate necessarily worsens standard distortion, establishing a fundamental limit on simultaneous preservation. We formalise this through a local tangent-space rate-distortion law and introduce a practical alignment diagnostic based on dominant eigenspace overlap. Experiments across scientific domains test the theory and validate that the alignment diagnostic correlates with observed data- and physics-space trade-offs.

Abstract: Graph Foundation Models (GFMs), built upon the Pre-training and Adaptation paradigm, have emerged as a research hotspot in graph learning. Although recent methods explain why graph prompt tuning works, how to rigorously measure its adaptation capacity remains an open problem. Addressing this problem is critical for understanding the capability limits of graph prompt tuning and for developing more powerful adaptation methods. In this paper, we propose Prismatic Space Theory (PS-Theory), a novel mathematical framework to quantify the capacity of adaptation methods, while focusing on establishing the upper bound for the adaptation capacity of graph prompt tuning. Building upon the proposed PS-Theory, we further introduce Message Tuning for GFMs (MTG), a lightweight approach that injects a small set of learnable message prototypes into each layer of the GNN backbone to adaptively guide message fusion without updating pre-trained weights. Through our PS-Theory, we prove that the adaptation capacity of MTG can exceed the theoretical upper bound of graph prompt tuning. ### [142] [A Graph Foundation Model with Spectral Parsing and Prototype-Guided Spatial Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03315)
*Ankang Yang,Jitao Zhao,Dongxiao He,Liang Yang,Di Jin,Weixiong Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了SPG模型，通过结合谱滤波分解与Gromov-Wasserstein原型几何学习，解决了图基础模型在跨图迁移中结构差异大及信号频率处理不当的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的图基础模型（GFM）在跨图迁移时面临两大挑战：一是图结构的多样性导致难以形成统一的结构理解，现有的结构标记或词表设计存在覆盖率不足的问题；二是图信号中高低频信息混叠，且缺乏对不同频率信号传播行为的差异化处理，限制了模型的泛化能力。

Method: 提出了SPG（Spectral parsing and Prototype-guided Graph foundation model）：1. 利用可学习的切比雪夫滤波器对节点特征进行谱分解，以解耦并处理不同频率的图信号；2. 构建Gromov-Wasserstein原型几何结构，将不同图的成对关系提炼到共享的结构空间中；3. 将学习到的原型几何投影为原型引导的传播算子，实现更有效的空间信息聚合。

Result: 实验结果表明，SPG模型在多个跨领域图学习基准数据集上均取得了性能提升，证明了其在处理不同结构分布和复杂图信号时的强大泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本文提出的SPG模型通过谱解析和原型引导的传播机制，有效地解决了跨图迁移学习中拓扑结构差异和特征频率混叠的问题，在多项跨领域任务中表现出优异的泛化性能，为图基础模型的发展提供了新的范式。

Abstract: Graph foundation models aim to learn transferable knowledge from diverse graphs for generalization to unseen graphs and tasks. Unlike text and images, graphs lack a shared vocabulary or regular spatial grid, making cross-graph transfer challenging. This challenge comes from both feature discrepancies and, more critically, diverse graph structures. Existing GFMs mainly improve transferability by unifying feature spaces or incorporating structural tokens and vocabularies. However, existing topology-aware designs still have limitations. Structural tokens are usually discrete, while structural vocabularies often rely on predefined substructures such as trees and cycles, whose limited coverage may miss richer relational patterns across graphs. Moreover, graph signals contain both high-frequency local patterns and smoother low-frequency patterns, which require different propagation behaviors. These components are often entangled in raw graph signals, while this spectral perspective is rarely explored in existing GFMs. To address these challenges, we propose SPG, a graph foundation model with spectral parsing and prototype-guided spatial propagation. SPG applies learnable Chebyshev filters to decompose node features into multiple spectral responses, reducing the mismatch between frequency-specific graph signals and propagation behaviors. It then constructs a Gromov-Wasserstein prototype geometry to distill transferable pairwise relations beyond predefined substructures into a shared structural space. The learned prototype geometry is further projected back as a prototype-guided propagation operator. Experiments demonstrate consistent improvements in cross-domain generalization.

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过引入由监控、诊断、自适应、安全审计和协调器组成的多智能体架构，辅以确定性的“冠军-挑战者”门控机制，可以实现热工水力预测模型在部署环境下的安全、可审计的持续学习与演进，显著优于传统的静态模型。

Abstract: Artificial-intelligence surrogates can support second-by-second thermal-hydraulic forecasting, but models selected and frozen offline may become condition-locked once deployed outside their pretraining envelope. This study develops a guarded continual-adaptation framework for experimental thermal-hydraulic loop data in which role-separated agents - Monitor, Diagnosis, Adaptation, Safety-Auditor, and Orchestrator - diagnose error signatures, prioritize candidate model families, and review promotions, while deterministic champion-challenger gates and background shadow learning retain final authority over model replacement. Seven surrogate families were screened by blocked three-fold cross-validation, and a temporal Fourier neural operator was selected as the initial champion for 60-s-history-to-10-s-trajectory forecasting on two held-out transients, with three seeds per adaptive mode. Static deployment gave a channel-averaged MAE of 7.06 and a 56.8% warning-exceedance ratio; rule-based adaptation reduced MAE to 6.54, whereas shadow refresh alone remained close to Static. The MA-Full mode, in which the role-separated multi-agent council reviews every evaluated stream step, achieved the lowest mean error, 5.72, and 35.8% exceedance, corresponding to a 19.0% improvement over Static. Paired bootstrap intervals against Static excluded zero, although intervals among adaptive modes overlapped and the six paired units limit broad statistical claims. Validated promotions from the neural operator to Transformer and graph neural network indicate that logged, gate-controlled adaptation can support auditable surrogate evolution while deterministic gates retain deployment authority.

### [145] [Calibration Data Trade-offs Across Capability Dimensions: Why Multi-Source Mixing Matters for High-Sparsity LLM Pruning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03328)
*Hu Xu,Zhaolong Xing,Congcong Liu,Jiaxing Wang,Zhida Jiang,Junshi Huang,Zhen Chen,Jianfeng Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 研究发现大语言模型剪枝后的能力损失取决于校准数据的选择，且不同能力维度（如通用vs数学）存在权衡。作者提出了IGSP协议，通过自动化多源校准集混合，显著缓解了剪枝带来的能力退化问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 既有研究认为校准数据集的选择对模型剪枝后的平均精度影响有限，但该结论往往掩盖了在不同能力维度（如通用能力与数学/代码能力）上的表现差异。研究旨在探究校准数据对不同能力维度的具体影响，并解决单一校准源难以全面维持模型性能的问题。

Method: 1. 对比分析：将大模型能力分解为通用、常识、代码和数学四个维度，分析15种不同校准源对各维度性能的影响。
2. 相关性研究：利用Spearman相关性分析校准困惑度（Perplexity）与各维度能力保持度之间的关系，发现存在显著的性能权衡。
3. IGSP协议：提出一种信息引导的自校准协议（Information-Guided Self-calibration Protocol），通过最小化4-gram聚合和平衡各维度的困惑度，自动生成优化的多源校准集。

Result: 1. 发现校准困惑度与通用能力保持呈正相关，但与数学及代码能力呈负相关，证明了不同能力维度之间存在“零和”权衡。
2. 在LLaMA-3.1-8B模型及60%稀疏度下，使用IGSP协议构建的多源校准混合方案，在总能力保持上达到58.8%，相比最佳单一来源（50.0%）提升了8.8个百分点，相比常用的C4数据集（40.0%）提升了18.8个百分点。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，校准数据的选择对大语言模型剪枝后的特定能力（如数学与代码）具有显著且差异化的影响。通过引入信息引导的自校准协议（IGSP），研究证明了多源校准混合能够有效平衡各类能力，并在剪枝模型性能保持上显著优于单一来源方案。

Abstract: Post-training pruning compresses large language models to high sparsity using a small unlabelled calibration set, and recent work has concluded that the choice of calibration source has only modest impact on averaged post-pruning accuracy. We ask whether this conclusion survives once calibration impact is evaluated separately across distinct capability dimensions rather than aggregated. Decomposing post-pruning capability into General, Commonsense, Code, and Math, and analysing $n{=}15$ calibration sources via Spearman correlations between OIT information metrics and per-dimension retention, we uncover an opposite-sign trade-off: calibration perplexity correlates positively with General retention ($ρ{=}{+}0.71$) but negatively with Math and Code retention ($ρ{=}{-}0.53,\,{-}0.59$; $p{<}0.05$), so no single source can preserve all capabilities. We respond with multi-source calibration mixing, and propose IGSP, an information-guided self-calibration protocol that automates multi-source construction without capability-aligned corpora by minimising 4-gram aggregation and balancing perplexity across dimensions. On LLaMA-3.1-8B at SparseGPT 60% sparsity, a uniform multi-source mix reaches 58.8% total retention, outperforming the best single source (MetaMath, 50.0%) by $+8.8$ and the C4 default (40.0%) by $+18.8$; IGSP improves over Self-Cal by $+2.4$ and SGS by $+4.8$.

### [146] [FLIPS: Instance-Fingerprinting for LLMs via Pseudo-random Sequences](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03330)
*Gurvan Richardeau,Gohar Dashyan,Erwan Le Merrer,Gilles Tredan*

Main category: cs.LG

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者提出了一种名为FLIPS的实例级指纹识别方法。该方法利用模型在生成二进制随机序列时表现出的内在偏差作为特征，并通过这些偏差来识别和区分同一LLM的不同运行配置（如不同的提示词、采样参数或量化方式）。

Result: 实验结果表明，在包含237个模型实例的测试中，FLIPS方法的识别准确率在封闭集下达到96%，在开放集下达到90%，显著优于基准方法LLMmap（仅35%）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的FLIPS方法证明了对LLM进行实例级指纹识别不仅是监管所必需的，而且在技术上是完全可行的，能够有效区分同一模型的不同配置，为AI合规性评估提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Literature reveals that a Large Language Model's (LLM) behavior is not only conditioned by its original weights but also its instance-level parameters, such as instructional prompt, sampling configuration or quantization. A model that generates safe outputs under one configuration may produce toxic content under another. However, current LLM identification techniques (such as fingerprinting) focus on intellectual property protection, and their design favors robustness to changes in these instance-level parameters. This poses a critical challenge for AI regulation in which compliance assessments target actual deployed behaviors, not model provenance. In this paper, we introduce instance-level fingerprinting, a regulator-oriented paradigm that distinguishes configurations of the same LLM. Our method FLIPS, exploits biases in generated binary random sequences to reach 96% (closed-set) and 90% (open-set, where some targets are unknown) identification accuracy across 237 model instances, versus 35% for the adapted LLMmap baseline. This shows that instance-level fingerprinting is both necessary for regulation and practically feasible. Code available at https://github.com/GurvanR/FLIPS-LLM-Instance-Fingerprinting.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在多个因果推断基准测试中，使用该方法训练的模型在 ATE 估计上始终优于标准的似然估计法（likelihood-based）和协变量平衡法（covariate-balancing）。实验表明，该方法能显著降低估计偏差和方差，提升因果推断的准确性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过将下游因果推断任务的目标（如 ATE 估计）直接嵌入到概率模型的训练损失函数中，证明了针对特定任务定制损失函数可以有效克服传统与任务无关的损失函数带来的偏差与方差问题，为因果推理及其他预测任务提供了更鲁棒的框架。

Abstract: Probabilistic models are typically trained using task-agnostic objectives like log-loss, which can lead to significant errors in downstream estimation. This disconnect is especially critical in Inverse Probability Weighting (IPW) for causal inference, where propensity score errors near $0$ and $1$ often lead to high bias and variance. We propose a principled framework for deriving task-specific strictly proper scoring rules by matching the local curvature of the downstream error metric. We apply this to the Average Treatment Effect (ATE) estimation, deriving a closed-form loss and its corresponding canonical probability mapping that can be readily integrated with any model like a neural network or a gradient boosting algorithm. Extensive evaluations on causal inference benchmarks demonstrate that our tailored objective consistently outperforms standard likelihood-based and covariate-balancing approaches.

### [148] [IdEst: Assessing Self-Supervised Learning Representations via Intrinsic Dimension](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03338)

Conclusion: 本研究证实了内在维度（ID）是评估自监督学习（SSL）表征质量的一种具有原则性的几何代理指标，能够作为传统线性探测方法的有效补充，并显著提升模型评估与超参数选择的效率。

Abstract: Self-supervised learning (SSL) has emerged as a powerful paradigm for learning meaningful representations from unlabeled data. In this work, motivated by connections between neural network generalization and intrinsic dimension (ID) we propose IdEst, a method for estimating the ID of SSL representations via the Minimum Spanning Tree dimension estimator ($\mathrm{dim}_\mathrm{MST}$). Across diverse datasets, architectures, and SSL pretraining objectives, we show that IdEst strongly correlates with downstream linear probe performances. Furthermore, we demonstrate that IdEst enables efficient hyperparameter selection, significantly reducing the computational cost compared to supervised alternatives. Our results highlight intrinsic dimensionality as a principled geometric proxy for assessing SSL representations, complementing standard supervised probing protocols.

### [149] [AugMask: Training Diffusion Models on Incomplete Tabular Data via Stochastic Augmentation and Masking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03347)
*Jungkyu Kim,Taeyoung Park,Kibok Lee*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: AugMask是一个通用的扩散模型训练框架，通过将缺失值视为条件上下文而非监督目标，有效地解决了表格数据中存在缺失值的问题，提升了数据生成的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于分数的扩散模型通常要求输入是完整的，而现实世界的表格数据经常存在缺失值，这限制了扩散模型在表格数据生成任务中的应用。

Method: 提出了一种名为AugMask的即插即用训练框架，包含两个核心机制：1) 使用轻量级辅助模型进行条件随机增强，构建数值输入；2) 仅对观测到的坐标应用去噪监督。该方法通过将缺失值的填充视为条件上下文而非训练目标，并将其与Rao-Blackwellized目标函数连接，通过边际化处理实现了方差加权的灵敏度惩罚。

Result: 实验结果表明，在多种数据集和不同的数据缺失情形下，使用AugMask训练的扩散模型能够显著优于现有的处理缺失数据的专用生成基准模型。

Conclusion: AugMask提供了一种灵活且高效的通用框架，能够将缺失值不敏感的扩散模型骨干网络扩展到处理具有缺失值的真实世界表格数据，在多项任务中优于专门设计的基准方法。

Abstract: Score-based diffusion models have emerged as prominent deep generative models; however, their application to tabular data remains challenging because their backbones assume fully specified inputs, whereas real-world tabular data often contain missing values. We propose AugMask, a plug-and-play training framework that adapts missing-unaware backbones to incomplete data by separating conditioning from supervision. AugMask 1) constructs numeric inputs via conditional stochastic augmentation using lightweight auxiliary models, and 2) applies denoising supervision only to observed coordinates. In effect, augmented missing entries serve as uncertain conditioning context rather than training targets. We connect this training rule to a Rao--Blackwellized objective and show that marginalizing missing entries yields a variance-weighted sensitivity penalty, discouraging over-reliance on uncertain completions. Across diverse datasets and missingness regimes, AugMask enables standard diffusion-based tabular generators to outperform specialized missing-aware baselines.

### [150] [APIC: Amortized Physics-Informed Calibration using Neural Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03355)
*Aishwarya Venkataramanan,Sai Karthikeya Vemuri,Joachim Denzler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了 APIC 框架，利用神经过程将传统的物理模型校准方法（KOH）升级为可处理大规模系统的高效摊销化学习方法，实现了物理参数与系统偏差的有效解耦。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的 Kennedy-O'Hagan (KOH) 模型在处理复杂系统时存在非摊销化、逐实例建模的局限性，导致其在大规模相关系统簇上的扩展性较差，无法有效解决物理模型中因机制缺失或设定错误带来的系统性偏差。

Method: 提出一种名为 APIC（Amortized Physics-Informed Calibration）的框架，通过神经过程（Neural Processes）实现对 KOH 模型的“摊销化”扩展；利用双分支潜在架构，将特定于实例的物理参数与共享的、依赖于状态的系统偏差结构进行解耦。

Result: 在阻尼弹簧振子、Lotka-Volterra 系统及对流扩散偏微分方程等实验中，APIC 表现出比传统校准方法更高的参数恢复精度，并能在稀疏观测下快速完成对未知实例的校准及不确定性量化。

Conclusion: APIC 框架成功将经典 KOH 模型扩展至可推广的人口学习范式，证明了结合神经过程与可微物理模型在处理大规模系统偏差和参数不确定性方面的有效性与优越性。

Abstract: Physics models are inherently imperfect due to misspecified or missing mechanisms, resulting in systematic discrepancies between model predictions and real-world observations. The Kennedy-O'Hagan (KOH) framework addresses this issue through explicit discrepancy modeling. However, its non-amortized, per-instance formulation limits scalability across families of related systems. We introduce Amortized Physics-Informed Calibration (APIC), a population-level extension of KOH that leverages Neural Processes to perform scalable Bayesian inference across realizations. Our framework employs a two-branch latent architecture to disentangle instance-specific physical parameters from shared, state-dependent structural discrepancies. By integrating differentiable physics into an amortized inference backbone, APIC enables rapid calibration of unseen realizations from sparse observations while quantifying uncertainty. Experiments on the damped spring oscillator, the Lotka-Volterra system, and the advection-diffusion PDE with misspecified physics demonstrate improved parameter recovery and consistent identification of the systemic discrepancy structure compared to other calibration approaches.

### [151] [The Impact of Temporal Granularity on Socio-Demographic Inference from Household Load Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03358)
*Dejan Radovanovic,Maximilian Schirl,Andreas Unterweger,Günther Eibl*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究定量分析了智能电表数据时间分辨率对家庭隐私泄露的影响，发现存在特定的数据聚合平台期，支持在保持一定效用的前提下通过降低分辨率来保护用户隐私。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 智能电表数据能够揭示家庭隐私信息，但目前学界尚不清楚数据的时间分辨率（Temporal Resolution）如何具体影响社会人口统计学属性的推断性能，缺乏针对该权衡关系的系统性研究，这限制了隐私保护技术在智能电网中的应用。

Method: 研究者使用了包含1589户家庭、时长为一年的智能电表数据集。通过将数据粒度从15分钟下调至7天，评估了对8种社会人口属性推断的影响。构建了跨季节和周变异的泛化评估框架，对比了手工特征、tsfresh自动提取特征与CNN自动编码器嵌入特征的表现，并采用了XGBoost等多种分类器进行建模与特征重要性分析。

Result: 1. 预测性能存在两个显著的“平台期”：15分钟至1小时之间，以及1天至7天之间，这意味着在不牺牲推断准确性的前提下存在显著的数据最小化空间。2. 基于XGBoost的手工/tsfresh特征方案在表现上与CNN自动编码器持平甚至更优。3. 特征重要性分析显示，属性类型决定了对粒度的依赖，如房屋面积通过粗粒度数据即可推断，而使用游泳池则高度依赖高频的时间信号。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了智能电表数据的时间粒度、特征提取方法及分类器选择对用户社会人口统计学特征推断的影响。研究结果表明，在隐私保护与数据效用之间存在平衡空间（如数据聚合到1小时仍能保持较高推断准确率），这为实施数据最小化策略提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Smart meter data can reveal sensitive socio-demographic characteristics of households, raising privacy concerns. While this risk has been demonstrated at fixed granularities, the role of temporal resolution in shaping inference performance remains insufficiently explored. This paper addresses this gap by analyzing how load profiles with granularities from 15 minutes to 7 days affect the predictability of eight socio-demographic attributes in a dataset of 1,589 households over one year. We introduce an evaluation framework where classifiers are trained on year-round data but tested on arbitrary weeks, forcing generalization across seasonal and weekly variations. Our results show three main findings. First, while coarsening granularity reduces predictive accuracy, two plateaus emerge: performance is stable between 15 minutes and 1 hour, and again between 1 and 7 days. This reveals opportunities for data minimization without sacrificing utility. Second, interpretable handcrafted and tsfresh features remain competitive with CNN-based autoencoder embeddings, while XGBoost consistently outperforms alternative classifiers. Third, feature importance analysis highlights differences between static and dynamic attributes: dwelling size can be inferred even from coarse data, whereas swimming pool usage requires fine-grained temporal signals. Overall, our study provides new insights into the privacy-utility trade-off in smart metering, showing how temporal resolution, feature extraction, and classifier choice jointly influence socio-demographic inference.

</details>


### [152] [WUSH: Near-Optimal Adaptive Transforms for LLM Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2512.00956)
*Jiale Chen,Vage Egiazarian,Roberto L. Castro,Torsten Hoefler,Dan Alistarh*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了WUSH（一种数据依赖的线性变换方法），通过纠正量化过程中的异常值分布，显著提升了低比特大语言模型的量化精度和推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在进行低比特量化部署时，权重和激活值中存在的极少数极端异常值会拉大动态范围并显著放大量化误差。现有的基于变换的缓解方法（如哈达玛变换）通常是固定的且与数据无关，其在量化方面的最优性尚未得到证明。

Method: 作者推导出了在标准RTN AbsMax缩放块量化器下，针对权重和激活联合量化的闭式最优线性分块变换。该方法构建了WUSH变换，这是一种结合了哈达玛变换主干与数据相关二阶矩分量的非正交变换，并针对GPU实现了高效的算子融合。

Result: WUSH在Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct模型上表现优异，在W4A4量化设置下，相较于现有的最优哈达玛基线，RTN量化平均准确率提升了2.8个百分点，GPTQ量化提升了0.7个百分点；同时通过FP4矩阵乘法实现了较BF16高达5.8倍的逐层吞吐量提升。

Conclusion: 本文提出的WUSH方法通过结合哈达玛变换与数据依赖的二阶矩成分，成功克服了权重和激活值中的极端异常值问题，为低比特量化提供了一种在保持高性能的同时具备理论支撑的优化方案，是实现高效大语言模型部署的重要技术进步。

Abstract: Quantizing LLM weights and activations is a standard approach for efficient deployment, but a few extreme outliers can stretch the dynamic range and amplify low-bit quantization errors. Prior transform-based mitigations (e.g., Hadamard rotations) are fixed and data-agnostic, and their optimality for quantization has remained unclear. We derive closed-form optimal linear blockwise transforms for joint weight-activation quantization under standard RTN AbsMax-scaled block quantizers, covering both integer and floating-point formats. The resulting construction, WUSH, combines a Hadamard backbone with a data-dependent second-moment component to form a non-orthogonal transform that is provably near-optimal for FP and INT quantizers under mild assumptions while admitting an efficient fused GPU implementation. Empirically, WUSH improves W4A4 accuracy over the strongest Hadamard-based baselines (e.g., on Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct in MXFP4, it gains +2.8 average points with RTN and +0.7 with GPTQ) while delivering up to 5.8$\times$ per-layer throughput over BF16 via FP4 MatMul. Source code is available at https://github.com/IST-DASLab/WUSH.

### [153] [Mitigating False Credit Propagation: Probabilistic Graphical Reward Aggregation for Rubric-Based Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03361)
*Can Lv,Mingju Chen,Heng Chang,Shiji Zhou*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型基于准则的奖励机制中存在的逻辑依赖忽视问题（FCP），本文提出了GEAR框架，通过图形模型显式处理准则间的先决条件，实现了更准确的奖励计算并提升了模型训练效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言模型基于准则（rubric）的奖励机制通常采用简单的标量聚合，忽略了准则之间存在的先决条件和激活逻辑。这导致了“错误信用传播”（FCP）问题，即即使准则的逻辑前提未达成，模型仍能获得奖励或惩罚。

Method: 提出名为GEAR的概率图形框架：将每个评分准则建模为类型化图中的潜在伯努利事件；利用图结构传播软抑制（soft suppression），当父准则未满足时自动抑制子准则的奖励，最后将事件概率聚合为归一化的期望效用。该方法保持了线性时间复杂度，可无缝接入现有的强化学习流水线。

Result: 在HealthBench、WritingBench和PLawBench三个基准测试中，GEAR相比传统的平坦聚合方法，相对增益最高达15.5%。在FCP诊断测试中，GEAR在减少奖励泄露方面表现卓越（降低了96.5%），同时比确定性门控方法保留了更多的有效下游效用。

Conclusion: GEAR框架通过引入结构化的概率依赖建模，有效解决了大语言模型基于准则（rubric）奖励机制中的“错误信用传播”（FCP）问题。该方法证明了在奖励评估中显式建模准则间的逻辑依赖关系，能够显著提升模型训练的质量与奖励反馈的准确性。

Abstract: Rubric-based rewards are increasingly used for open-ended language model post-training, but criterion-level scores are often aggregated as independent utilities. This flat scalarization ignores rubric-specified prerequisite and activation relations among criteria, allowing reward or penalty to be counted even when the condition that licenses it is absent. We call this structural reward-aggregation failure \textbf{False Credit Propagation} (FCP). To address this limitation, we propose \ourname (\textbf{G}raphical \textbf{E}vent \textbf{A}ggregation for \textbf{R}ubric rewards), a probabilistic graphical framework for dependency-aware rubric aggregation. \ourname models each criterion outcome as a latent Bernoulli event in a typed rubric graph, propagates soft suppression from unsupported parent events to their children, and aggregates the resulting event probabilities into a normalized expected signed utility. This yields a linear-time reward computation that can be plugged into standard rubric-based RL pipelines without changing the outer optimization algorithm. Experiments on HealthBench, WritingBench, and PLawBench with two policy backbones show that \ourname consistently improves over flat aggregation and deterministic gating, achieving relative gains of up to 15.5\% over flat aggregation. FCP diagnostics further show that \ourname reduces leakage by 96.5\% relative to flat aggregation while preserving more licensed downstream utility than deterministic gating. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/LvCan926/GEAR.

</details>


### [154] [Link Prediction or Perdition: the Seeds of Instability in Knowledge Graph Embeddings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03365)
*Guillaume Méroué,Fabien Gandon,Pierre Monnin*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了知识图谱嵌入模型在评估中普遍存在的稳定性缺失问题，发现模型预测结果受随机因素影响极大，且现有主流指标无法反映这种不确定性，对 KGEMs 的实际应用可靠性提出了严峻挑战。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过对多种知识图谱嵌入模型（KGEMs）和数据集进行系统的稳定性分析，量化评估了初始化、三元组排序、负采样、丢弃（dropout）和硬件环境等随机因素对模型预测结果和嵌入空间组织结构的影响，并评估了集成学习（投票机制）在提升稳定性方面的作用。

Result: 研究发现，即便是高性能的模型，其三元组级别的预测结果也存在显著差异，嵌入空间结构高度不稳定。各种随机因素对不稳定性贡献的程度相当。此外，MRR 指标与模型稳定性之间并无直接的正相关关系，且投票机制仅能带来有限的稳定性改进。

Conclusion: 现有的知识图谱嵌入模型评估协议存在重大局限性，忽略了结果不稳定性带来的潜在风险。研究表明，追求高 MRR 分数的模型并不一定具备高稳定性，且简单的集成方法（如投票）无法有效解决这一问题。评估知识图谱模型时，除了关注性能指标，还必须将稳定性纳入核心考量范畴。

Abstract: Embedding models (KGEMs) constitute the main link prediction approach to complete knowledge graphs. Standard evaluation protocols emphasize rank-based metrics such as MRR or Hits@$K$, but usually overlook the influence of random seeds on result stability. Moreover, these metrics conceal potential instabilities in individual predictions and in the organization of embedding spaces. In this work, we conduct a systematic stability analysis of multiple KGEMs across several datasets. We find that high-performance models actually produce divergent predictions at the triple level and highly variable embedding spaces. By isolating stochastic factors (i.e., initialization, triple ordering, negative sampling, dropout, hardware), we show that each independently induces instability of comparable magnitude. Furthermore, for a given model, hyperparameter configurations with better MRR are not guaranteed to be more stable. Moreover, voting, albeit a known remediation mechanism, only provides a limited enhancement of stability. These findings highlight critical limitations of current benchmarking protocols, and raise concerns about the reliability of KGEMs for knowledge graph completion.

### [155] [Local Guidance, Global Impact: Gaussian-Reshaped Trust Region Unlocks Behavior Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03382)
*Bingxu Liu,Jiashun Liu,Johan Obando-Ceron,Hao Wang,Runze Liu,Pablo Samuel Castro,Aaron Courville,Ling Pan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对PPO在非平稳环境中更新低效的问题，本文提出GTR算法，通过高斯核重塑信任域并引入动态锚点机制，显著提升了策略在持续学习场景下的适应能力与训练鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: PPO在非平稳和持续学习环境中表现不佳，研究发现其核心问题并非模型容量不足或裁剪限制，而是由于缺乏几何感知指导，导致策略更新方向效率低下，且基于散度的正则化在必要时会过度限制策略演变，阻碍了对新行为模式的有效适应。

Method: 提出高斯信任域策略优化（Gaussian Trust Region Policy Optimization, GTR）：
1. 使用高斯核函数重塑信任域，引入有界且非单调的约束，实现局部稳定性与持续高优势更新下的灵活适应之间的平衡；
2. 引入混合高斯锚点（Mixture Gaussian Anchor），根据近期策略轨迹动态调整，以降低陈旧引用带来的方差影响。

Result: GTR算法在游戏、模拟机器人控制、开放世界探索及语言模型后期训练等多类任务中均取得了优于基准方法（如PPO）的性能，证明了该方法在处理复杂非平稳环境时的稳健性与高效性。

Conclusion: 本文证明了基于几何感知的信任域设计是处理非平稳强化学习环境的有效途径。通过引入高斯核重塑信任域并结合混合高斯锚点机制，GTR能够克服传统PPO在持续学习中因方向性更新低效导致的行为适应障碍，展现了在多类复杂任务中的鲁棒性与广泛适用性。

Abstract: While Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) demonstrates strong performance in stationary settings, we show that its standard optimization paradigm struggles in continual and non-stationary environments. The failure does not stem from insufficient model capacity or overly restrictive clipping. Instead, PPO performs persistent, directionally inefficient local updates, which indicates a lack of geometry-aware guidance for accumulating meaningful behavioral change and ultimately hindering transitions toward new behavior patterns. Although divergence-based regularization introduces partial geometric awareness, its monotonically increasing penalties implicitly discourage large policy deviations, even when such shifts are necessary for effective adaptation. To address this limitation, we propose Gaussian Trust Region Policy Optimization (GTR), which reshapes the trust region using a Gaussian kernel. The resulting constraint is bounded and non-monotonic, providing strong local stability while progressively relaxing under sustained high-advantage updates. To further improve robustness, we introduce a Mixture Gaussian Anchor that adapts to recent policy trajectories, reducing variance induced by stale references. GTR is architecture-agnostic and achieves strong performance across games, simulated robotic control, open-world exploration, and language model post-training. These results demonstrate that geometry-aware trust-region design can be a promising direction for robust reinforcement learning in complex non-stationary environments. Our code is available at https://anonymous.4open.science/r/GTR_demo/README.md.
