### [156] [When Model Merging Breaks Routing: Training-Free Calibration for MoE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03391)
*Canbin Huang,Tianyuan Shi,Xiaojun Quan,Jingang Wang,Jianfei Zhang,Qifan Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对MoE模型合并时路由失效的问题，本文提出HARC框架，通过二阶曲率信息在无训练的情况下校准路由，显著提升了MoE模型合并后的推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的模型合并技术在应用于混合专家（MoE）模型时会遇到“路由崩溃”问题，即合并后的路由层无法将Token分发给合适的专家。由于Softmax和Top-k机制对参数扰动高度敏感，简单的线性合并会导致性能显著下降。

Method: 提出了Hessian-Aware Router Calibration (HARC) 框架。该方法利用二阶曲率信息（Hessian矩阵）对合并后的路由层进行校准，通过无矩阵共轭梯度法求解闭式解，从而在无需重新训练的情况下恢复路由逻辑。

Result: 在数学推理和代码生成任务上的实验表明，HARC能够有效缓解各种MoE合并基线中的路由崩溃问题，并显著提升合并后模型的性能。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了MoE模型合并中的“路由崩溃”现象，并通过HARC框架提供了一种无需训练的二阶校准方案，有效提升了合并后模型的路由准确性和推理能力，为多专家模型的组合提供了新思路。

Abstract: Model merging has emerged as a cost-effective approach for consolidating the capabilities of multiple LLMs without retraining. However, existing merging techniques, largely based on linear parameter arithmetic or optimization, struggle when applied to Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architectures. We identify a critical failure mode in MoE merging, termed routing breakdown, in which the merged router fails to dispatch tokens to suitable experts. Routing breakdown stems from the sensitivity of the non-linear softmax and discrete Top-k routing mechanisms to parameter perturbations from merging, a sensitivity further amplified by load-balancing constraints imposed during MoE pretraining. Because fine-tuned experts exhibit distinct specializations, even modest misrouting can cause severe performance degradation. To address this issue, we propose Hessian-Aware Router Calibration (HARC), a training-free framework that leverages second-order curvature information to realign the merged router. This approach admits a closed-form solution that can be efficiently solved using a matrix-free conjugate gradient method. Experiments on mathematical reasoning and code generation tasks show that HARC effectively mitigates routing breakdown across diverse MoE merging baselines and leads to substantial performance improvements. Our code is available at https://github.com/huangcb01/HARC.

### [157] [Flicker-DDPM: Accelerating Denoising Diffusion via 1/f Colored Noise Injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03393)
*Kexiang Mao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Flicker-DDPM通过在前向扩散过程中使用模拟自然图像统计规律的“闪烁噪声”（1/f噪声）代替传统白噪声，在保证生成质量的前提下，显著提升了扩散模型的采样效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统DDPM模型在前向扩散过程中使用各向同性白噪声，未能充分利用自然图像在频域上通常遵循幂律分布（P(k) ∝ 1/k^α）的统计特性。作者旨在通过引入符合自然系统自组织临界性（SOC）的闪烁噪声，使噪声分布更贴合真实数据，从而提升模型生成质量及采样效率。

Method: 提出了一种名为Flicker-DDPM的新型扩散模型，其核心在于将前向扩散过程中的各向同性白噪声替换为具有幂律谱特征的“闪烁噪声”（1/f噪声）。通过引入空间相关核σ(d) = (d + 1)^{-η}，模型能够灵活调整噪声的谱指数α，以匹配不同数据集的统计特性。此外，作者建立了频域线性理论，解释了光谱匹配的噪声如何线性化反向生成轨迹，从而实现采样加速。

Result: 在CIFAR-10数据集上，Flicker-DDPM在保持生成质量不逊于甚至优于标准DDPM的情况下，将采样步数减少了3.33倍，且每步的额外计算开销可以忽略不计。理论分析和实验结果共同验证了光谱匹配噪声对于加速反向扩散轨迹的有效性。

Conclusion: Flicker-DDPM通过引入具有特定幂律谱的“闪烁噪声”，成功利用自然图像的统计规律优化了扩散模型的生成过程。这一研究证实了将物理系统中的自组织临界性原理应用于生成模型的可行性，并为提高采样效率提供了一种无需显著增加计算开销的新思路。

Abstract: We propose a novel diffusion model, Flicker-DDPM, which incorporates flicker (1/f) noise inspired by self-organized criticality (SOC), a widely observed phenomenon in natural systems. Unlike denoising diffusion probabilistic models (DDPMs), which employ isotropic white noise in the forward process, Flicker-DDPM adopts colored noise with power-law spectra to better match the spectral statistics of natural images, whose power spectra typically follow P(k) proportional to 1/k^α. To this end, we develop a colored-noise module based on a spatial correlation kernel, σ(d) = (d + 1)^{-η}, and theoretically establish that adjusting η controls the spectral exponent α of the generated 1/fα noise, enabling adaptation to datasets with diverse spectral characteristics. On CIFAR-10, Flicker DDPM matches or surpasses the generation quality of a standard DDPM baseline using 3.33 times fewer sampling steps, with negligible additional computational cost per step. We further develop a frequency-domain linear theory demonstrating that spectrally matched colored noise linearizes the reverse trajectory, theoretically explaining the observed sampling acceleration.

</details>


### [158] [Forgetting is Not Erasure: Recovering Latent Knowledge via Transport Keys](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02860)
*Archie Chaudhury*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文指出持续学习中的“灾难性遗忘”更多是由于模型内部阶段间的接口不匹配（接口漂移）导致的，而非特征的永久性遗忘；通过引入“传输密钥”进行接口对齐，可以有效恢复旧任务性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对灾难性遗忘现象，作者挑战了传统的“特征丢失”观点，旨在探究遗忘是否由权重更新导致的功能性擦除，还是由于模型内部表示结构的漂移导致的检索困难。

Method: 提出了一种“缝合评估协议”（stitched evaluation protocol），通过将后续任务更新后的网络早期计算与前序任务网络后期的计算进行组合，并引入任务特定的“传输密钥”（transport keys）作为接口对齐算子，用以恢复模型在旧任务上的性能表现。

Result: 实验证明，通过使用传输密钥，ResNet和视觉Transformer模型在处理Split CIFAR-100任务后，能够找回绝大部分旧任务的性能，验证了遗忘主要源于接口漂移的假设。

Conclusion: 灾难性遗忘并非仅仅源于权重的永久性改变或特征的擦除，很大程度上归因于模型内部阶段间的“接口漂移”（interface drift）。持续学习的未来研究方向应更多地关注如何索引和重新获取潜在的计算过程，而非仅局限于防止权重更新。

Abstract: Catastrophic forgetting is often framed as a representational problem: after sequential training, a model appears to lose the features that supported performance on earlier tasks. We challenge the stronger form of this view. Across controlled continual-learning settings, we find that a significant portion of apparent forgetting can be attributed to interface drift between internal stages rather than permanent erasure of task-relevant computation. We study this phenomenon through a stitched evaluation protocol that combines early computation from a post-update network with late computation from its predecessor, optionally mediated by a compact, task-specific transport key. We describe transport keys at a systems level as compact interface-alignment operators estimated from a small set of paired anchor activations and evaluated through model stitching. On split CIFAR-100 with a ResNet-style network, transport keys recover most of the original Task A performance after sequential training on Task B. On a compact vision transformer, we observe a similar recovery pattern. These results suggest that continual learning may require better mechanisms for indexing and re-accessing latent computations, not only methods that prevent weight change.

</details>


### [159] [KVarN: Variance-Normalized KV-Cache Quantization Mitigates Error Accumulation in Reasoning Tasks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03458)
*Lorenz K. Muller,Philippe Bich,Chiara Boretti,Hyun-Min Chang,Jiawei Zhuang,Lukas Cavigelli*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大模型长序列推理中 KV-cache 量化带来的误差累积难题，论文提出了 KVarN 方法，通过 Hadamard 旋转和方差归一化技术，实现了高质量的 2-bit KV-cache 量化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大模型推理中，测试时扩展（test-time scaling）对长序列生成至关重要，但受限于 KV-cache 的内存开销。现有的量化方法多针对预填充阶段，在自回归生成过程中会因错误的 Token 尺度导致量化误差随时间步长不断累积，从而影响模型推理性能。

Method: 提出了一种名为 KVarN 的免校准 KV-cache 量化方法。该方法通过应用 Hadamard 旋转将异常值分布均匀化，随后在 K 和 V 矩阵的两个轴上进行双重缩放的方差归一化（Dual-scaling Variance Normalization），从而消除错误的 Token 缩放带来的误差累积。

Result: KVarN 在 2-bit 低精度条件下，在 MATH500、AIME24 和 HumanEval 等生成式基准测试中达到了行业领先水平，显著减少了误差累积，并提供了开源的 vLLM 实现。

Conclusion: KVarN 通过 Hadamard 旋转和双重缩放方差归一化，有效解决了 KV-cache 在长序列推理中因量化误差累积导致的问题，在 2-bit 量化下实现了顶尖的生成性能，为大规模推理的内存优化提供了高效且免校准的解决方案。

Abstract: Test-time scaling is a powerful approach to obtain better reasoning in large language models, but it becomes memory-bottlenecked during long-horizon decoding, as the KV-cache grows. KV-cache quantization can help improve this, but current methods are evaluated under prefill-like settings and errors behave differently under autoregressive decoding. We show that in the latter regime, quantization errors accumulate across timesteps, driven primarily by incorrect token scales. We introduce KVarN, a calibration-free KV-cache quantizer that applies a Hadamard rotation followed by a dual-scaling variance normalization across both axes of the K and V matrices. We find that this combination fixes outlying token-scale errors and substantially reduces error accumulation over existing baselines. KVarN establishes a new state-of-theart for KV-cache quantization on generative benchmarks, including MATH500, AIME24 and HumanEval, at 2-bit precision. A vLLM implementation of the KVarN method is available at https://github.com/huawei-csl/KVarN

### [160] [Topology-Aware Gaussian Graph Repair for Robust Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03462)
*Anubha Goel,Juho Kanniainen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对图结构噪声和缺失问题，本文提出了TAGR框架，通过自适应高斯修复与残差修正技术，在保持稀疏性的前提下高效修复图拓扑，从而显著提升了GNN的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实应用中图结构往往存在噪声边（无关节点连接）或缺失边（信息传递受阻）。现有的方法要么仅能去除噪声边，要么通过学习新的图结构引入了过高的优化复杂度，且往往无法同时有效处理噪声和缺失边。

Method: 提出了“拓扑感知高斯修复（TAGR）”框架。该方法包含两个核心组件：1. 基于自适应高斯核构建稀疏特征邻域图，用于引入特征相似节点的辅助边；2. 拓扑感知残差修正，根据局部特征与结构一致性对原始图进行保留与重加权。修复后的图可直接用于标准GNN，无需修改其架构。

Result: 在基准引文网络上的实验表明，TAGR在噪声边和缺失边两种场景下均提升了GNN的鲁棒性。实验分析进一步指出，高斯特征邻域修复是鲁棒性提升的主要来源，而拓扑感知残差修正则增强了图不完整时的模型稳定性。

Conclusion: 本研究证明，通过轻量级的稀疏图修复（而非复杂的稠密图结构学习）即可有效提升图神经网络的鲁棒性。TAGR框架简单且易于集成，为解决不完美图拓扑问题提供了一种高效的通用方案。

Abstract: Graph neural networks have achieved strong performance on graph-structured data, but their effectiveness depends heavily on the quality of the observed graph. In real applications, graph topology is often imperfect: noisy edges may connect unrelated nodes, while missing edges may prevent useful information from being propagated. Existing robust graph learning methods mainly address this problem by removing suspicious edges or by learning a new graph structure during training. However, edge removal alone cannot recover missing connections, and graph structure learning may introduce additional optimization complexity. In this paper, we propose Topology-Aware Gaussian Repair (TAGR), a simple graph repair framework for robust message passing in graph neural networks. Instead of learning a dense adjacency matrix, TAGR constructs a sparse feature-neighborhood graph using an adaptive Gaussian kernel and combines it with a topology-aware residual correction of the observed graph. The Gaussian repair component introduces auxiliary edges between feature-similar nodes, while the residual correction preserves and reweights the original topology according to local feature and structural consistency. The repaired graph can be used directly with standard graph neural networks without changing their architectures. Extensive experiments on benchmark citation networks show that TAGR improves the robustness of GNNs under both noisy-edge and missing-edge settings. The analysis further show that Gaussian feature-neighborhood repair provides the main robustness gain, while topology-aware residual correction improves stability when the observed graph is incomplete. These results suggest that effective graph robustness can be achieved through lightweight sparse graph repair rather than dense graph structure learning.

### [161] [Are we really tilting? The mechanics of reward guidance in flow and diffusion models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02884)
*Sanjit Dandapanthula,Nicholas M. Boffi*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究揭示了扩散模型“奖励欺骗”的数学根源在于Doob h-函数的有限采样估计偏差，并通过闭式奖励阻尼策略及best-of-n采样机制成功解决了该问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 奖励引导扩散模型在推理阶段常出现“奖励欺骗”现象，即模型在盲目追求高奖励的同时牺牲了生成样本的分布保真度。现有研究多归因于神经网络的复杂性或训练偏差，但缺乏对该现象根本数学机制的理解。

Method: 1. 通过高斯和高斯混合目标分布的闭式分析，推导了Doob h-函数的有限粒子估计导致的两个核心失效模式（模态内偏差与模态选择失败）；2. 提出了一种无需额外计算量的闭式奖励阻尼（reward damping）调度方法；3. 定量分析了best-of-n采样在弥补模态选择缺陷中的作用。

Result: 1. 证明了即便在简单的二次奖励高斯任务中，标准的plug-in估计器也会产生系统性偏差；2. 验证了所提出的奖励阻尼策略能显著改善生成质量与奖励之间的平衡；3. 在包括2D棋盘格和大规模文生图模型FLUX.1的实验中，证明了该理论框架的有效性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，奖励引导扩散模型中的奖励欺骗（reward hacking）源于Doob h-函数的有限样本插值估计（plug-in estimation）偏差。作者提出的闭式奖励阻尼（reward damping）策略能有效纠正模态内偏差，并解释了“best-of-n”采样在模态选择中的互补作用。该理论在从高斯混合模型到FLUX.1等复杂生成模型中均得到了验证。

Abstract: Reward guidance algorithms steer a learned generative process toward the reward-tilted measure at inference time. While empirically powerful, these methods are prone to reward hacking: the guided model over-optimizes the reward at the cost of fidelity to the learned distribution. Prior work has attributed this to the complexity of neural reward functions or implicit biases in diffusion training, but its fundamental origins remain poorly understood. We show that reward hacking arises from an approximation made in most practical implementations of reward-guided diffusion -- finite-particle plug-in estimation of the Doob h-function -- even in the simplest non-trivial settings of Gaussian and Gaussian mixture targets with quadratic rewards. In closed form, we isolate two distinct failure modes of the plug-in estimator: it leads to reward hacking within each mode and it cannot select high-reward modes. We propose a closed-form reward damping schedule that corrects the within-mode bias with no additional compute, and clarify the role of best-of-n sampling in compensating for the mode selection failure. Experiments on Gaussian mixture targets, a 2D checkerboard, and FLUX.1 text-to-image generation confirm that our theoretical insights carry over to practical settings.

However, existing studies evaluate these methods in narrow settings, leaving unclear whether tensorization is effective at large-scale deployment. We systematically evaluate tensor compression across dense and MoE architectures, establishing performance trade-offs grounded in both empirical analysis and theoretical analysis. We identify a fundamental mismatch between the shared subspaces assumed by tensor decompositions and the heterogeneous representations learned by modern LLMs, thereby delineating their practical limits and clarifying their viable role in large-scale deployment. ### [163] [Scalable Uncertainty Quantification for Extreme Weather Forecasting via Empirical Neural Tangent Kernels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.02886)
*Jose Marie Antonio Miñoza,Rex Gregor Laylo,Sebastian C. Ibañez*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于神经正切核（NTK）的高效不确定性量化框架（NTK-UQ），通过动态选择特征分解技术，无需模型重训练即可显著提升极端天气预报的可靠性与自适应性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前深度学习天气预报模型虽然效率极高，但往往只能提供确定性预测，缺乏在极端天气决策中至关重要的不确定性评估能力，且现有的事后不确定性量化方法（如分位数预测）往往无法有效捕捉极端事件的波动性。

Method: 1. 基于神经正切核（NTK）的末层经验特征进行不确定性量化；2. 分析特征空间有效秩与方差坍缩机制，指出架构依赖性对不确定性估计的影响；3. 采用独立成分分析（ICA）或奇异值分解（SVD）提取特征，并根据特征谱集中度动态选择最佳分解方法；4. 仅需单次矩阵-向量乘法即可完成推理。

Result: 在保持 90% 覆盖率的情况下，NTK-UQ 相比分位数预测方法将预测区间尖锐度提高了 31%-37%，且能够生成随极端事件严重程度自适应调整的预测区间。

Conclusion: 本研究提出的 NTK-UQ 框架证明了无需重新训练即可为深度学习天气模型提供高效、自适应的不确定性量化。通过利用末层经验特征和矩阵分解技术，该方法能够精确识别极端天气事件，并提供比传统分位数预测法更尖锐、更具区分度的预测区间。

Abstract: Deep learning weather models now match numerical weather prediction accuracy while running orders of magnitude faster, but produce deterministic forecasts without uncertainty estimates, a critical gap for high-stakes decisions during extreme weather events. This paper proposes Neural Tangent Kernel-based uncertainty quantification (NTK-UQ) using last-layer empirical features. Theoretical analysis predicts that UQ quality is architecture-dependent through two mechanisms. First, a variance collapse mechanism explains when UQ fails: when the eigenvalue truncation rank approaches the effective rank of the feature space, the GP correction term consumes nearly all prior variance, destroying discrimination between tropical cyclones and routine conditions; architectures with concentrated spectra (spectral operators) require aggressive truncation ($k \leq 10$), while attention-based models tolerate full-rank computation. Second, decomposition performance depends on the non-Gaussian, heavy-tailed structure of extreme weather: Independent Component Analysis exploits higher-order statistics (kurtosis, negentropy) to isolate heavy-tailed extreme-event features, achieving higher discrimination than singular value decomposition, which captures only second-order variance. A data-driven selection rule chooses ICA or SVD from the feature eigenspectrum concentration ratio, correctly prescribing the superior decomposition for all four evaluated architectures. Compared to split conformal prediction (the natural post-hoc baseline), NTK-UQ achieves 31--37\% sharper prediction intervals at 90\% coverage, and uniquely produces \emph{adaptive} intervals that scale with extreme event severity, which conformal prediction cannot achieve by construction. The framework requires no retraining; inference-time uncertainty requires only a single matrix-vector product per sample.

### [164] [Analyzing Stream Collapse in Hyper-Connections: From Diagnosis to Mitigation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03483)
*Ekaterina Alimaskina,Gleb Molodtsov,Aleksandr Beznosikov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究人员使用了细粒度的诊断方法（fine-grained diagnostics）对基于HC的语言模型进行分析，追踪多流表示的实际使用情况，并对比了对称初始化与打破对称性初始化对模型性能的影响。

Result: 研究发现，经过早期的“种子阶段”后，残差混合往往保持在接近恒等映射的状态，限制了流间信息交换；此外，模型倾向于将信号和特征集中在单一的“主导流”中，导致多流结构的容量利用率不足，其表现类似于单流残差路径。

Conclusion: 超连接（HC）架构中存在对称性问题，且往往未能充分利用多流架构的潜力。通过在初始化阶段打破这种对称性，可以有效抑制“主导流”现象，并显著提升模型性能。

Abstract: Hyper-Connections (HC) replace the single Transformer residual stream with multiple streams, introducing a permutation symmetry over stream indices. We study how this symmetry is resolved in practice: whether streams specialize in a balanced way or exhibit dominant-stream usage. Using fine-grained diagnostics for HC-based language models, we trace how multi-stream representations are actually used. We find that after an early seeding stage, residual mixing often remains close to identity, limiting a core HC mechanism for exchanging information between streams. Moreover, both signal and interpretable features concentrate in a dominant stream, and the nominally multi-stream residual connection can underutilize its capacity, behaving closer to a single-stream residual pathway. Finally, we show that breaking symmetry at stream initialization reduces dominant behavior and improves performance across \textit{m}HC variants. Our code is publicly available.

### [165] [HiSE: A Lightweight Hierarchical Semantic Explainer for Heterogeneous Graph Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03495)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 HGNN 解释方法主要存在两大缺陷：一是无法反映 HGNN 固有的语义层级结构，导致解释缺乏保真度；二是依赖复杂的搜索或扰动机制，造成计算开销过大、效率低下，难以在高风险应用中落地。

Method: 提出了一种名为 HiSE 的轻量级特征导向解释模型。该方法包含两个关键步骤：1. 在语义层，利用基于 LASSO 的局部代理模型学习各语义视图下的稀疏特征表示；2. 在跨语义层，通过 KL 散度自适应地刻画不同语义视图的贡献，从而生成统一的解释结果。

Result: 实验结果表明，HiSE 在保真度、鲁棒性以及跨语义解释能力方面均优于现有主流方法，且因其轻量级架构，具备极高的计算效率，能够在大规模复杂异构图上高效运行。

Conclusion: HiSE 通过层次化语义建模，有效解决了异构图神经网络（HGNN）在解释性方面的保真度与计算效率问题，为高风险应用领域提供了一种高效、可靠且具有语义感知能力的解释工具。

Abstract: Heterogeneous graph neural networks (HGNNs) have demonstrated remarkable performance in modeling complex relational data, however their interpretability in high-stakes applications remains a critical challenge. Existing explanation methods suffer from two major limitations: on the one hand, the generated explanations fail to reflect the inherent semantic hierarchy of HGNNs, resulting in a lack of fidelity to the model's internal decision-making mechanism; on the other hand, feature explanations often rely on complex search or perturbation mechanisms, leading to excessive computational complexity and poor efficiency. To address these issues, we propose HiSE, a lightweight feature-oriented interpretable model for HGNNs. HiSE achieves semantically aware feature explanations through hierarchical semantic modeling: at the semantic level, local surrogate models based on the Least Absolute Shrinkage and Selection Operator (LASSO) are employed to learn sparse feature representations under each semantic view; at the cross-semantic level, the contributions of different semantic views are adaptively characterized via KL divergence to produce a unified explanation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that HiSE outperforms existing methods in terms of fidelity, robustness, and cross-semantic explanation capability, while its lightweight framework incurs low computational overhead, enabling efficient application to large-scale, complex real-world heterogeneous graphs.

### [166] [Demystifying Pipeline Parallelism: First Theory for PipeDream](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03498)
*Ivan Ilin,Peter Richtárik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文深入剖析了流水线并行（PipeDream）的理论基础与扩展性局限，证明了其收敛性并量化了由流水线深度带来的梯度陈旧性损耗，同时对比了其与LocalSGD在不同场景下的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着现代机器学习模型规模的扩大，计算必须分布在多个加速器上。虽然数据并行是主流，但在模型参数、激活值或优化器状态超出单设备内存限制时，流水线并行变得不可或缺。研究旨在解决PipeDream类方法在理论收敛性证明上的缺失，并量化其在大规模分布式训练中的延迟代价与扩展性瓶颈。

Method: 1. 理论建模：提出了Randomized PipeDream (RPD) 抽象，基于陈旧块随机梯度下降（Stale block-SGD）分析非凸收敛性；
2. 扩展性诊断：数学推导了PipeDream稳态延迟与流水线阶段数（S）的关系，分析了陈旧梯度更新对收敛的影响；
3. 实验对比：通过模拟实验，将PipeDream与LocalSGD在不同目标函数（二次目标、语言模型损失、逻辑回归）下的性能进行了对比分析。

Result: 1. 首次为PipeDream类方法提供了清晰的非凸收敛性保证；
2. 证明了PipeDream的延迟随阶段数S呈平方级增长（S^2），其陈旧梯度对收敛的影响随阶段数呈四次方关系（Θ(S^4)）；
3. 实验显示，对于简单的二次目标和特定的小型语言模型任务，PipeDream表现更好；但对于逻辑回归等任务，随着阶段数增加，LocalSGD因其同步机制的优势在特定条件下表现更佳。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了流水线模型并行（PipeDream）在扩展性上的理论瓶颈，并为理解分布式训练中异步机制（如延迟梯度更新）的收敛性提供了严谨的数学框架。研究表明，不同分布式训练方法（PipeDream与LocalSGD）的优劣取决于特定的目标函数和系统规模。

Abstract: Training modern machine learning models increasingly requires computation to be distributed across many accelerators. Data parallelism remains the default choice and is often paired with tensor-parallel sharding, but model parallelism becomes unavoidable once parameters, activations, or optimizer states no longer fit on a single device. This paper studies pipeline model parallelism through the lens of PipeDream (PD) (Harlap et al., 2018). Our first contribution is theoretical: we introduce Randomized PipeDream (RPD), a stale block-SGD abstraction that yields, to our knowledge, the first clean nonconvex convergence guarantee for a PD-style method. Our second contribution is a scaling diagnosis: we prove that the delay induced by steady-state PD grows as $S^2 - S/2 + O(1)$ for $S$ stages, so the stale-read contribution in the convergence theorem scales as $Θ(γ^2 S^4)$, equivalently as $Θ(S^4/K)$ in the tuned-rate form. Our third contribution is a comparison with LocalSGD, whose periodic model averaging trades weight staleness for synchronization bubbles. In our reported simulated-time experiments, the better-performing method depends on the objective: PD performs better on the quadratic objective and on a small language-modeling training-loss task, while for logistic regression LocalSGD becomes superior as the number of stages increases.

</details>

On the server side, an evolution agent aggregates these patches to dynamically model client-specific capability boundaries, facilitating strictly personalized skill evolution rather than a suboptimal global average. Conclusion: 本文提出了一种无需额外训练即可提升深度强化学习智能体鲁棒性的有效方法，证明了结合模型预测控制与对抗性推理可以在保持计算效率的同时，显著增强智能体在面对环境扰动时的稳定性。

Abstract: To improve the real-world applicability of reinforcement learning (RL), the field of adversarially robust RL studies how to train agents under adversarial environment perturbations. In this setting, a protagonist agent optimizes a policy under environmental perturbations from an adversary, resulting in a zero-sum Markov game. When adversarially robust RL is combined with model-based RL, the adversary can target a learned transition model instead of the training environment. Extending this idea, this work introduces post-hoc robustification of deep RL agents at inference time. By using the learned model in combination with a trained nominal policy, our approach performs a robust policy improvement step. The goal is to improve robustness without any additional training of neural networks. Specifically, we utilize model-predictive control under adversarial rollouts, which are approximated via projected gradient descent within a bounded uncertainty set. Furthermore, these offline rollouts are performed while considering and mitigating out-of-distribution issues. The proposed methodology is validated by demonstrating significant improvements in robustness when the algorithm is evaluated in perturbed Gymnasium MuJoCo environments, while considering the computational limitations of the post-hoc inference setting.

### [169] [When Should the Teacher Move? Temporal Coupling and Stability in Self On-Policy Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03532)
*Haowei Guo,Baolong Bi,Ruicheng Zhang,Bingqian Sun,Wentao Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对自我同策略蒸馏中的训练不稳定问题，研究发现“教师更新隔离期”是关键，并提出CGTR机制，通过基于性能指标的门控刷新替代固定时钟更新，有效解决了长期训练中的崩溃现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自我同策略蒸馏中，教师更新的时间调度作为影响训练稳定性的关键变量尚未被系统研究。现有的固定调度机制在长周期训练中容易导致“状态遗忘性崩溃”，使得学生模型在训练中发生不可逆的性能倒退，且这种失效模式在短期评估中难以被发现。

Method: 1. 建立了诊断框架（包括时间KL结构、刷新冲击和长度尾部风险），以分析训练动态。2. 提出“整合门控教师刷新（CGTR）”机制，在保持隔离期的前提下，根据奖励提升和尾部长度安全的联合证据动态触发教师更新，而非基于固定的时钟信号。

Conclusion: 该研究揭示了自我同策略蒸馏中教师更新机制对训练稳定性的核心影响，证明了“隔离期”而非“教师年龄”是稳定训练的关键。提出的CGTR方法通过基于奖励提升和长度尾部安全性的门控更新机制，有效消除了状态遗忘性崩溃，实现了在多种任务上的鲁棒学习。

Abstract: Self on-policy distillation trains a student policy against a teacher derived from its own parameter history, yet the teacher's update schedule -- which governs the \emph{temporal coupling} between teacher and student -- has not been systematically studied as a stability variable. Through a controlled schedule sweep on Qwen3-8B, we establish that \emph{isolation periods}, defined as complete teacher freezing between updates, are the key structural property enabling stable learning, not teacher age. To characterize these underlying training dynamics, we introduce a diagnostic framework of temporal KL structure, refresh shock, and length-tail risk. This framework further uncovers \emph{state-oblivious collapse}: optimal short-horizon fixed schedules catastrophically fail under long-horizon training because a clock-driven refresh can copy a transiently drifting student into the teacher in a single, irreversible step. This failure mode is invisible under short-horizon evaluation and mechanistically distinct from EMA's chronic contamination. To address this, we propose \emph{Consolidation-Gated Teacher Refresh} (CGTR), which preserves isolation periods while gating each refresh on joint evidence of reward improvement and length-tail safety, ensuring every teacher movement responds to genuine student consolidation rather than a clock signal. With a single shared parameter set and no per-dataset retuning, CGTR achieves \textbf{zero collapse} and the best final score on all four tasks (Chemistry, Biology, Physics, ToolUse), self-regulating its refresh frequency to each task's learning dynamics.

### [170] [How Many Trees in a Random Forest? A Revisited Approach with Plateau Search and Optuna Integration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03549)
*Vadim Porvatov,Andrey Dukhovny,Andrey Lange*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对随机森林中树数量优化难题，本文提出了一种基于OOB分数三元组的动态平台搜索算法，能够根据数据特性自适应确定最优的森林规模，无需预设搜索范围，显著优于传统的固定启发式方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机森林中树的数量优化面临挑战：由于预测性能通常随树的数量增加呈单调递增，传统超参数优化方法（如TPE、Hyperband）往往受限于预定义的搜索空间，且倾向于在边界处搜索，而现有的早停策略又容易受到噪声干扰导致过早停止。因此，需要一种能够动态确定最佳树数量的有效方法。

Method: 提出了一种基于“三元组平台搜索”的集成方法。该方法将树的数量从传统的TPE搜索空间中移除，改为通过监控三个森林规模（三元组）下袋外（OOB）分数的相对变化，自适应地追踪接近最小的充分森林规模，并基于一个容差参数进行自动化控制。此外，文中还通过理论分析建立了OOB分数标准与当前分数及极限分数之间差距的数学关系。

Result: 实验结果表明，该方法选定的树数量与传统启发式方法（通常设为固定值）存在显著差异：在大多数经典基准数据集上所需的树数量更少；而在某些高维生物信息学数据集（如Arcene和Dorothea）上则需要更多树。该方法不仅提高了搜索效率，还增强了结果的可解释性。

Conclusion: 该研究通过提出的基于三元组的平台搜索算法，成功将随机森林中树的数量优化问题转化为一个更具可解释性且自动化的过程，克服了传统方法对预定义搜索范围的依赖，并为不同复杂度的数据集提供了更优的树数量选择策略。

Abstract: Hyperparameter optimization (HPO) for Random Forest faces a specific difficulty in tuning the number of trees: the predictive score typically improves monotonically with ensemble size, so standard methods such as Tree-structured Parzen Estimator (TPE) and Hyperband require a predefined search range and often drive the estimate toward its right boundary. Early-stopping strategies avoid fixing such a range, but can be sensitive to score noise and prone to premature stopping. To address this, we propose an integrated triplet-based plateau-search algorithm that removes the number of trees from the direct TPE search space and still exploits information accumulated across HPO trials. The method adaptively tracks a near-minimal sufficient ensemble size by monitoring relative changes in the out-of-bag (OOB) score across a triplet of forest sizes and shifting this triplet accordingly. This yields an automated and user-interpretable procedure based on a tolerance parameter. We also provide a theoretical analysis: we relate the proposed relative OOB-score criterion to the gap between the current and limiting scores, and derive an asymptotic variance estimate for the corresponding OOB-based absolute relative difference. Experiments show that the selected number of trees can differ substantially from the common heuristic: for most classical benchmark datasets it is smaller, whereas for some high-dimensional bioinformatics datasets, such as Arcene and Dorothea, it is larger. The source code and reproducible experiments are available at https://github.com/lange-am/rf_plateau_hpo.

*Yohei Kakimoto,Yuto Omae,Hirotaka Takahashi*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RBF-SVR模型的预测函数是非凸的，直接进行优化存在困难。现有的优化方法缺乏对其收敛特性及超参数影响的定量分析，亟需一种能够利用核函数解析结构的方法来系统地评估优化性能。

Method: 利用高斯径向基函数（RBF）核的解析结构，构建了RBF-SVR预测函数的显式DC（Difference of Convex）分解，并导出了DC分量强凸参数下界 $\mu$ 和子问题梯度Lipschitz常数上界 $L$ 的封闭解。

Result: 数值实验证实，$\mu$ 和 $L$ 均由 $C_αρ$ 主导。该标量量化了收敛特性与初始点的依赖关系，并揭示了优化行为是如何通过超参数 $(C, γ)$ 在训练前后发生关联的。

Abstract: For nonconvex optimization problems whose objective is the prediction function of a trained Support Vector Regression (SVR) model with the Gaussian radial basis function (RBF) kernel (RBF-SVR), we present a framework that applies the difference of convex functions (DC) algorithm (DCA) by exploiting the analytical structure of the RBF kernel to construct an explicit DC decomposition. Specifically, we derive in closed form both the lower bound $μ$ of the strong convexity parameter of the DC components and the upper bound $L$ of the gradient Lipschitz constant of the subproblem. Both $μ$ and $L$ are determined solely by the post-training dual-coefficient sum $C_α$ and the RBF kernel parameter $γ$, together with the DC decomposition parameter $ρ$, and they share a common leading term $C_αρ$. Through numerical experiments on six benchmark functions, we show that $C_αρ$ is the primary single quantity characterizing both the convergence properties and the initial-point dependence of DCA, and further demonstrate that it decomposes into two independent pathways, $C \to C_α$ and $γ\to ρ$, with its primary variation governed by the SVR hyperparameters $(C, γ)$. Together, these results allow the convergence properties of DCA on RBF-SVR to be assessed in advance through the single scalar quantity $C_αρ$: approximately from $(C, γ)$ before training, and exactly in closed form after training.

However, EP's practical applications have so far remained limited to relatively small-scale problems. Predictive coding networks (PCNs), another class of energy-based models rooted in computational neuroscience, are typically trained with a specialized algorithm and have likewise not yet been demonstrated at large scale. In this work, we develop an EP-based training method for PCNs which combines the centered variant of EP with a novel equilibration scheme for PCNs. Using this approach, we train a 10-layer convolutional PCN (VGG10) on full-size ImageNet, achieving 13.23\% test error rate on the top-5 classification task, close to the 12.2\% backpropagation baseline. ### [173] [CauTion: Knowing When to Trust LLMs for Ensemble Causal Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03602)
*Bo Peng,Kaiwen Wu,Sirui Chen,Zhiheng Wang,Yu Qiao,Chaochao Lu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: CauTion 是一种通过算法集成投票与可信度校准机制整合 LLM 领域知识的新型因果发现框架，实现了比传统方法更准确、更稳健的因果图推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纯统计方法难以处理等价类区分及小样本问题；而现有的 LLM 增强型因果发现方法存在易受 LLM 错误干扰、成本高昂及对单一算法偏见敏感的问题，亟需一种可靠的集成框架来整合 LLM 先验知识。

Method: 提出名为 CauTion 的三阶段框架：1. 使用算法集成进行共识投票以初步确定边；2. 实施无标注的信任校准机制，动态权衡 LLM 与统计算法的可靠性，仅在算法证据不足时引入 LLM；3. 执行循环修复步骤以确保最终生成的因果图满足无环约束。

Result: 在六个数据集上的实验表明，CauTion 在因果发现的准确性上持续优于现有的数据驱动基准和 LLM 增强基准，尤其在大型图中优势显著，且对 LLM 的潜在错误表现出极强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: CauTion 框架通过结合算法集成和经过可信度校准的 LLM 辅助决策，有效克服了传统因果发现方法在区分马尔可夫等价类及依赖单一算法时的局限性，实现了更高精度和鲁棒性的因果图构建。

Abstract: Causal discovery from observational data remains challenging due to the fundamental limitations of purely statistical methods, such as statistical distinguishability within equivalence classes and sensitivity to finite sample sizes. While large language models (LLMs) offer a promising source of domain knowledge to complement statistical inference, existing LLM-augmented methods are vulnerable to LLM errors and incur high token costs. Moreover, reliance on a single data-centric algorithm can make results sensitive to algorithm-specific biases. To address these limitations, we propose CauTion, a framework that reliably integrates LLM domain knowledge into an ensemble of statistical causal discovery algorithms through consensus filtering and LLM reliability estimation. CauTion proceeds in three stages. First, an algorithm ensemble utilizes a consensus voting to resolve up to 96% of edges on which algorithms agree, achieving near-perfect accuracy on the filtered consensus edges. Second, a trust-calibrated arbitration mechanism estimates the relative reliability of the LLM and the algorithms via an annotation-free trust calibration procedure, which is then utilized to govern a trust-weighted voting process that restricts LLM arbitration exclusively to edges with unreliable algorithmic evidence. Third, a cycle repair step is applied to guarantee the final causal graph is validly acyclic. Experiments on six datasets demonstrate that CauTion consistently outperforms both data-centric and LLM-augmented baselines, with larger gains on larger graphs and strong robustness to LLM errors. Code is available at https://github.com/OpenCausaLab/CauTion.

### [174] [Exploiting Verification-Generation Gap: Test-Time Reinforcement Learning with Confidence-Conditioned Verification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03608)
*Jiahui Li,Jianfeng Shan,Wenpei Chen,Shunyu Wu,Jian Lou,Wenjie Feng,Dan Li,See-Kiong Ng*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文针对大语言模型测试时强化学习中优化Pass@k困难的问题，提出TTRL-CoCoV框架，通过置信度条件下的差异化策略解决了伪标签错误与多样性坍缩挑战，显著提升了模型在复杂推理任务中的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时强化学习（Test-time RL）研究多关注Pass@1表现，但如何优化衡量生成覆盖率的Pass@k指标在无标签环境下仍未得到充分探索，且现有的RLVR（强化学习验证奖励）方法在提升Pass@k时存在伪标签估计错误和高置信度样本多样性坍缩等瓶颈。

Method: 提出TTRL-CoCoV（置信度条件验证测试时强化学习）框架。该方法基于“验证能力优于生成能力”的洞察，根据样本的置信度采取不同策略：1. 高置信度样本：增强验证器并施加鼓励探索的奖励，防止多样性坍缩；2. 低置信度样本：利用验证器过滤错误的伪标签；3. 中置信度样本：绕过验证过程。

Result: 在6个主流推理基准测试中，TTRL-CoCoV表现优于现有最优方法。与TTRL相比，Pass@1平均提升9.8%，Pass@16平均提升18.7%；与全监督强化学习方法相比，在多个推理基准上的Pass@1最高提升达5.0%。

Conclusion: 该论文提出的TTRL-CoCoV框架通过针对不同置信度样本采取差异化的验证与探索策略，成功解决了测试时强化学习在优化Pass@k时面临的伪标签错误与多样性坍缩问题，为提升大语言模型的复杂推理能力提供了一种高效且无需标签的通用范式。

Abstract: Test-time reinforcement learning has emerged as a promising paradigm for enhancing the complex reasoning abilities of large language models in a completely label-free manner. Despite existing studies focusing on Pass@1 performance, optimizing Pass@k remains under-explored yet critical in label-free settings, which measures generation coverage for sustained exploration. Optimizing Pass@k in label-free setting is highly non-trivial, as directly applying the Pass@k advantage designs effective for RLVR yields unsatisfactory performance. Through in-depth empirical analysis, we discover the root causes hindering performance: pseudo-label estimations for low-confidence samples have a high probability of being incorrect, while candidate answers for high-confidence samples suffer from severe diversity collapse. To overcome these hurdles, we propose TTRL-CoCoV (Test-Time Reinforcement Learning with Confidence-Conditioned Verification), a novel confidence-adaptive framework that expands Pass@k coverage and improves Pass@1 performance. Based on our key insight that verification capability generally leads generation capability, TTRL-CoCoV employs a confidence-conditioned mechanism: for high-confidence samples, it bootstraps verifier and applies an exploration-enhancing reward to prevent diversity collapse; for low-confidence samples, it delegates pseudo-label selection to the verifier to filter incorrect pseudo-labels; and for medium-confidence samples, it bypasses verification entirely. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TTRL-CoCoV outperforms the best competing methods across 6 widely-recognized benchmarks, achieves average absolute gains of +9.8% in Pass@1 and +18.7% in Pass@16 over TTRL, and even achieves absolute Pass@1 improvements of up to +5.0% across multiple reasoning benchmarks when compared against fully supervised RL methods. Our code repository: https://github.com/shanjf666/CoCoV.

</details>


### [175] [Physics-Guided Policy Optimization with Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03620)
*Ke Wang,Yuning Wu,Haoran Liu,Chaoqun Jia,Devin Chen,Kai Wei*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对LLM自蒸馏训练中步长敏感导致的不稳定问题，本文提出了一种物理引导的策略优化方法（PGPO），通过互信息动态调制更新步长，实现了更稳定高效的训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的自蒸馏策略优化（SDPO）在训练过程中对更新步长的敏感性较高，因为自教师产生的反馈在不同批次间质量差异大，固定的步长会导致训练不稳定甚至崩溃。

Method: 受粘性流体动力学启发，在随机微分方程（SDE）层面将策略优化形式化。提出了“物理引导策略优化”（PGPO），引入了一个基于学生预测与反馈条件教师之间互信息估计的步长调制乘子，用于动态调整更新步长。

Result: 在Science-QA数据集上，PGPO在4个领域中的3个优于SDPO，最高提升了4.5个百分点，且在SDPO发生训练崩溃的场景下仍能保持稳定性。

Conclusion: PGPO通过引入互信息调制步长，有效解决了SDPO在训练后期不稳定的问题，并提升了模型在多领域任务上的表现，证明了将物理动力学思想引入策略优化的有效性。

Abstract: Self-distilled policy optimization (SDPO) has become a popular paradigm for LLM post-training, where a model learns from its own predictions conditioned on privileged information. SDPO, however, is sensitive to how much each update step should be trusted: corrections from a self-teacher can be highly informative on some batches and misleading on others, and applying them uniformly with a fixed step size can destabilize training. Drawing inspiration from viscous-fluid dynamics and formalizing the analogy at the SDE level, we propose Physics-Guided Policy Optimization (PGPO), which introduces an information-modulated step-size multiplier derived from a mutual-information estimate between the student's predictions and the feedback-conditioned teacher. We show that this modulation preserves the order-1 weak-approximation guarantees of vanilla SGD, and incurs negligible overhead per iteration. We evaluate PGPO on the Science-QA dataset, where it outperforms SDPO on 3 of the 4 domains with gains of up to +4.5 points, while remaining stable in a setting where SDPO collapses late in training.

</details>


### [176] [AnchorMoE: Interpretable Time Series Classification via Anchor-Routed MoE](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03631)
*Tao Xie,Zexi Tan,Haoyi Xiao,Mengke Li,Yiqun Zhang,Yang Lu,Cuie Yang,Yiu-ming Cheung*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了 AnchorMoE，一种具备内置可解释性的多元时间序列分类框架。通过混合专家架构、几何正交约束和不确定性感知门控，实现了对时间序列决策路径的精确分解与噪声抑制，解决了复杂时序数据中可解释性与分类性能难以兼顾的难题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多元时间序列分类（MTSC）在临床诊断等高风险领域应用广泛，但现有的模型往往难以解释。现有的可解释性方法多为事后（Post-hoc）估计，难以准确捕捉稀疏且被噪声掩盖的判别性时序信号。因此，研究旨在构建一种“构造性可解释（Interpretable-by-construction）”的分类框架，直接从原始时序中溯源决策。

Method: 1. 基于混合专家（MoE）架构，通过对局部片段的多视图编码与路由，实现模型预测的精确加法分解（Ante-hoc 透明度）；2. 引入几何正交约束（Geometric Orthogonality Constraint），强制不同专家专注于异构预测模式，减少表示冗余；3. 设计不确定性感知可靠性门控机制（Uncertainty-aware Reliability Gate），动态校准片段贡献度，抑制背景噪声影响。

Result: 在多个真实世界及合成数据集上的实验表明，AnchorMoE 不仅实现了具有竞争力的分类准确率，还能有效将决策精准定位于原始时序的特定片段，证明了其在提供预测结果的同时具备高度的决策可信度。

Conclusion: AnchorMoE 提供了一种高性能且具备内置可解释性的 MTSC 解决方案，证明了通过结构化设计（MoE 架构与几何约束）可以实现模型预测与决策依据的高度一致，为临床医疗等高风险领域提供了可靠的决策支持工具。

Abstract: Multivariate time series classification (MTSC) is pivotal in high-stakes domains, such as clinical diagnosis and industrial fault detection, where safe deployment necessitates transparent decision-making. However, isolating the temporal segments that drive model predictions is challenging because discriminative signals in real-world time series are typically sparse, heterogeneous, and heavily obscured by background noise. This paper, therefore, proposes AnchorMoE, an interpretable-by-construction classification framework. Built upon a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architecture, AnchorMoE encodes multi-view representations of local patches and routes them to specialized experts, ensuring that the final prediction is formulated as an exact additive decomposition over the input segments, facilitating ante-hoc transparency rather than relying on post-hoc estimations. To maintain the reliability of this decomposition under sparse signal distributions, we introduce a geometric orthogonality constraint that penalizes representational redundancy, compelling distinct experts to specialize in heterogeneous predictive patterns. Furthermore, an uncertainty-aware reliability gate is designed to dynamically calibrate the contribution of each segment, effectively suppressing residual background noise. Extensive experiments on real-world and synthetic benchmarks demonstrate that AnchorMoE achieves highly competitive classification performance while faithfully grounding its decisions in the raw time series.

### [177] [Dynamic Short Convolutions Improve Transformers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03825)
*Oliver Sieberling,Bharat Runwal,Rameswar Panda,Yoon Kim*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本论文提出了一种名为“动态短卷积”的新型神经网络基元。通过使用输入依赖的滤波器，该方法显著提升了Transformer模型在语言建模任务中的表达能力与计算效率，并被证明在多种主流模型架构中均具有通用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Transformer架构在大型语言模型中占据主导地位，但现有组件在捕捉局部特征和关联性检索任务上仍有改进空间。研究者旨在通过引入一种能够增强模型表达能力且具备硬件高效性的卷积基元，来进一步提升Transformer及其变体的性能。

Method: 本研究引入了“动态短卷积”（Dynamic Short Convolutions）作为Transformer的附加组件。不同于静态卷积，动态卷积使用依赖于输入的滤波器（Input-dependent filters），从而在保留卷积局部性偏置的同时提升了模型的表达能力。研究团队还开发了定制的Triton内核，以确保该方法在实际训练中的高效性。

Result: 实验表明，在150M至2B参数规模的语言模型任务中，动态卷积在关联性检索任务上表现优异，且在计算资源匹配的情况下，相较于标准Transformer分别具备1.33倍至1.60倍的计算优势。此外，该方法还能有效提升线性RNN（如Mamba-2）和混合专家（MoE）模型的性能。

Conclusion: 动态短卷积是一种高效、可扩展且具备高表达能力的神经元基元，能够显著提升Transformer及其他架构的性能。通过定制的Triton内核，该方法在保持训练效率的同时，实现了优于标准Transformer的计算优势。

Abstract: Transformers have become the dominant architecture for large language models, largely due to the scalability and flexibility of attention, feed-forward layers, residual connections, and normalization. This paper introduces dynamic short convolutions as an additional neural network primitive for improving Transformers. Unlike static short convolutions, dynamic convolutions use input-dependent filters, which preserves the locality bias of convolution while increasing expressivity. Motivating experiments show that applying dynamic short convolutions to key, query, and value representations improves performance on challenging associative recall tasks compared with static convolutional variants. Across language-modeling experiments ranging from 150M to 2B parameters, dynamic convolutions consistently outperform standard Transformers and Transformers augmented with static short convolutions. Fitting scaling laws indicates a 1.33$\times$ compute advantage over compute-matched Transformers when dynamic convolutions are applied to the key, query, and value vectors, and a 1.60$\times$ advantage when adding dynamic convolutions after every linear layer. Dynamic convolutions also offer improvements on linear RNNs (Mamba-2/Gated DeltaNet) and mixture-of-experts architectures. We make these gains practical with custom Triton kernels that enable efficient training with a manageable end-to-end slowdown. These results suggest that dynamic short convolutions are a scalable, hardware-efficient, and expressive primitive for advancing Transformer-based language models.

In this study, we present a Spatial Transcriptomics-guided Alignment framework for Molecular Profiling (STAMP), which endows PFMs with intrinsic molecular awareness. To support this paradigm, we curated HumanST-1k, a human ST dataset spanning diverse anatomical organs and sequencing platforms. This atlas yields 1.8 million pairs of H&E patches and corresponding transcriptomic profiles, providing a corpus that links histological structures with their molecular states. To mitigate the technical noise inherent to raw transcriptomics, STAMP applies a pathway-informed alignment strategy that aggregates transcriptomic data into biologically functional pathways, which are subsequently integrated into PFMs via parameter-efficient fine-tuning. This alignment enriches the representation space of PFMs and unlocks their capacity to resolve sub-visual molecular signatures. ### [179] [The Shape of Addition: Geometric Structures of Arithmetic in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03645)
*Liuyuan Wen,Xun Zhu,Lihao Huang,Wenbin Li,Yang Gao*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文揭示了大语言模型算术错误的几何根源，即内部连续计算在转化为离散输出时产生的“量化滑移”，并据此提出了一种基于几何一致性的错误检测与修正方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在基础算术任务中表现出的脆弱性与其强大的计算能力存在矛盾，作者旨在揭示这种“逻辑断层”背后的底层几何机制，并探索如何利用这种机制来提高模型的鲁棒性和可解释性。

Method: 1. 几何分析：通过分析残差流（residual stream）中的几何结构，识别出“等原始和轨迹”（IRST）。2. 建模：提出“噪声量化模型”（Noisy Quantization Model），将算术错误定义为内部神经噪声导致的几何滑移。3. 探测验证：通过探针技术验证了从单个激活向量中解耦潜在信号的能力。4. 应用验证：开发了一种几何一致性检查方法，用于推理阶段的错误检测与修正。

Result: 1. 发现了残差流中的IRST结构，揭示了算术计算在连续潜空间中的表示方式；2. 证实了算术错误源于潜变量越过量化阈值；3. 证明了轻量级探针能够从单一激活向量中同时提取多种潜在信息；4. 验证了几何一致性检查在实际推理中纠正量化错误的可行性。

Conclusion: 大语言模型在算术任务中的错误并非简单的逻辑缺失，而是源于神经表示空间中连续潜变量与离散输出之间的“量化滑移”。通过几何视角理解这种内部机制，能够有效提升模型的可解释性并提供实时的纠错方案。

Abstract: Large Language Models exhibit paradoxical fragility in fundamental arithmetic, implying a disconnect between internal computation and discrete output. By analyzing the residual stream geometry during multi-operand addition, we identify the Iso-Raw-Sum Trajectory (IRST), a geometric structure where representations are anchored by semantic digits and modulated by continuous carry fibers. We propose the Noisy Quantization Model to explain this geometry, framing arithmetic errors as Geometric Slippages caused by internal neural noise pushing a continuous, latent Carry Potential across quantization thresholds. This geometric framework further elucidates Probe Versatility, explaining how lightweight probes can disentangle coexisting latent signals (such as ground truth versus hallucination) from a single activation vector. Finally, we validate these insights through a geometric consistency check method that effectively detects and corrects these quantization failures during inference. Our code is available at https://github.com/RL-MIND/Shape-of-Addition.

### [180] [Value-Aware Stochastic KV Cache Eviction for Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03928)
*Ting-Yun Chang,Harvey Yiyun Fu,Deqing Fu,Chenghao Yang,Jesse Thomason,Robin Jia*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对长思维链推理模型的 KV 缓存瓶颈，本文提出了 VaSE 方法。它通过保护异常大数值的状态并引入随机淘汰机制，在大幅压缩内存占用的同时，显著提升了推理模型的精度，填补了传统淘汰方法与稀疏注意力机制之间的性能差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推理模型通过长思维链（CoT）提升准确率，但长输出导致了严重的显存和计算瓶颈。现有的 KV 缓存淘汰方法往往会牺牲模型精度，而稀疏注意力机制又无法降低缓存占用，作者旨在寻找一种既能高效压缩 KV 缓存，又能保持高推理性能的方案。

Method: 提出了一种名为“VaSE（Value-aware Stochastic KV Cache Eviction）”的无需训练的 KV 缓存淘汰策略。其核心机制包括：1. 识别并保护具有异常大数值的“值状态（Value states）”，防止因关键信息丢失导致的推理重复或崩溃；2. 在淘汰过程中引入随机性（Stochasticity）以增强缓存的多样性。该方法支持 FlashAttention2，并实现了静态内存占用。

Result: 在六项推理任务测试中，使用 VaSE 进行 4 倍 KV 缓存压缩的 Qwen3 模型，在同等稀疏度下表现优于现有的 SOTA 选择方法，且比最强的现有淘汰方法精度提升超过 4%，成功实现了效率与精度的平衡。

Conclusion: VaSE 证明了在无需额外训练的情况下，通过保护关键值状态并引入随机性，可以在大幅降低 KV 缓存需求的同时保持高推理精度，从而有效缓解了推理模型在长思维链下的计算与存储瓶颈。

Abstract: Reasoning models improve accuracy through extended chains of thought, but their long outputs create a memory and compute bottleneck. KV cache eviction methods reduce this cost by evicting unimportant key-value pairs from the cache, yet they often yield worse accuracy than selection-based sparse attention alternatives, which keep the full KV cache. We identify key factors crucial to KV cache eviction accuracy. First, a small fraction of value states have abnormally large magnitudes, and evicting them causes catastrophic failure where models enter repetitive reasoning loops. Second, introducing stochasticity during eviction improves accuracy by increasing cache diversity. Based on these findings, we propose Value-aware Stochastic KV Cache Eviction (VaSE), a training-free recipe that protects large-magnitude value states and promotes diverse eviction decisions. Across six reasoning tasks, Qwen3 models using VaSE with 4x KV cache compression yield higher average accuracies than SOTA selection method at the same sparsity, while outperforming the strongest eviction method by more than 4%. Overall, VaSE bridges the gap between efficiency and accuracy, supporting FlashAttention2 and enabling a static memory footprint for reasoning models.

The speedrun format provides a simple protocol for the community to add, verify, and stack pretraining improvements, with the leaderboard open to contributions. ### [182] [Skill-RM: Unifying Heterogeneous Evaluation Criteria via Agent Skill](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03980)
*Tao Chen,Gangwei Jiang,Pengyu Cheng,Siyuan Huang,Yihao Liu,Jingwei Ni,Jiaqi Guo,Mengyu Zhou,Kai Tang,Junling Liu,Qinliang Su,Xiaoxi Jiang,Guanjun Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: Skill-RM 是一种将奖励建模统一为结构化代理任务的新框架，通过动态编排异构证据来源，显著提升了 LLM 奖励评估的准确性、一致性和透明度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的奖励模型（RM）评估标准高度碎片化且异构，缺乏一个能够整合规则、参考数据、检查清单和评估准则的统一机制。作者旨在构建一个统一的框架，以解决当前奖励评估中一致性和透明度不足的问题。

Method: 提出了 Skill-RM 框架，将奖励建模重构为“奖励评估技能”（Reward-Evaluation Skill）的执行过程。该方法将奖励计算视为一个结构化的代理（agentic）任务，能够动态地编排、选择和聚合包括规则验证器、真值参考、过程检查清单及复杂准则等异构评估证据。

Result: 在多个奖励评估基准及下游应用（如 Best-of-N 选择和强化学习）的实验中，Skill-RM 的表现持续优于传统的裁判模型（Judge baselines），证明了其在动态证据编排方面的卓越能力。

Conclusion: Skill-RM 提出了一种将奖励建模视为“可重用技能执行”的范式，通过动态证据编排实现了统一、透明且高效的奖励评估。该研究证明了结构化代理任务在提升奖励模型性能方面的有效性，为复杂 LLM 对齐任务提供了强有力的评估工具。

Abstract: Reward models (RMs) provide critical feedback signals for LLM post-training, notably in reinforced fine-tuning (RFT) and reinforcement learning (RL) pipelines. However, current reward evaluation relies on heterogeneous criteria such as rule-based verifiers, ground-truth references, procedural checklists, and complex rubrics, where a unified mechanism to integrate all types of evidence remains unexplored. To this end, we propose Skill Reward Model (Skill-RM), a unified framework that reformulates reward modeling as the execution of a reusable Reward-Evaluation Skill. By treating reward computation as a structured agentic task, Skill-RM provides a consistent interface to orchestrate heterogeneous resources, dynamically selecting and aggregating evidence tailored to the specific requirements of each input. This approach enables the reward model to move beyond static evaluation, ensuring consistency and transparency across diverse tasks. Extensive experiments on reward benchmarks and downstream applications, including best-of-N selection and reinforcement learning, demonstrate that Skill-RM consistently outperforms traditional judge baselines. Our findings suggest that Skill-RM not only provides a unified solution for reward modeling but also achieves superior performance through the strategic and dynamic orchestration of evidence. The code is at https://github.com/Qwen-Applications/Skill-RM.

</details>


### [183] [A Close Look At World Model Recovery In Supervised Fine-Tuned LLM Planners](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03685)
*Patrick Emami,Nan Qiang,Peter Graf*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了大型语言模型在经过经典规划任务的监督微调后，是否真正习得了底层规划问题的世界模型，实验证明模型不仅学会了生成动作，还在线性表征层面内化了规划问题的逻辑规则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管监督微调（SFT）提升了大语言模型（LLM）在经典规划任务上的端到端性能，但目前尚不清楚模型究竟是“理解”了规划逻辑，还是仅仅在进行模式匹配。研究旨在探究模型是否在内部学习到了规划问题的世界模型（World Model）。

Method: 采用了多维度的可解释性实验方法，通过分析微调后模型的内部表征（Linear probing）和生成能力（探测行动有效性和状态谓词），并对比不同微调数据分布（如随机游走数据）对世界模型恢复效果的影响。

Result: 1. 微调使模型能够线性编码行动的有效性及部分状态谓词；2. 即使模型在生成阶段难以准确判断行动有效性，其内部表征层仍能区分有效与无效行动；3. 在微调过程中引入更广泛的状态空间覆盖（如随机游走数据）能显著提高对底层世界模型的恢复精度。

Conclusion: 本研究为评估规划类大语言模型的内在知识表示提供了一套方法论框架，并证实了监督微调确实能让模型习得规划问题的部分领域模型（World Model）特征，为理解大语言模型在符号推理任务中的表现提供了深刻见解。

Abstract: Supervised fine-tuning (SFT) improves end-to-end classical planning in large language models (LLMs), but do these models also learn to represent and reason about the planning problems they are solving? Due to the relative complexity of classical planning problems and the challenge that end-to-end plan generation poses for LLMs, it has been difficult to explore this question. In our work, we devise and perform a series of interpretability experiments that holistically interrogate world model recovery by examining both internal representations and generative capabilities of fine-tuned LLMs. We find that: a) Supervised fine-tuning on valid action sequences enables LLMs to linearly encode action validity and some state predicates. b) Models that struggle to use output probabilities for classifying action validity may still learn internal representations that separate valid from invalid actions. c) Broader state space coverage during fine-tuning, such as from random walk data, yields more accurate recovery of the underlying world model. In summary, this work contributes a recipe for applying interpretability techniques to planning LLMs and generates insights that shed light on open questions about how knowledge is represented in LLMs.

### [184] [Neuron Populations Exhibit Divergent Selectivity with Scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03990)
*Amil Dravid,Yasaman Bahri,Alexei A. Efros,Yossi Gandelsman*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文通过研究神经网络中跨模型共享的“Rosetta神经元”，揭示了神经网络在微观层面的缩放定律：随模型规模增大，这些核心神经元呈现出次线性增长、选择性增强及专业化分工的演化规律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在探讨神经网络中的神经元群体是否随模型规模的扩大而呈现出可预测的演化规律，从而将缩放定律（Scaling Laws）的研究范围从宏观的损失函数扩展到神经元层级的微观可解释性特征上。

Method: 作者通过对高达30B参数的语言模型和5B参数的视觉模型进行独立分析，研究了“Rosetta神经元”（在不同模型中激活模式相似的神经元）。研究构建了一个解析模型，平衡了特征效用与有限神经元容量之间的关系，以解释观察到的缩放规律。此外，还通过针对性的数据过滤案例研究验证了神经元的选择性。

Result: 1. Rosetta神经元数量随模型规模增长遵循次线性幂律（Sublinear Power Law），即其在总神经元中所占比例随模型增大而缩小；2. 观察到“神经元极化效应”（Neuron Polarization Effect），即Rosetta神经元随规模扩大变得更加具有选择性和单义性；3. Rosetta神经元随规模扩大表现出更强的领域专业化特性。

Conclusion: 研究表明，神经网络中存在可解释的、共享的神经元层级结构，其演化规律随模型规模扩展呈现出系统性的变化。这种神经元层级的缩放定律连接了模型规模与神经元的普适性、选择性和专业化程度。

Abstract: We investigate whether neuron populations within neural networks evolve predictably with scale, extending scaling laws beyond macroscopic observables such as loss. To probe this question, we study Rosetta Neurons, a previously characterized class of neurons whose activation patterns are similar across independently trained models (Dravid et al., 2023). In separate analyses of language models up to 30B parameters and vision models up to 5B parameters, we observe that the population of Rosetta Neurons follows a sublinear power law in model size, growing in absolute number but occupying a shrinking fraction of the total neuron count. We further observe a Neuron Polarization Effect: Rosetta Neurons become more selective and increasingly monosemantic with scale, separating from a growing non-Rosetta population that remains less selective. An analytical model balancing feature utility against limited neuron capacity explains the sublinear power-law scaling and this polarization effect. Finally, we find that Rosetta Neurons become more domain-specialized with scale and illustrate their selectivity through a targeted data-filtering case study for continued pretraining. Our results point to a scaling law for interpretable, shared neuron-level structure, linking model size to systematic changes in neuron universality, selectivity, and specialization.

### [185] [Constitutional On-Policy Safe Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03089)
*Ming Wen,Yuxuan Liu,Kun Yang,Yunhao Feng,Zhuoer Xu,Yuhao Sun,Shiwen Cui,Xiang Zheng,Xingjun Ma,Yu-Gang Jiang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对在线策略自蒸馏在安全对齐中导致的模型坍塌和推理能力下降问题，本文提出了COPSD方法，通过预先校准教师模型，成功在增强安全性的同时保留了模型的表达能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线策略自蒸馏（OPSD）在安全对齐任务中存在严重的模型坍塌现象，即宪法约束迫使教师模型偏向短促、过度保守的回答，且反向KL散度进一步加剧了这种表达能力的衰退。研究旨在解决这一因安全压力导致的推理能力受损问题。

Method: 提出了“宪法在线策略安全蒸馏”（COPSD）方法：首先通过交叉监督微调（Cross-SFT）对教师模型进行冷启动校准，以解决因宪法约束导致的分布偏移，随后进行基于宪法条件的在线策略蒸馏，并通过几何视角分析了安全边界压力对模型表达能力的负面影响。

Result: 在12个基准测试上的实验结果显示，COPSD在安全性和有用性之间取得了更优的平衡，且显著降低了进行安全对齐对模型通用推理能力产生的代价（安全税）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过交叉监督微调（Cross-SFT）对教师模型进行校准，可以有效缓解安全合规训练中的模型坍塌问题，COPSD方法成功在保持模型安全性的同时，最大限度地减少了对模型通用推理能力的负面影响（即“安全税”）。

Abstract: On-policy self-distillation (OPSD) has emerged as an efficient post-training paradigm by using a teacher conditioned on privileged information to provide dense token-level supervision. Prior work has shown that OPSD can collapse in verifiable reasoning tasks, but safety alignment differs in that it is guided by high-level constitutions rather than explicit target answers, making it a natural setting to revisit dense distillation. However, our pilot study show that safety OPSD still suffers from severe collapse: constitutional conditioning contracts the teacher distribution toward short and overly conservative responses, and Reverse KL further amplifies this contraction into reduced expressiveness. We formalize this effect as geometric leakage under safety boundaries in a non-orthogonal semantic space, where safety pressure transfers into the expressiveness dimension. Based on this analysis, we propose Constitutional On-Policy Safe Distillation (COPSD), which first calibrates the teacher through a Cross-SFT cold-start and then performs constitution-conditioned on-policy distillation. Experiments on 12 benchmarks show that COPSD achieves a consistently stronger safety--helpfulness trade-off than baselines while substantially reducing the safety tax on general reasoning ability.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在标准生存分析基准数据集上的实验结果表明，该方法在性能上与多种需要训练的参数及半参数生存回归模型（如Cox回归和参数化AFT模型）具有高度竞争力。

Abstract: Survival Analysis (SA) is a statistical framework that models the time span until some event of interest occurs. Widely used in several domains, including healthcare and churn prediction, a central challenge in its applicability stems from the time of the event being partially observed or \emph{right-censoring}.
  Tabular Foundation Models (TFM) have attracted significant interest in recent years due to their ability to perform prediction tasks in a single forward pass, requiring no dataset-specific parameter fitting. Despite their success, their application to prediction tasks on time-to-event data remains difficult due to right censoring. In this work, we present a training-free method to survival regression by leveraging TFMs to both predict the time of the event and iteratively impute right-censored data.
  Our method uses a TFM to construct an Accelerated Failure Time (AFT) model requiring no training beyond fitting a single scalar parameter. Subsequently, by building on the Buckley-James estimator, we introduce a non-parametric in-context estimator for right-censored data. Our experiments on standard survival analysis benchmarks show that our method is competitive with several parametric and semi-parametric survival regression models that require training, including Cox regression and parametric AFT models.

### [187] [Multi$^2$: Hierarchical Multi-Agent Decision-Making with LLM-Based Agents in Interactive Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03698)
*Sangeun Park,Minhae Kwon*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为 Multi$^2$ 的分层多智能体框架，通过将高层目标规划与底层动作执行解耦，有效缓解了大语言模型在长期决策任务中常见的“目标偏移”问题，并配套开源了相关基准数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前大语言模型智能体在处理长周期（long-horizon）决策任务时存在脆弱性，特别是在持续交互过程中极易发生“目标偏移”（objective drift），导致规划失效。为了实现更稳定、可规划的智能体，需要解决长期交互中的目标稳定性与执行一致性问题。

Method: 提出了一种分层多智能体框架 Multi$^2$：高层智能体（System 1）利用监督微调（SFT）进行上下文感知的子目标生成；底层智能体（System 2）通过从离线到在线的强化学习（RL）执行原子动作。通过角色解耦实现决策任务的拆解与稳定控制。

Result: Multi$^2$ 在多种交互式环境中均优于现有的强基准模型，展现出更强的鲁棒性和协作能力；同时，该研究还构建并开源了三个层次化的基准数据集，填补了该领域在训练和评估方面的空白。

Conclusion: Multi$^2$ 框架通过分层协作有效解决了大语言模型智能体在长期决策中面临的目标偏移难题，不仅提升了系统执行长周期任务的鲁棒性和适应性，还通过发布新的基准数据集为 hierarchical 智能体领域的研究提供了重要的评估工具。

Abstract: A central goal of large language model (LLM) research is to build agentic systems that can plan, act, and adapt through sustained interaction with dynamic environments. While recent LLM-based agents exhibit impressive contextual reasoning, their long-horizon decision-making remains fragile, often suffering from objective drift, where goals and plans drift over extended interactions. We introduce Multi$^2$, a hierarchical multi-agent decision-making framework that explicitly decomposes agent behavior into complementary roles. A high-level agent (System 1) focuses on context-aware sub-goal generation using supervised fine-tuning (SFT), while a low-level agent (System 2) executes atomic actions through offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) in interactive environments. This separation enables stable long-horizon control, mitigates objective drift, and allows efficient adaptation. Across diverse interactive environments, Multi$^2$ consistently outperforms strong agentic baselines, demonstrating improved robustness and coordination in multi-turn interaction. Beyond performance, we introduce and release three hierarchical benchmark datasets, filling a long-standing gap in training and evaluating hierarchical decision-making for LLM-based agents.

### [188] [When Graph Tokens Sink: A Mechanistic Analysis of Graph Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03712)
*Ding Zhang,Runtao Zhou,Wenqing Zheng,Rizal Fathony,Bayan Bruss,Chirag Agarwal*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了图语言模型（GLM）内部对图token的处理机制，发现GLM中出现的显著“sink token”并不等同于有效的图信息载体，揭示了当前GLM在图语义表示和信息对齐方面的结构性局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管图语言模型（GLM）在将大语言模型（LLM）应用于图学习任务方面表现出潜力，但目前尚不清楚LLM如何内部解释这些图token，以及这些token是否真正有效地承载了图结构信息。作者旨在揭示GLM内部处理图信息的机制及其局限性。

Method: 作者通过分析代表性GLM架构，深入探究了LLM处理图token的行为。主要手段包括：检测激活层面的异常值（即图sink token），并通过剪枝（pruning）、重定位（repositioning）和交换（swapping）等干预实验，评估这些token对下游预测任务的实际语义和结构贡献。

Result: 研究发现，GLM中存在“图sink token”，表现为在少量隐藏状态维度上具有极高的激活值，且倾向于出现在早期位置。然而，这些显著的激活并不代表其承载了重要的图信息。实验证明，这些sink token并非预测任务中最重要的语义或结构载体，其激活显著性与图信息的实际利用率之间存在明显脱节。

Conclusion: 现有的图语言模型（GLM）在将图结构转化为LLM token空间时存在局限性，其图token表示未能形成完全可用的拓扑感知表示。研究揭示了激活层面的显著性与图语义效用之间的脱节，这表明当前图token的构造、放置及对齐机制需要进一步改进。

Abstract: Graph Language Models (GLMs) have become a promising direction for adapting Large Language Models (LLMs) to graph learning tasks. By transforming graph topology and node information into graph tokens, GLMs allow LLMs to jointly process structured graph inputs and textual instructions. Yet, it remains unclear how LLMs internally interpret these graph tokens and whether graph tokens act as meaningful carriers of graph structure. In this work, we analyze how LLMs process graph information through graph-token behavior in representative GLM architectures.
  Findings. We find that the internal saliency of graph tokens in GLMs is not equivalent to graph information utilization. Graph sink tokens consistently emerge as activation-level outliers: they can be identified by massive activation values along a small set of hidden-state dimensions and are biased toward early graph-token positions. However, this activation-level saliency does not imply that these tokens are the main carriers of graph information. Unlike classical attention sinks in language and vision-language models, graph sink tokens do not necessarily attract the largest attention weights from query tokens. Through pruning, repositioning, and swapping interventions, we show that graph sink tokens are not the most important semantic or structural tokens for downstream prediction.
  Implications. Together, these results suggest that after current GLMs map graph structure into the LLM token space, the resulting graph-token representations do not naturally form a fully usable topology-aware internal representation; instead, they exhibit a decoupling between activation-level saliency and graph-semantic utility. This decoupling points to limitations in existing graph-token construction, placement, and alignment mechanisms.

### [189] [Compress then Merge: From Multiple LoRAs into One Low-Rank Adapter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03723)
*Zhengbao He,Ruiqi Ding,Zhehao Huang,Ruikai Yang,Tao Li,Xiaolin Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种名为 CtM 的 LoRA 合并算法，通过改变传统“先合并后压缩”的流程为“先压缩后合并”，成功解决了多适配器合并时低秩结构被破坏的问题，在保持参数高效性的同时提升了模型性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的 LoRA 合并方法（如先合并后压缩）通常在全参数空间进行合并，这会破坏原始的低秩结构，导致后续的压缩难以恢复有效的 rank-r 模型，且在多任务部署中导致适配器碎片化，管理复杂。

Method: 提出了“先压缩后合并”（Compress-then-Merge, CtM）框架。该方法在合并前先通过低秩权重计算共享的 r 维子空间，将每个适配器投影到这些共享空间中获取 r×r 的坐标，最后在缩减空间内执行合并，从而在构建阶段就保证了输出结果满足 rank-r 的约束。

Result: 实验结果表明，CtM 方法在多种模型和任务上始终优于现有的单 LoRA 输出基线，并显著缩小了与全参数合并方法之间的性能差距，证明了其在保持低秩结构的同时维持高性能的能力。

Conclusion: CtM 通过先压缩再合并的策略，克服了现有模型合并方法在处理低秩约束时的局限性，提供了一种高效、高质量的多适配器合并方案，为大规模模型适配器的部署提供了更优的路径。

Abstract: Low-rank adaptation (LoRA) enables parameter-efficient specialization of foundation models, but the proliferation of task-specific adapters fragments capabilities across many adapters, complicating reuse and deployment. We study the problem of merging $T$ LoRAs into a single rank-$r$ LoRA, thereby preserving the benefits of low-rank structure. Existing Merge-then-Compress pipelines treat the rank constraint as an afterthought: they merge adapters in the full parameter space, then compress the merged result to rank $r$ via truncated SVD. However, full-parameter merging may destroy the low-rank structure, making it difficult for subsequent compression to recover an effective rank-$r$ LoRA. We propose Compress-then-Merge (CtM), a reversed pipeline that enforces the rank-$r$ bottleneck before merging: CtM computes shared $r$-dimensional subspaces using only the LoRA weights to capture cross-adapter common structure, projects each adapter into the shared subspaces to obtain $r\times r$ coordinates, and then applies standard merging rules in this reduced space. CtM guarantees a rank-$r$ LoRA by construction, avoiding post-hoc truncation, and enables efficient computation in the core space spanned by concatenated LoRA factors. Experiments across multiple models and tasks show that CtM consistently outperforms existing single-LoRA-output baselines while narrowing the performance gap to full-parameter merging methods.

</details>

Abstract: Large Language Models remain plagued by hallucinations. Recent work has sought to tame their prevalence using statistical techniques based on conformal prediction, with both theoretical and empirical success. However, these methods operate in a post-hoc fashion, treating the sampling procedure itself as atomic and then surgically altering samples to remove hallucinated claims. This disconnect between filtering and generation can result in samples that are incoherent, inconsistent, or simply unlikely under the model itself. Moreover, post-hoc surgery is unable to shift probability mass towards more useful and helpful responses. To address these issues, we propose to instead sample from approximations to an LLM posterior, where the conditioning event corresponds to a calibrated, high-scoring region. We develop a calibration procedure tailored to the setting of conditional sequential generation that effectively identifies this region and achieves target risk control. Empirically, we apply our method to case studies focused on open-ended biography generation and mathematical problem solving; compared to prior work, we obtain the same statistical guarantees, with higher downstream utility.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1. 数据层面：提出工具感知轨迹过滤机制，剔除无效工具调用及无法提供判别性学习信号（全对或全错）的轨迹。
2. 算法层面：引入工具感知熵引导奖励（Entropy-guided bonus），在工具调用后的关键决策点重塑优势函数，鼓励模型探索更多样化的推理路径。

Result: 在 7 个具有挑战性的推理基准测试中，跨越 3 种不同模型规模的实验结果表明，TAO-RL 在性能上显著优于现有的基准方法。

Abstract: Agentic reinforcement learning (RL) equips large language models (LLMs) with tool-use capabilities that substantially improve reasoning on complex tasks. However, integrating external tools often destabilizes training: over-reliance on tools can induce input distribution shift, while overly conservative tool use limits effective exploration. To address this issue, we propose a unified framework TAO-RL that couples tool-aware trajectory filtering with entropy-guided exploration for efficient policy optimization. Specifically, at the data level, TAO-RL filters rollout trajectories along two criteria: discarding those where all tool invocations fail to execute, and removing those where all rollouts are either correct or incorrect, as both cases yield degenerate advantage estimates that contribute no discriminative learning signal. This joint filtering retains data that are both tool-capable and informative, establishing a high-quality training distribution. At the algorithmic level, we introduce a tool-aware entropy-guided bonus that reshapes the advantage function at post-tool-call tokens, encouraging the policy to explore more diverse reasoning paths at critical decision points. These two components are mutually reinforcing: trajectory filtering establishes a clean and informative training foundation, while entropy-guided exploration drives stronger reasoning behaviors at critical tool-interaction junctures. Extensive experiments on 7 challenging reasoning benchmarks across 3 model scales demonstrate the superiority of TAO-RL over existing methods.

Safe exploration is a key challenge in Reinforcement Learning (RL) that aims to prevent agents from making harmful decisions while exploring their environment. Shielding is one such technique that assumes domain knowledge in the form of an environment model to decide upon action safety. Although well-established, shielding has seen limited adoption in RL due to the lack of accessible end-to-end infrastructure connecting formal shield synthesis with standard RL frameworks. ### [196] [PURGE: Projected Unlearning via Retain-Guided Erasure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03808)
*Vedant Jawandhia,Daksh Ahuja,Ghufran Alam Siddiqui,Prashant Trivedi,Yash Sinha,Pratik Narang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: PURGE是一种基于持续学习与机器遗忘对偶性的机器遗忘算法，通过梯度投影约束、多层表征擦除及保留混淆目标，实现了高隐私保护且性能损失极小的遗忘效果，并具备自动化停止机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的机器遗忘方法在保护隐私（如抵御成员推理攻击）与维持保留集模型性能之间往往难以取得平衡。作者观察到持续学习（CL）与机器遗忘（MU）在本质上是互为对偶的问题，旨在利用这一特性开发一种高效的遗忘算法。

Method: 1. 利用持续学习中的梯度投影技术（源自A-GEM），确保遗忘步骤不会增加保留集的损失；2. 执行多层表征擦除，将遗忘集的中间层激活值推向保留集的分布；3. 采用“保留混淆目标”（Retain-confusion target）而非均匀分布，模拟模型在保留数据上的自然混淆模式以增强隐私；4. 引入自调节停止准则（保留损失预算和遗忘准确率目标），实现自动化控制。

Result: 在5个数据集（CIFAR-10, MNIST, SVHN, STL10, PathMNIST）及22项任务中，PURGE将保留集准确率稳定保持在96%以上，并将成员推理攻击（MIA）的AUROC降至0.5（理想状态），其隐私-效用边界表现优于梯度上升（Gradient Ascent）和KL-散度一致性（KL-uniform）等基线模型。

Conclusion: PURGE 通过利用持续学习与机器遗忘的对偶性，成功实现了高效且具有隐私保障的机器遗忘。该算法不仅能保护保留集性能，还能通过精细的表征擦除和保留混淆目标，有效抵御成员推理攻击，在多个数据集上表现优于现有主流方法。

Abstract: We propose PURGE, a machine unlearning algorithm built on a simple but an under-exploited observation: continual learning (CL) and machine unlearning (MU) which are fundamentally dual problems. CL tries to learn new tasks without forgetting old ones; MU tries to erase specific data without hurting retained performance representing the same underlying tension in opposite directions. PURGE leverages this duality by adapting gradient projection from A-GEM (Chaudhry et al., 2019) so that every unlearning step is constrained to not increase the retain-set loss. On top of this, it performs multi-layer representation erasure, pushing forget-set activations in intermediate layers towards the retain distribution to remove information from hidden representations rather than just suppressing it at the output. A key design choice is the retain-confusion target: rather than pushing forget outputs toward the uniform distribution, which we found to be surprisingly easy for membership inference attacks to detect, we instead target the model's natural confusion pattern on retain data. This makes the unlearned model hard to distinguish from one retrained from scratch. Two self-regulating stopping criteria (a retain-loss budget and a forget-accuracy target) let the algorithm decide on its own when to stop, removing the need for manual epoch tuning. In experiments on five datasets (CIFAR-10, MNIST, SVHN, STL10, PathMNIST) across 22 class-level forgetting tasks, PURGE consistently keeps retain accuracy above 96% while achieving MIA AUROC close to 0.5 (the ideal), outperforming gradient ascent, KL-uniform, and several published baselines on the privacy-utility frontier.

</details>


### [197] [TreeFlash: Parallel AR-Approximation for Faster Speculative Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03819)
*Peer Rheinboldt,Frédéric Berdoz,Roger Wattenhofer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: TreeFlash 提出了一种新的单步草稿生成方法，通过引入 MLP 层近似自回归分布，解决了现有模型因缺乏自回归依赖导致的分布偏差问题，显著提升了推测解码的效率和速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统“一次性”草稿模型（one-shot block drafters）因采用非自回归生成方式，在生成长草稿时，其分布会偏离验证器的自回归分布，导致接受率下降及效率受限，特别是在树形草稿中更为严重。

Method: 引入一个结合草稿模型隐藏状态与前一个 token 的 MLP 层来近似自回归分布；采用两阶段近似机制，在保持 O(1) 推理时间复杂度的情况下，提升了草稿生成的准确性。

Result: 在多种任务和模型上达到行业领先水平，与现有的边际树形草稿（marginal tree drafting）相比，块效率（block efficiency）提升了 12%，推理速度提升了 9%。

Conclusion: TreeFlash 通过两阶段近似机制，在保持单次前向传播的高效性的同时，显著缓解了非自回归草稿模型与验证器分布不匹配的问题，为加速推理提供了更高效的草稿生成方案。

Abstract: One-shot block drafters for speculative decoding generate the full draft in a single forward pass, achieving strong throughput by eliminating sequential token generation. However, they predict each draft token conditioned only on the prefix context, with no dependence on previously drafted tokens. This non-autoregressive conditioning causes the drafter's distribution to diverge from the verifier's true autoregressive distribution as draft depth grows. This problem becomes more severe in tree-based drafting, where distinct branches are forced to share the same marginal distribution for subsequent tokens. We propose TreeFlash, which addresses this by incorporating an MLP layer conditioned on the drafter's hidden state and the previous token to approximate an autoregressive distribution. TreeFlash retains the $\mathcal{O}(1)$ decoding time complexity of one-shot drafters by employing a two-stage approximation mechanism. TreeFlash achieves state-of-the-art performance across a variety of tasks and models, improving over marginal tree drafting by $12\%$ higher block efficiency and $9\%$ higher speedup.

</details>


### [198] [Finding Needles in the Haystack: Transductive Active Labeling in Ecology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03821)
*Rupa Kurinchi-Vendhan,Sara Beery*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对生态数据主动学习中因评估方式偏差导致长尾类别（稀有物种）发现不足的问题，该论文提出了一种基于生态稀疏曲线的混合停止准则，强调了从“预测”向“发现”的范式转换，有效提升了长尾数据的标注效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前主动学习在生态学领域多采用归纳式评估（基于测试集），这与生态学研究中需要对整个数据集进行转导式标注（transductive labeling）的目标不匹配；此外，现有的评估方式忽略了“人在回路”中对长尾类别（如稀有物种）的发现需求，导致标注过程往往过早停止。

Method: 1. 提出了一种衡量长尾类别“采样难度”的新度量标准，量化了稀有样本在密集样本空间中的分布情况；2. 基于生态学中的稀疏曲线（rarefaction curves），构建了一种保守的混合停止准则；3. 通过实验对比，验证了将预测性能与发现标准相结合在处理长尾数据时的优越性。

Result: 实验结果表明，在处理生态数据时，转导式学习目标的重心应从单纯的分类性能转向对稀有样本的“发现”。所提出的混合停止准则有效地减少了对长尾类别的过早停止标注，显著提高了稀有类别的召回率，验证了在发现任务受限时该方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该研究强调了生态学任务中“发现”比单纯的“预测”更为关键。通过引入基于生态稀疏曲线的停止准则，研究者成功解决了主动学习中对长尾类别（稀有物种）过早停止标记的问题，为生态数据的高效标注提供了更符合实际需求的评估与决策框架。

Abstract: Active learning is now standard practice in labeling ecological data, enabling ecologists to quickly process large volumes of field data to understand and monitor natural environments. Current practices evaluate active learning inductively, estimating predictive performance on a held-out test set. We argue that this evaluation is misaligned with most ecological tasks, where the goal is to transductively label an entire pool of data as efficiently as possible. We demonstrate that ignoring the human-in-the-loop underestimates the importance of continuing to label, particularly for classes in the long tail which may be of disproportionate ecological importance (rare species, uncommon behaviors, etc.). Our analysis shows that, for this long tail, the transductive objective shifts importance from prediction to discovery: the true challenge becomes finding "needles in the haystack," examples of rare classes that are embedded within dense regions of abundant classes in the latent geometry, which we quantify with a novel metric of sampling difficulty. Finally, to translate these insights to practical ecological workflows, we propose a conservative hybrid stopping criterion inspired by ecological rarefaction curves, and show that combining predictive performance with discovery criteria reduces premature stopping on long-tailed pools, improving rare-class recovery when discovery, not classification, is the limiting factor.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统在线学习算法主要关注全局遗憾，但在处理非平稳环境时，对任意时间间隔内的性能（区间遗憾）表现不足。现有算法难以同时实现对梯度变化（gradient variation）的优化、对问题相关参数的自适应，以及处理超参数调节的困难。

Method: 采用一种简单的两层在线集成结构（two-layer online ensemble structure），并引入了一种新颖的Lipschitz自适应元算法，使得算法无需预先知道Lipschitz常数和平滑度参数即可实现自适应调节。

Result: 该算法实现了与梯度变化成比例的区间遗憾界，在最坏情况下保持极小极大最优性；在区间动态遗憾和随机扩展对抗优化方面也取得了显著的理论突破，并通过实验验证了其有效性。

Abstract: This paper investigates non-stationary online learning using the metric of interval regret, which requires an online algorithm to perform well over every time interval. We propose the first online learning algorithm that achieves an interval regret bound scaling with gradient variation, a fundamental measure of the cumulative change in online function gradients, which relates to various problem-dependent quantities and is closely connected to stochastic optimization and other problems. Our method employs a simple and efficient two-layer online ensemble structure that achieves strong theoretical guarantees. Specifically, it enjoys a regret bound that simultaneously adapts to various problem-dependent quantities while also preserving the minimax-optimal rate in the worst case. Moreover, recognizing the challenge of hyperparameter tuning, we introduce a Lipschitz- and smoothness-agnostic variant that automatically adapts to these potentially unknown constants. This is primarily enabled by a novel Lipschitz-adaptive meta algorithm, which may be of independent interest. Beyond interval regret, our method also yields broader implications: it provides versatile bounds for interval dynamic regret, a stronger measure that competes with changing comparators over any interval, and yields the first piecewise characterization for stochastic extended adversarial optimization. Theoretical findings are validated by experiments.

### [200] [Text-attributed Graph Condensation via Text Selection and Attribute Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.03839)

  <summary>Details</summary>
